# Wiki Index

The catalog of all pages in this wiki. Each entry: a wikilink to the page and a one-line summary. The LLM reads this first when answering queries to identify candidate pages.

Keep summaries tight — one line each. The index is engineered to be cheap to read; a fat index defeats its purpose.

When this file exceeds ~300 lines or the wiki passes ~150 pages, shard into `wiki/indexes/<type>.md` and replace this file with a directory of shards. See the `scaling-playbook.md` reference in the `llm-wiki` skill for the migration procedure.

---

## Sources

- [[readme]] — the project's front-page `README.md`: what Seqeron is, its three entry points, and headline facts.
- [[algorithms-checklist-v2]] — the test-unit validation registry: 364 units (255 done / 109 proposed), DoD, evidence, coverage.
- [[advanced-testing-checklist]] — 2026-03-19 effectiveness/gap analysis rating the ten testing techniques by applicability, coverage, effort, and P0–P3 priority.
- [[mcp-methods-audit]] — a 2026-01-23 census of the C# API surface: 277 public static methods across 54 classes, with counting rules and the tool-count caveat.
- [[mcp-checklist]] — the SUPERSEDED (2026-07-01) MCP build tracker: a 12-server/241-tool plan never built; DoD gates, error-code catalog, two-tests-per-tool. Live status now in `docs/mcp/MCP_STATUS.md`.
- [[mcp-plan]] — the SUPERSEDED (2026-07-01) MCP design doc (sibling of the checklist): v3→v4 rationale, full 241-tool inventory across 12 servers, and the still-valid standards (naming, JSON-Schema 2020-12, error ranges, SemVer, 2-tests-per-tool, doc contract).
- [[mcp-prompt]] — the CURRENT one-tool-per-session MCP-completion subagent prompt: names the real 11 servers (server→project→file), the 3-part tool DoD (binding+tests+docs), and reverses the old no-business-asserts test policy. Ground truth: `docs/mcp/MCP_STATUS.md`.
- [[sonar-gate-plan]] — the Sonar-ratchet tracker: 66/66 SonarAnalyzer rules moved from report-only to blocking (or silenced-with-justification); Groups A–E, notable behaviour changes, and review-not-blind-fix on the S1244/S125 giants.
- [[align-global-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ALIGN-GLOBAL-001 (Needleman–Wunsch): Wikipedia sources, the `GCATGCG`/`GATTACA` worked example, and the GapExtend-as-*d* / GapOpen-unused note.
- [[align-multi-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ALIGN-MULTI-001 (MSA): main doc + MUSCLE and T-Coffee addenda; star/iterative/consistency aligners, SP-score and consensus design choices.
- [[align-semi-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ALIGN-SEMI-001 (semi-global / fitting): Wikipedia + Rosalind SIMS/SMGB + Brudno 2003 sources, fitting-variant init/traceback, INV-1..5.
- [[align-stats-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ALIGN-STATS-001 (identity/similarity/gaps + srspair formatting): EMBOSS needle/AlignFormats + BLAST + pseqsid sources, denominator-includes-gaps rule, three datasets.
- [[annot-coding-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ANNOT-CODING-001 (CPAT hexamer coding-potential score): CPAT paper + FrameKmer.py + EMBOSS tcode sources, mean-ln-ratio formula, ±1 pseudo-scores, worked example 0.3466.
- [[annot-codonusage-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ANNOT-CODONUSAGE-001 (RSCU): LIRMM + PMC2528880 + Sharp & Li 1986 + CodonU sources, n_i·x/Σx formula, Leu 3/1.5/1.5/0/0/0 example, pooled-counts + sense-codons-only, no CAI pseudocount.
- [[annot-repeat-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ANNOT-REPEAT-001 (repeat detection/classification): Wikipedia + IUPACpal + RepeatMasker sources; tandem/inverted/gapped-IR + repeat-class vocab; exact-substring-not-Smith-Waterman ClassifyRepeat assumption.
- [[assembly-consensus-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-CONSENSUS-001 (column-wise consensus): Biopython dumb_consensus + EMBOSS cons + Wikipedia sources; threshold/tie→ambiguous/gap-skip decision rule; default N-not-X and 0.5-not-0.7 assumptions.
- [[assembly-correct-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-CORRECT-001 (two-sided k-mer-spectrum read error correction): Musket + Quake + solid-k-mer sources; trusted/untrusted rule, ambiguity→unchanged, k=3/k=1 worked examples; non-behavioral kmerSize=15/minKmerFrequency=2 defaults.
- [[assembly-cover-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-COVER-001 (per-base coverage/depth): Illumina + Daniel Cook + Metagenomics Wiki + Lander-Waterman sources; depth/average/breadth definitions, ACGTTGCAAT worked example (1.5/1.0), e^−c gap/breadth Poisson check; placement-out-of-scope assumption.
- [[assembly-dbg-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-DBG-001 (de Bruijn graph assembly): Langmead notes + Jones & Pevzner (Euler theorems 8.1/8.2) + Compeau-Pevzner-Tesler 2011 sources; (k-1)-mer node/edge construction, Eulerian-walk spelling rule, AAABBBA/a_long…/to_every…/ATGGCGTGCA oracles; multiple-walk/gap/error failure modes; walk-selection + empty + short-read assumptions.
- [[assembly-merge-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-MERGE-001 (contig merging / suffix–prefix overlap collapse): Langmead SCS + OLC + MIT 7.91J sources; overlap = suffix-of-X/prefix-of-Y, `MergeContigs` collapse arithmetic |m|=|c1|+|c2|−l, BAAB/AAABBBA/plain-concat oracles; trusted-length + out-of-range→concatenate API-contract assumptions.
- [[assembly-olc-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-OLC-001 (Overlap-Layout-Consensus): Compeau/Pevzner/Tesler 2011 + Langmead OLC/SCS sources; overlap graph + Hamiltonian-path (NP-complete) layout + majority consensus; GTACGTACGAT 12-edge / 5-overlap-tiling / CTCTAGGCC oracles; identity-1.0 + empty-input assumptions.
- [[assembly-scaffold-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-SCAFFOLD-001 (scaffolding): ABySS 2.0 + NCBI AGP v2.1 + Sahlin 2012 + Bambus sources; scaffold = ordered contigs interspersed with `N`-runs = distance estimate, non-positive gap → AGP unknown-size default 100 N; ACGTNNNTTGGNNCCAA / AAAA+100N+TTTT oracles; source-backed-100-constant scoping assumption.
- [[assembly-stats-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-STATS-001 (assembly statistics N50/L50/Nx/auN): Miller 2010 + Wikipedia + QUAST `N50.py` + Heng Li 2020 sources; largest-first inclusive-≥ threshold, auN=ΣL²/ΣL; Assembly A {80,70,50,40,30,20}→N50 70/L50 2, Assembly B→N50 50/L50 3, auN 73.333 oracles; empty→zeros + upper-median-not-source-derived assumptions.
- [[assembly-trim-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ASSEMBLY-TRIM-001 (quality trimming, BWA/cutadapt running-sum): cutadapt algorithm docs + BWA `bwa_trim_read`/`BWA_MIN_RDLEN` + Cock et al. 2010 sources; subtract-cutoff/argmin-partial-sum = BWA argmax, Phred+33 decode; `KI;<)(,%#$`@thr 10→first 4 bases oracle; both-end-order + minLength-filter assumptions.
- [[chrom-aneu-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CHROM-ANEU-001 (aneuploidy detection): first Chromosome-analysis file; Wikipedia Aneuploidy/CNV + Griffiths + Santaguida-Amon + McCarroll-Altshuler sources; log2 depth-ratio → CN=round(2^logRatio×2) clamped [0,10], ≥80%-bin whole-chromosome call, confidence=1−min(1,|CN/2−2^logRatio|); Down/Edwards/Patau/Turner/Klinefelter oracles; sex-chromosome + partial-aneuploidy limitations.
- [[chrom-karyo-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CHROM-KARYO-001 (karyotype analysis): third Chromosome-analysis file; Wikipedia Karyotype/Ploidy/Aneuploidy sources; `AnalyzeKaryotype` (descriptor counts → cytogenetic nomenclature, TotalChromosomes/GenomeSize/MeanLength invariants) + `DetectPloidy` (median-depth ratio → round(ratio×2) clamped [1,8], confidence 1−|ratio×2−ploidy|×2); Down/Turner + diploid/tetraploid/haploid oracles; DD1–DD5 (nullisomy-unreachable, disomy-only-in-polyploid); deviations None.
- [[chrom-synt-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CHROM-SYNT-001 (synteny analysis): fourth Chromosome-analysis file; Wikipedia Synteny/Comparative-genomics/Rearrangement + MCScanX/SyRI/MUMmer sources; `FindSyntenyBlocks` (ortholog pairs grouped by chr pair → collinear runs merged under maxGap, ≥minGenes; I1–I5 incl. SequenceIdentity=NaN per MCScanX) + `DetectRearrangements` (adjacent-block signals → Translocation/Inversion/Deletion/Duplication); forward/inverted-block + translocation/inversion oracles; §7 coverage-strengthen (M16 maxGap gap closed); deviations None.
- [[chrom-telo-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CHROM-TELO-001 (telomere analysis): fifth Chromosome-analysis file; Wikipedia Telomere + Meyne 1989 (TTAGGG conserved) + Cawthon 2002 (T/S ratio) + Blackburn-Gall 1978 sources; 3′ TTAGGG / 5′ CCCTAA end detection, 70%-per-window purity (5/6 or 5/7 match), T/S linearity length=refLen×(tsRatio/refRatio), IsCriticallyShort=(hasTelomere&&len<criticalLen)OR empty; 1200-bp/purity-0.833/12000/searchLen-truncation + T/S oracles; criticalLength/minTelomereLength/searchLength/referenceLength are configurable defaults not biological constants; deviations None.
- [[chrom-cent-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CHROM-CENT-001 (centromere analysis): second Chromosome-analysis file; layered multi-session record; Wikipedia + Levan 1964 + Hartley/McNulty/Masumoto/Rosandić/Alkan/Shepelev + Dfam/T2T (CC0) sources; Levan q/p arm-ratio classes (1.7/3.0/7.0 boundaries), additive alpha-satellite/CENP-B/HOR/SF detectors (171-bp monomer, 17-bp box, <5% inter-HOR); AlphaSatelliteContent-is-density + SF1/SF2-unresolved limitations.
- [[codon-cai-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CODON-CAI-001 (Codon Adaptation Index): Wikipedia + Sharp & Li 1987 + Jansen 2003 (verbatim single-codon exclusion) + Kazusa sources; geometric-mean-of-w=f/maxf formula, dual include/exclude-Met/Trp mode, E. coli oracles (CUA-CCA-ACA→0.1980); one deviation = 1e-6 zero-freq clamp (not the RSCU page's 0.5 pseudocount).
- [[codon-enc-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CODON-ENC-001 (Effective Number of Codons, ENC/Nc, Wright 1990): Fuglsang 2004/2006 (verbatim Wright equations) + NCBI degeneracy partition sources; codon-homozygosity F̂=(n·Σp²−1)/(n−1), Nc=2+9/F̂₂+1/F̂₃+5/F̂₄+3/F̂₆, unbiased→61 / max-bias→20 / no-bias-sim→40.5 oracles, Ile (F̂₂+F̂₄)/2 fallback; one assumption = non-source lower clamp at 20.
- [[codon-opt-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CODON-OPT-001 (codon optimization / OptimizeSequence): Wikipedia codon-usage-bias + CAI + Plotkin-Kudla 2011 + Mignon 2018 + Kazusa sources; five strategies (MaximizeCAI / BalancedOptimization 40-60% GC / HarmonizeExpression / AvoidRareCodons / MinimizeSecondary), protein-preservation + Met/Trp-fixed + CAI∈(0,1] invariants, E. coli/yeast/human preferred-codon tables; RNA-notation + T→U + trim-to-codon + 1e-6 CAI clamp implementation notes; no source contradictions.
- [[codon-rscu-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CODON-RSCU-001 (RSCU + `CountCodons`): second RSCU unit; Sharp/Tuohy/Mosurski 1986 + LIRMM + GenomicSig + seqinr `uco` + cubar `est_rscu` sources, n_i·x/Σx formula, Leu CTGCTGCTGCTA→4.5/1.5/0 + Phe TTTTTTTTC→4/3,2/3 examples, CountCodons non-overlapping-triplet/non-ACGT-exclusion contract; stop-codons-as-degeneracy-3-family framing (cross-page nuance vs the concept's forward_table exclusion), cubar pseudocount vs repo-returns-0 for absent families.
- [[codon-stats-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CODON-STATS-001 (Codon Usage Statistics, GetStatistics + CalculateCai): the codon-family aggregation/reporting view; bundles RSCU + ENC + CAI + positional GC (GC1/GC2/GC3, GC3s=synonymous-3rd-position GC excluding Met/Trp/stop, Peden 1999) + E. coli/human reference tables; Sharp & Li 1987 + Biopython + Kazusa + CodonW/EMBOSS sources; ATGGCA→GC3s 0/GC3 50 + GCTGCC→CAI √0.122 oracles; deviations = GC3s-as-percentage + skip-zero-w (not 0.01 floor); reuses existing codon concepts, no new concept.
- [[codon-usage-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CODON-USAGE-001 (raw codon usage table + TVD comparison, CalculateCodonUsage + CompareCodonUsage): Wikipedia codon-usage-bias + Kazusa + Sharp & Li 1987 sources; unnormalized Dictionary<codon,int> counts (T→U, drop partial codon), Similarity=1−Σ|f₁−f₂|/2 TVD in [0,1] with proven identity/symmetry/range/disjoint→0 properties, AUGGCUGCU→{AUG:1,GCU:2} + sim oracles (2/3, 0.5, 0.75, 0.25, disjoint→0); TVD-not-cosine + empty→0 deviations; new codon-usage-comparison concept, reuses RSCU counting.
- [[codon-rare-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit CODON-RARE-001 (rare codon detection, FindRareCodons + %MinMax/Sherlocc cluster addendum): Wikipedia + GenScript GenRCA (Fan 2024) + Kazusa + Shu 2006 (5×CUA ~3-fold inhibition) + Sharp & Li 1987 sources; freq<threshold (default 0.15) per-family rule, E. coli AGA/AGG/CGA/CUA rare set; Clarke&Clark 2008 %MinMax 18-codon window (%Min/%Max signed, ±100%) + Chartier 2012 Sherlocc 7-codon ≥4-slow cluster rule; Arg-family %MinMax oracles (−86.36/+100/+36.47) + Sherlocc 7×AGA/4+3/3+4 oracles; single-codon-AA no-NaN + overlapping-window-merge corner cases; no contradictions.
- [[compgen-ani-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-ANI-001 (Average Nucleotide Identity, ANIb; first Comparative-genomics file): Goris 2007 + Konstantinidis & Tiedje 2005 + pyani sources; 1020 nt query fragmentation, best-match placement, >30% identity / ≥70% alignable cut-offs recalculated over query-fragment length, mean of qualifying fragments; ANI≈95%↔70% DDH species boundary; gapped Smith-Waterman recovers indels (AAAACCCC/AAAATCCCC 0.875→1.0), reciprocal ANI = mean of both directions; exact-arithmetic oracles (1.0/0.9375/0.875, cut-off/short→exclude→0); engine decision = LocalAlign not NCBI-BLASTN; deviations None.
- [[compgen-cluster-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-CLUSTER-001 (Conserved Gene Clusters / common intervals of permutations; Comparative-genomics): Uno & Yagiura 2000 + Heber & Stoye 2001 + Bui-Xuan/Habib/Paul 2013 + Didier et al. 2013 sources; cluster = gene-label set contiguous in EVERY genome (order/strand-free), size ≥2, whole set trivial, K≥2; golden vector Id₇ vs (7 2 1 3 6 4 5) → {1,2}{1,2,3}{3,4,5,6}{4,5}{4,5,6}{1..6} + trivial {1..7}, split-negative {2,3}, sequence-with-duplicates {1,2,3,4}; strict gap-free model (maxGap inert, API back-compat only; gene-teams not implemented); deviations None.
- [[compgen-dotplot-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-DOTPLOT-001 (Dot Plot Generation, word-match / k-tuple dot matrix; Comparative-genomics): Gibbs & McIntyre 1970 + EMBOSS `dottup` + Wikipedia + Huttley sources; dot at (x,y) iff length-`wordSize` word at x in seq1 exactly matches word at y in seq2 (case-insensitive, x=seq1/y=seq2, all overlapping occurrences), `wordSize` (default 10) noise/sensitivity trade-off, `stepSize` x-subsampling; AGCGT/AT k=1→{(0,0),(4,1)}, ACGTACGT self wordSize4→7-dot overlapping set, ACGT self main-diagonal oracles; word>seq/null/empty/disjoint→no dots, non-positive wordSize/stepSize→ArgumentOutOfRangeException; orientation + case-insensitivity assumptions, deviations None.
- [[compgen-ortho-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-ORTHO-001 (ortholog detection by Reciprocal Best Hits + in-paralog within-genome best hits; Comparative-genomics): Fitch 1970 (orthology=speciation / paralogy=duplication) + Tatusov 1997 (COG symmetrical best hits) + Moreno-Hagelsieb 2008 (operational RBH, best hit=max similarity, ≥50% coverage, E≤1e-6) + Remm 2001 (InParanoid RBH seed + in-paralog rule) sources; RBH reciprocity guard (one-directional best hit is NOT an ortholog), within-genome mutual best hits = recent paralogs; reciprocity/non-reciprocity(RBH count 1)/in-paralog/empty oracles; one assumption = alignment-free 5-mer Jaccard replaces BLAST bit-score ranking; deviations None. Shared anchor for COMPGEN-RBH-001, sub-unit of genome-comparison-core-dispensable.
- [[compgen-compare-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-COMPARE-001 (end-to-end genome comparison `CompareGenomes`; Comparative-genomics orchestrating pipeline): Tettelin 2005 (pan-genome core/dispensable) + Moreno-Hagelsieb 2008/Tatusov 1997 (RBH = shared gene) + fraction-of-syntenic-genes metric + MCScanX (Wang 2012) sources; core=RBH ortholog pairs, dispensable=rest, outputs Conserved/Specific1/Specific2 + OverallSynteny=(genes in blocks)/min(|g1|,|g2|) clamped ≤1; oracles one-shared→1/1/1, disjoint→0/2/2, identical 5-collinear+1→5/1/1 & 0.8333; symmetric partition; empty→all-0; two assumptions (alignment-free RBH gate inherited from COMPGEN-RBH-001, MCScanX ≥5-anchor block threshold → OverallSynteny can be 0 with conserved orthologs); deviations None.
- [[compgen-rearr-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-REARR-001 (genome rearrangement detection by breakpoints, signed gene-order comparison; Comparative-genomics): Hunter Lecture 16 (Hannenhalli–Pevzner/Bafna–Pevzner) + Tannier PMC3887456 + Bafna–Pevzner 1998 sources; signed permutation `α(i)=±a`, extended `(0,…,n+1)`, breakpoint = pair where neither `(x,y)` nor `(−y,−x)` in β, `b(α)` count + `d_BP=n−sim` + reversal lower bound `d≥b/2`; Inversion (sign-flip reversal) vs Transposition (orientation-preserving block move); Hunter `α=(−2,−3,+1,+6,−5,−4)`→b=6, identity→0, single-inversion→2 oracles; three scoping assumptions (orthologMap-supplied anchors, strand=sign, only Inversion/Transposition classified — Translocation/indel/dup "Not implemented"); the signed-permutation alternative to block-signal [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]]; deviations None.
- [[compgen-reversal-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-REVERSAL-001 (Reversal/inversion distance as the breakpoint lower bound ⌈b/2⌉; Comparative-genomics): NOT a new algorithm — the UNSIGNED specialization of [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]'s reversal-distance bound (Bafna–Pevzner 1998 + Hunter Lecture 16 + Hübotter 2020 + Bergeron–Mixtacki–Stoye 2009); `CalculateReversalDistance` counts unsigned breakpoints `|Δ|≠1` on the extended perm and returns `⌈b/2⌉=(b+1)/2`; [2,3,1,6,5,4]→2, [4,3,2,1]→1, identity→0 oracles; lower-bound-not-exact (no HP cycle/hurdle refinement); two assumptions (integer ⌈b/2⌉ rounding, unequal-length→ArgumentException); deviations None.
- [[compgen-synteny-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-SYNTENY-001 (synteny / collinearity block detection, MCScanX DP model; Comparative-genomics): reuses [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] and supplies its concrete scoring parameters — chain DP `Score(v)=max(MatchScore(v), max_u[Score(u)+MatchScore(v)+GapPenalty×NumberofGaps(u,v)])`, MatchScore 50/GapPenalty −1/MAX_GAPS 25, report ≥250 score (≥5 anchor pairs), both transcriptional directions → forward + inverted blocks, anchors from BLASTP E≤1e-5 (generation delegated to COMPGEN-ORTHO-001); forward(250)/reverse-inverted/4-anchor-200-no-block/25-gap-break/empty oracles; two source-backed assumptions (≥250 AND ≥5 pairs report rule, orthologMap-supplied anchors); deviations None.
- [[disorder-lc-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit DISORDER-LC-001 (protein low-complexity, SEG / Wootton & Federhen; first of the protein-disorder family): NCBI `blast_seg.c` + GCG/manpage + Wootton-Federhen sources; W=12/K1=2.2/K2=2.5, Shannon-entropy bits/residue two-stage trigger-extend, QQ../AAAAAALLLLLL/AAABBBCCCDDD/12-distinct H=0/1/2/3.585 oracles; X-rich label + greedy-single-residue-extension assumptions; deviations flagged non-boundary-affecting.
- [[disorder-morf-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit DISORDER-MORF-001 (MoRF / Molecular Recognition Feature prediction, dip-in-disorder; second of the protein-disorder family): Mohan 2006 + Cheng/Oldfield PMC2570644 + Oldfield 2005 + Wikipedia sources; ordered dip (per-residue TOP-IDP disorder score <0.5) of total length 10–70 flanked both sides by disorder = one MoRF, 0.5 threshold, α/β/ι sub-types, score∈[0,1] increases with dip depth; synthetic L-dip-in-P/E-flanks oracle; one assumption = paywalled exact flank-length parameters → qualitative criterion (threshold/band/shape source-traceable); no contradictions.
- [[disorder-pred-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit DISORDER-PRED-001 (intrinsic-disorder prediction, TOP-IDP sliding window `PredictDisorder`; third of the protein-disorder family): Campen 2008 (TOP-IDP Table 2 + cutoff 0.542 max-likelihood, window 21) + Dunker 2001 (disorder/order/ambiguous sets) + Kyte-Doolittle 1982 + Wikipedia sources; Sᵢ=mean of (p−(−0.884))/1.871 normalized TOP-IDP over window, disordered when ≥0.542, all 20 values, W30→0.0/P30→1.0/E30→0.866 oracles, edge-clip + skip-non-canonical (all-unknown→0.0) + case-insensitive; assumptions None (all params source-traced), impl = simplified single-feature heuristic (not IUPred2A/MobiDB-lite).
- [[disorder-region-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit DISORDER-REGION-001 (disordered-region detection — contiguous-run aggregation + IDR classification over the [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp|PredictDisorder]] profile; fifth of the protein-disorder family, enriches the anchor): Campen 2008 + Dunker 2001 + van der Lee 2014 (proline-rich/acidic/basic/Ser-Thr-rich + short-vs-long≥30 subtypes) + Necci 2020 MobiDB-lite 3.0 v3 + Wikipedia sources; contiguous run ≥ minRegionLength(5) with MeanScore, empty/all-ordered→no regions / all-disordered→one region / trailing-region-no-off-by-one oracles; two classification schemes — default RegionType (fraction > 0.25 internal ~5×-random heuristic) vs opt-in ClassifyRegionFlavorMobiDbLite (charge PA/PPE/NPE/WC via Das&Pappu FCR/NCPR 0.35, composition Cys→Pro→Gly→SEG→Polar at ≥0.32, 9-residue window); hand-traced flavor oracles; contradiction flagged = 0.25 is NOT Das&Pappu NCPR (that is a conformational-state threshold); Confidence∈[0,1] declared heuristic (MobiDB-lite has none).
- [[protmotif-cc-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-CC-001 (coiled-coil prediction, heptad a/d hydrophobic-core occupancy; first of the ProteinMotif family): Mason & Arndt 2004 (heptad a/d burial, ≥3-heptad requirement) + Lupas 1991 (COILS: 7 registers, 28-residue window, "196 preliminary scores") + Wikipedia Coiled-coil/Heptad-repeat ({I,L,V} core set, leucine-zipper L at d) sources; `PredictCoiledCoils` scores each window by fraction of a/d positions ∈ {I,L,V} maximised over 7 registers, contiguous runs ≥21 residues emitted with peak Score∈[0,1]; closed-form oracles (LAALAAA)×5→(0,34,1.0) / all-Gly→0.0 / (LAAAAAA)→0.5 boundary; INV-01..05 (score∈[0,1], region≥21, len<window→empty, off-frame found via 7-register max); COILS 21×20 PSSM deliberately omitted (weights not retrievable) + {I,L,V}-only assumption, both source-anchored; new concept [[coiled-coil-prediction]], distinct from the ProteinPred disorder family.
- [[protmotif-common-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-COMMON-001 (common motif finding, `ProteinMotifFinder.FindCommonMotifs`; ProteinMotif family second unit): scans an amino-acid sequence against the fixed built-in `CommonMotifs` PROSITE-pattern dictionary (PS00001 N-glycosylation `N-{P}-[ST]-{P}`, PS00005 PKC phospho `[ST]-x-[RK]`, PS00006 CK2 phospho `[ST]-x(2)-[DE]`, PS00016 RGD `R-G-D`, PS00017 ATP/GTP A `[AG]-x(4)-G-K-[ST]`), reports every hit with accession/name; PROSITE syntax (x wildcard, [ ] allowed, { } excluded, x(n)/x(m,n) repetition), 0-based-inclusive MotifMatch, overlaps-all-reported; seven oracles; one API-shape (0- vs 1-based) assumption; concept [[common-protein-motifs]], the protein fixed-catalog analogue of DNA [[regulatory-element-detection]].
- [[protmotif-domain-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-DOMAIN-001 (protein domain prediction & signal-peptide prediction; ProteinMotif family): `FindDomains` deterministic PROSITE-**pattern** domain scan (PS00028 C2H2 zinc finger `C-x(2,4)-C-x(3)-[LIVMFYWC]-x(8)-H-x(3,5)-H`/PF00096, PS00017 P-loop `[AG]-x(4)-G-K-[ST]`/PF00069, PS00678 WD40 15-residue signature/PF00400; ScanProsite→regex rules; GBB1_HUMAN P62873 WD40 positive at 69/156/284) — SH3/PDZ are PROSITE **PROFILEs** with no deterministic pattern (honest residual, unsourced regexes removed); opt-in `FindDomainsByHmm`/`Plan7ProfileHmm` reproduces HMMER3 over 3 bundled CC0 Pfam HMMs (PF00018 SH3/PF00595 PDZ/PF00400 WD40) — Viterbi/Forward log-odds (1e-9 hand-HMM pin), local-multihit `pre_score` vs Swiss-Prot `bg->f` (~1e-5-bit hmmsearch parity), null2 bias, Gumbel/exp E-values (`E=P·Z`), `p7_domaindef` envelope decomposition (GBB1→7 blades exact) + stochastic-traceback clustering (Easel LCG seed 42), all verified vs pyhmmer 0.12.1; `PredictSignalPeptide` von Heijne tripartite n/h/c + −1,−3 rule {A,G,S}, weights (n+2h+c)/4, evidence-based constraints (nScore>0 & hScore≥0.5, no arbitrary threshold), Probability=Score; C2H2 4..24 / P-loop 4..11 / signal `MKRLLL…`→cleavage≈25 oracles; six resolved design decisions; MSV/bias prefilters + exact-RNG parity + full-Pfam out of scope; new concept [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]].
- [[protmotif-find-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-FIND-001 (Protein Motif Search, Pattern-based; ProteinMotif family general engine): `ProteinMotifFinder.FindMotifByPattern` — the **general, arbitrary caller-supplied PROSITE-pattern** protein motif finder that [[common-protein-motifs|`FindCommonMotifs`]] is a fixed-dictionary application of. Three primitives: `ConvertPrositeToRegex` (PROSITE→regex: `x`→`.`, `[ABC]`→`[ABC]`, `{ABC}`→`[^ABC]`, `x(n)`→`.{n}`, `x(n,m)`→`.{n,m}`, `<`→`^`, `>`→`$`); `FindMotifByPattern` (overlapping matches via regex lookahead `(?=(pattern))`, ScanProsite-consistent, 0-based Start/End, case-insensitive, empty/null→empty, invalid regex handled gracefully); information-content scoring `CalculateMotifScore` IC=Σlog₂(20/allowed_count) over constrained positions + `CalculateEValue` E=(N−L+1)·2^(−IC) (Schneider & Stephens 1990 — BLAST citation explicitly removed). Verified PROSITE patterns PS00001/00004–00009/00016–00018/00028/00029 and **fixed two impl bugs**: PS00007 `[RK].{2}[DE].{3}Y` (was loosened `.{2,3}`) and PS00018 EF-hand (`{W}` not `x` at pos 2 + restored trailing `[LIVMFYW]`); five non-PROSITE patterns literature-verified (NLS1/NES1/SIM1/WW1/SH3_1). Datasets: Human Insulin P01308 + constructed pattern fixtures; all assumptions eliminated (0-vs-1-based coord convention only); new concept [[protein-motif-pattern-search]].

- [[meta-class-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit META-CLASS-001 (Taxonomic classification, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.ClassifyReads` + `BuildKmerDatabase` + `TaxonomyTree.Lca`; fourth Metagenomics family Evidence): faithful Kraken algorithm (Wood & Salzberg 2014) + Kraken 1/2 manuals + Wikipedia Metagenomics sources; canonical-k-mer (min(kmer,revcomp), default k=31) → LCA-of-owning-taxa database, per-read classification tree (hit taxa + ancestors weighted by k-mer count) → max-scoring root-to-leaf (RTL) path leaf, ties → LCA of leaves, no hits → Unclassified (root); Confidence = C/Q (Kraken 2, C = clade k-mers, Q = non-ambiguous queried); invariants |out|=|in| / 0≤C/Q≤1 / C≤Q / canonical uniqueness / DB-build LCA / RTL assignment / LCA siblings→parent-ancestor→ancestor-disjoint→root; empty/short-<k/no-hit → Unclassified, empty DB → all Unclassified corner cases; C1 enhancement superseded the obsolete flat best-hit wording; no open questions / no deviations. - [[meta-beta-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit META-BETA-001 (Beta diversity, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.CalculateBetaDiversity`; second Metagenomics family Evidence, sibling of META-ALPHA-001): Whittaker 1960 (α/β/γ) + Bray & Curtis 1957 + Jaccard 1901 + Wikipedia sources; two between-sample dissimilarities over two taxon→abundance maps — Bray-Curtis BC=1−2·Σmin(N_ij,N_ik)/Σ(N_ij+N_ik) (abundance, NOT a true metric) and Jaccard distance J=1−|A∩B|/|A∪B| (presence/absence via >0, true metric); union-pass O(u), no BC normalization, +SharedSpecies/UniqueToSample1/2 counts; fish-tank oracle BC 13/33≈0.3939 & J 1/3≈0.3333, symmetry BC 3/5 & J 2/3, identical→0/0, disjoint→1/1, both-empty→0/0, one-empty→1; one accepted deviation = UniFracDistance hard-coded 0 (needs a phylo tree); no contradictions.
- [[meta-func-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit META-FUNC-001 (Functional prediction, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.PredictFunctions` + `FindPathwayEnrichment`; fifth Metagenomics family Evidence): Altschul NCBI BLAST-statistics tutorial + NCBI `blast_stat.c` (ungapped BLOSUM62 λ=0.3176/K=0.134/H=0.4012) + NCBI BLOSUM62 diagonals (W11…) + PNNL ORA §8.2 sources; homology transfer = exact-signature `string.Contains` hit scored by BLOSUM62 self-score S → bit `S'=(λS−lnK)/ln2` and E-value `E=K·m·n·e^(−λS)=m·n·2^(−S')`, best hit = lowest E-value (INV-01..03,06); hypergeometric right-tail ORA `P(X≥x)=1−Σ_{i=0}^{x−1}C(M,i)C(N−M,n−i)/C(N,n)` in log-Gamma space, p∈[0,1], x=0/M=0/n=0→p=1 (INV-04,05); oracles WWW→S33/S'18.0202932787533/E 3.3852730346546e−5 (both forms agree) + ORA N8000/M400/n100/x20→7.88e−8; one assumption ASM-01 = ungapped exact-match model (affects which hits found, not the formulas); no contradictions. Own concept [[functional-prediction]]; the ORA half is the shared-but-separate META-PATHWAY-001 unit (now ingested, owned by [[pathway-enrichment-ora]]).
- [[meta-pathway-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit META-PATHWAY-001 (Pathway enrichment / over-representation analysis, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindPathwayEnrichment` / `HypergeometricUpperTail`; the DEDICATED unit for the ORA machinery that META-FUNC-001 exercises as component B): Boyle et al. 2004 GO::TermFinder (PMC3037731) + PNNL Proteomics ORA §8.2 (`phyper` reference) sources; hypergeometric right-tail `P(X≥x)=1−Σ_{i=0}^{x−1}C(M,i)C(N−M,n−i)/C(N,n)` (N=background/M=pathway size/n=query/x=overlap), `phyper(x−1,M,N−M,n,lower.tail=FALSE)`, log-Gamma summation, p∈[0,1], sorted ascending; x=0/M=0/n=0→p=1 corner cases, M↔n symmetry; oracles PNNL N8000/M100/n400/x20→7.88e−8 + exact rational 1/252 (all overlap) / 5/6 (partial) / 1 (no overlap) / 251/252 (at-least-one); one assumption = background defaults to union-of-pathway-members when caller supplies none (formula-preserving, caller-overridable); no FDR correction; no contradictions. Own concept [[pathway-enrichment-ora]].
- [[meta-resist-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit META-RESIST-001 (Antibiotic-resistance gene detection, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindAntibioticResistanceGenes`; seventh Metagenomics family Evidence): Zankari 2012 (original ResFinder — BLASTed DB "best-matching gene", 2/5 coverage floor, 98% ID selected to suppress fragment noise) + ResFinder GitHub (`-t 0.80`/`-l 0.60` defaults) + Sci Rep 2023 & JAC 2016 (98% ID/60% cov, coverage relative to reference length, edge/split-contig rationale) + Heng Li 2018 (BLAST identity = matches/alignment-columns, gapless→window length) + CARD RGI (Perfect=100% full-length, best-hit by bit score) sources; gapless `BestUngappedMatch` slide (offsets −(m−1)..n−1) → identity=matches/w & coverage=w/m, dual-threshold report (id≥t AND cov≥t), best match per contig (max identity, tie→max coverage); INV-01..05, defaults 0.90 ID/0.60 cov; oracles CGTACGT@AAACGTACGT→1.0/1.0, CGTTCGT vs CGTACGT→6/7≈0.857/1.0, edge CGTA→1.0 / 4⁄7≈0.571; one assumption ASM-01 = gapless model (indel matches under-scored; substitution + contig-edge truncation exact); flagged provenance note (evidence 0.80/0.98 vs impl 0.90 default). - [[meta-prof-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit META-PROF-001 (Taxonomic profile / community abundance profiling, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.GenerateTaxonomicProfile`; sixth Metagenomics family Evidence): Wikipedia Metagenomics/Relative-abundance-distribution + MetaPhlAn docs + Segata 2012 (Nature Methods) sources; aggregates an `IEnumerable<TaxonomicClassification>` (the per-read output of META-CLASS-001) into a `TaxonomicProfile` — relative-abundance maps at four ranks (kingdom/phylum/genus/species, count(taxon)/Σcount(classified)), inline species-level Shannon H=−Σpᵢln(pᵢ) (nats) + Simpson λ=Σpᵢ², and TotalReads/ClassifiedReads; Unclassified excluded from denominators, empty rank strings filtered; invariants Σabundance≈1.0 per rank / ClassifiedReads≤TotalReads / ClassifiedReads=Σ(counts any rank) / Shannon≥0 / 0≤Simpson≤1; oracles Shannon=ln(3) for 3 uniform species, Simpson=0.375 for [2,1,1], TotalReads3/ClassifiedReads2; empty→0/0/empty, all-Unclassified→ClassifiedReads0, single taxon→abundance1/H0/λ1, empty-sum→H0/λ0; verified design decisions all mathematical facts (nats log, concentration-index λ, empty→0); no contradictions / no deviations. Own concept [[taxonomic-profile]].
- [[meta-taxa-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit META-TAXA-001 (Significant / differentially-abundant taxa detection, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.MannWhitneyU` / `FindSignificantTaxa`; eighth Metagenomics family Evidence): Wikipedia Mann–Whitney U (citing Mann & Whitney 1947) + SciPy `mannwhitneyu` + Xia & Sun 2017 (PMC6128532, microbiome domain) + A&S 7.1.26 erf sources; per-taxon two-group Mann–Whitney U / Wilcoxon rank-sum with midrank ties, tie-corrected `σ_U`, optional 0.5 continuity correction (SciPy default), z from `max(U1,U2)`, two-tailed `p=2·(1−Φ(z))` via `StatisticsHelper.NormalCDF`; invariants U1+U2=n1·n2 / 0≤U≤n1·n2 / p∈[0,1] / Significant⇔p<threshold / all-tied→σ0→p1 / group-swap symmetric; oracles SciPy x[19,22,16,29,24]/y[20,11,17,12]→U1=17/U2=3/σ=sqrt(200/12)/z_cc=1.5922→p≈0.11135/z_nocc=1.7146→p≈0.08641 + tortoise/hare U_T=11/U_H=25/sum=36; empty group→ArgumentException, label∉{1,2}/length-mismatch→ArgumentException, empty profiles→empty, absent taxon→0; asymptotic-not-exact + no-FDR limitations; three source-backed assumptions (cc-on default, two-tailed, two-label/absence=0); no contradictions. - [[onco-ccf-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit ONCO-CCF-001 (cancer cell fraction estimation + 1D clonal/subclonal clustering; fifth Oncology unit): Tarabichi 2021 Nat. Methods (Box 1: CCF=CP/purity, closed form CCF=f·(ρ·N_T+2(1−ρ))/(ρ·m), m rounded to nearest non-zero int, highest-CP cluster=clonal) + Zheng 2022 PICTograph (VAF=(m·CCF·p)/(c·p+2(1−p)), no [0,1] cap) + McGranahan 2016 (n_mut=VAF·(1/p)·[p·CN_t+2(1−p)], CCF=n_mut/m) + CNAqc (raw CCF 1.06 noise case, formula not bounded ≤1) + Lloyd 1982 k-means sources; exact oracles A–F (clonal-diploid→1.0, subclonal→0.5, m=2→1.0, purity-0.5→1.0, noise 0.942, overshoot 1.5→cap 1.0) + Lloyd k=2 {1.0,0.98,0.96,0.50,0.48,0.52}→centroids {0.50,0.98}, clonal=0.98-cluster; two source-consistent assumptions ([0,1] reported cap exposing raw; deterministic Lloyd k-means + quantile seeding as the 1D method); no contradictions (formula corroborated three ways). Own concept [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]].

- [[phylo-tree-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-TREE-001 (Phylogenetic Tree Construction — UPGMA & Neighbor-Joining; the phylogenetics PHYLO-* tree-building core): Wikipedia UPGMA / Neighbor-joining / Phylogenetic-tree + Saitou & Nei 1987 (MBE 4(4):406–425, NJ) + Sokal & Michener 1958 (UPGMA) + Felsenstein 2004 sources; `BuildTree`/`BuildTreeFromMatrix` consume the distance matrix and emit a `PhyloNode` tree via two agglomerative methods — **UPGMA** (rooted ultrametric, molecular clock, **height=d/2**, arithmetic-mean update, O(n³)/O(n²)) and **NJ** (unrooted/midpoint-rooted, clock-free, **Q(i,j)=(n−2)·d(i,j)−Σd(i,k)−Σd(j,k)** join minimum-Q, δ(f,u)=d(f,g)/2+(Σd(f,k)−Σd(g,k))/(2(n−2)), additive-matrix topology guarantee, **negative branches preserved, not clamped**, O(n³)); invariants all-taxa-leaves / binary / n leaves+n−1 internal / UPGMA branches≥0 / UPGMA ultrametric+rooted / NJ additive-correct+may-be-negative+no-clock; oracles UPGMA 5S-rRNA matrix→(a,b)@17→((a,b),e)@22→(c,d)@28→final@33, δ(a,u)=8.5/δ(e,v)=11/δ(c,w)=14/root 16.5 (tips all 16.5, tol 1e-10), NJ 5-taxon→first join (a,b) **Q₁(a,b)=−50**, δ(a,u)=2/δ(b,u)=3/δ(u,v)=3/δ(c,v)=4/δ(v,w)=2/δ(d,w)=2/δ(e,w)=1 (patristic recovers input); edge cases <2/unequal→throw, identical→arbitrary join, all-equal→star, saturated p>0.75→JC +∞; 32 runs (M01–M13/S01–S05/C01–C05), S06 removed (dup of S02); deviations None (§8). Own concept [[distance-based-tree-construction]].
- [[pop-ancestry-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-ANCESTRY-001 (Ancestry Estimation — supervised/projection ADMIXTURE, estimate ancestry proportions Q by EM with **fixed** reference allele frequencies F; **first population-genetics POP-\* unit**): Alexander, Novembre & Lange 2009 *Genome Research* 19(9):1655 (rank 1 — genotype g∈{0,1,2}=allele-1 count, Q I×K / F K×J, **log-likelihood Eq. 2** `L=ΣᵢΣⱼ{g·ln(Σq·f)+(2−g)·ln(Σq·(1−f))}` under `Σ_k q_ik=1`, **FRAPPE EM Eq. 4** `q^{n+1}=(1/2J)Σⱼ[g·a+(2−g)·b]`, convergence Eq. 5 ΔL<ε default 10⁻⁴, cost O(IJK²), K! label-permutation maxima) + Alexander & Lange 2011 *BMC Bioinformatics* 12:246 (supervised mode — labelled reference individuals as training samples, less allele-freq uncertainty; full text Springer-gated) + ADMIXTURE 1.4 Manual §2.10 supervised / §2.14 projection (reference rows of Q pinned, refs 100% single-ancestry; learned F as fixed input `admixture -P`) sources; oracles symmetric K=2 J=2 panel f_A=[0.8,0.2]/f_B=[0.2,0.8] g=[2,0] from (0.5,0.5) → **one EM iter (0.8,0.2) exactly** → (0.9412,0.0588) → converges (1.0,0.0), single-SNP f=[0.9,0.1] g=2→(0.9,0.1)/g=1→(0.5,0.5) uninformative-het/g=0→(0.1,0.9), identical panels uniform fixed point; MUST Σ_k q=1 / EM-ascent L non-decreasing / diagnostic→source; two assumptions (maxIterations budget augments ε=10⁻⁴ convergence — same fixed point; missing genotype ∉{0,1,2} skipped); label non-identifiability pinned by fixed labelled panels; no contradictions. - [[pop-div-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-DIV-001 (Diversity statistics — nucleotide diversity π, Watterson's θ, Tajima's D, heterozygosity; **second population-genetics POP-\* unit**, sibling of POP-ANCESTRY-001): Nei & Li 1979 *PNAS* (π = Σ_{i<j} d_ij / (C(n,2)·L), mean per-site pairwise differences) + Watterson 1975 *TPB* (θ̂_W = S/a_n, a_n = Σ_{i=1}^{n−1} 1/i harmonic number; per-site θ_W = S/(a_n·L)) + Tajima 1989 *Genetics* (D = (k̂ − S/a_1)/√(e_1·S + e_2·S(S−1)), **k̂ = average pairwise-difference COUNT not per-site π**, variance terms a_1/a_2/b_1/b_2/c_1/c_2/e_1/e_2; D≈0 neutral / D<0 excess rare alleles=sweep-or-expansion / D>0 deficit=balancing-or-contraction) + Nei 1978 *Genetics* (unbiased gene diversity H_obs = n/(n−1)·H_exp, H_exp = (1/L)Σ(1−Σp²); haploid H_obs ≡ π) sources; all "exact match" no deviations; Wikipedia oracle n=5/L=20/S=4/a_1=25/12 → k̂=2.0/π=0.1/S/a_1≈1.92/d=0.08/θ_W≈0.096 → **D≈0.273** (TD-C01/TD-C02); edge cases n=0→0, n=1→π0/θ undef, n=2→π defined but **D undefined→0** (needs n≥3), S=0/monomorphic→all 0, Var≤0→D=0; API note `CalculateTajimasD(k̂, S, n)` takes k̂ NOT per-site π; no contradictions. Own concept [[genetic-diversity-statistics]].
- [[pop-freq-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-FREQ-001 (Allele & genotype frequencies — major/minor frequencies, MAF, MAF filtering; foundational population-genetics POP-\* primitive): Wikipedia *Allele frequency* / *Genotype frequency* (biallelic `p = f(AA) + ½f(AB)`, `q = f(BB) + ½f(AB)`, **`p + q = 1`**; allele-counting `total = 2·(n_AA+n_AB+n_BB)`, `major = 2·n_AA+n_AB`, `minor = 2·n_BB+n_AB`; four-o'clock oracle 49/42/9 → freq(a)=0.30/freq(A)=0.70) + Wikipedia *Minor allele frequency* (`MAF = min(alt_freq, 1−alt_freq)`, **`0 ≤ MAF ≤ 0.5`**; HapMap MAF ≥ 0.05, common>0.05 vs rare<0.05) + VCF/PLINK dosage encoding (0=hom-ref/1=het/2=hom-alt, `alt_freq = Σg/(2n)`) + Gillespie 2004 / NDSU PopGen sources; oracles AF-1…AF-6, MAF-1…MAF-6 (alt_freq 0.7 → MAF 0.3 symmetry; monomorphic → 0; 50/50 → 0.5), FLT-1…FLT-6 (MAF<0.01 / <0.05 / >0.4, empty/all/none); invariants p+q=1, major+minor=total, MAF symmetric 0…0.5; edge cases zero samples→(0,0), empty vector→MAF 0, **negative count → `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`**; scope = biallelic counting/normalization only (no HWE test, no multiallelic, no phasing/imputation); all exact-match, no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[allele-genotype-frequencies]].
- [[pop-fst-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-FST-001 (Fst fixation index + F-statistics Fis/Fit/Fst + pairwise Fst; population-genetics POP-\* differentiation unit, **consumes** per-population allele frequencies from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Fixation index* (**Wright 1965 variance-based** `Fst = σ_S²/(pBar(1−pBar))`; two-pop `pBar=(n1·p1+n2·p2)/(n1+n2)`, `σ_S²=(n1(p1−pBar)²+n2(p2−pBar)²)/(n1+n2)`; multi-locus **ratio-of-sums** `Σσ_S²/Σhet`; Fst∈[0,1], 0=panmixia/1=fixed differences; **not a metric** — fails triangle inequality) + Wikipedia *F-statistics* (heterozygosity partition `Fis=1−Hi/Hs`, `Fit=1−Hi/Ht`, `Fst=1−Hs/Ht`; **exact identity** `(1−Fit)=(1−Fis)(1−Fst)`) + Wright 1950/1965, Weir & Cockerham 1984 (θ estimator — cited as what is **deliberately NOT** implemented: no ANOVA/finite-sample bias correction), Holsinger & Weir 2009, Cavalli-Sforza 1994 sources; oracles identical→0, fixed p1=1/p2=0→**1.0 exactly** (pBar=.5,var=.25,het=.25), pop1=(.9,.8)/pop2=(.1,.2)→1/2, unequal sizes 0.006274…, components Fis=1/19/Fit=1/13/Fst=1/39, scale 1/2499 & 61/198, pairwise cells 1/99,4/21,3/25, excess-het **negative** Fis=−2/3/Fit=−2/5/Fst=4/25; ref values Cavalli-Sforza (Mbuti–PNG 0.4573, mean 0.1338) + Elhaik 2012 HapMap; edge cases denominator 0 (pBar=0/1, both-fixed-same, empty)→**return 0**, monomorphic→0; pairwise matrix symmetric, zero diagonal; 25 tests (−1 dup +4 new); no deviations/contradictions. - [[pop-hw-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-HW-001 (Hardy-Weinberg equilibrium chi-square test; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** genotype counts from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Hardy-Weinberg principle* (Hardy 1908 / Weinberg 1908 — expected genotype freqs `f(AA)=p²`/`f(Aa)=2pq`/`f(aa)=q²`, Ford moth example, deviation causes, genotyping-error note) + Wikipedia *Chi-squared test* (Pearson goodness-of-fit `χ²=Σ(O−E)²/E`) + Emigh 1980 (chi-square comparison) + Wigginton et al. 2005 AJHG (**exact test** — cited as the out-of-scope alternative) sources; allele freq `p=(2·n_AA+n_Aa)/(2n)`/`q=1−p`, expected counts `E={p²n,2pqn,q²n}`, **df=1** (`#genotypes−#alleles=3−2`), p-value via chi-square CDF (lower-incomplete-gamma approx), default **α=0.05** critical 3.841; `TestHardyWeinberg` returns InEquilibrium/ChiSquare/PValue; oracles Ford moth (1469,138,5)→`p≈0.954`/`χ²≈0.83`→in-eq (HW-E01), perfect (25,50,25)→`χ²=0` (HW-E02), excess-het (10,80,10)→`χ²=36 ≫ 3.84`→out-of-eq (HW-E03), zero samples→InEquilibrium true/PValue 1 (HW-E04), fixed (100,0,0)→in-eq (HW-E05), all-het (0,100,0)→out-of-eq (HW-E06); edge cases **zero n→PValue 1** (no evidence against H₀), **expected-0 term skipped** (div-by-zero guard); scope = biallelic chi-square goodness-of-fit only (no exact test, no multiallelic); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]].
- [[pop-ld-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-LD-001 (Linkage disequilibrium — `CalculateLD` (D, D', r²) + `FindHaplotypeBlocks`; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** allele/haplotype frequencies from POP-FREQ-001): Wikipedia *Linkage disequilibrium* (`D = p_AB − p_A·p_B`; Lewontin 1964 `D' = |D|/D_max` with sign-branched `D_max` clamped [0,1]; Hill & Robertson 1968 `r² = D²/(p_A·q_A·p_B·q_B)`; **diploid-frequency result** `R_AB = r_AB` (Wright 1933) ⇒ r² computable **without phase**) + Wikipedia *Haplotype block* (Gabriel 2002 / Patil 2001 threshold blocks) sources; implementation `r²` = squared Pearson correlation of 0/1/2 genotype dosage vectors `Cov²/(Var·Var)`, `D` from diploid covariance `Cov=2D ⇒ D=Cov/2`; `FindHaplotypeBlocks` = simplified adjacent-pair Gabriel (consecutive `r² ≥ threshold`, default **0.7**, ≥2 variants); oracles perfect LD (identical vectors)→`r²≈1`, no LD (balanced)→`r²≈0`, anti-correlation→`r²=1`/`D'=1` (sign-blind), block oracles single→none / two-high→one / two-low→none / all-strong→one span / non-contiguous→multiple; INV `0≤r²≤1`, `0≤|D'|≤1`, block Start≤End/≥2/non-overlapping/ordered, distance+IDs preserved; edge cases empty→`r²=0,D'=0`, monomorphic (zero variance/denominator)→`r²=0` (guarded), all-identical→`r²=0`; scope = two-biallelic-loci r²/D' + adjacent-pair blocks only (no full LD matrix, no phasing/EM, no decay-curve fit, no exact Gabriel CI); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[linkage-disequilibrium]].
- [[pop-select-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit POP-SELECT-001 (Selection-signature detection — `CalculateEhh`, `CalculateIHS`, `StandardizeIHS`, `ScanForSelection` = integrated Haplotype Score iHS; population-genetics POP-\* unit, **consumes** derived/ancestral allele freqs + MAF filter from POP-FREQ-001): Voight et al. 2006 PLoS Biol (**iHS = ln(iHH_A/iHH_D)** ancestral numerator, standardized to std-normal in derived-freq bins, integration truncated at **EHH<0.05**, scan = proportion `|iHS|>2` in ~50-SNP windows, **MAF>5%**) + Sabeti 2002 (EHH = homozygosity prob of two core-allele chromosomes) + selscan Szpiech & Hernandez 2014 (`EHH_c=ΣC(n_h,2)/C(n_c,2)`, trapezoidal iHH, **opposite sign convention** `ln(iHH_1/iHH_0)`) + rehh (worked SNP F1205400 `iHH_A=284429.9`/`iHH_D=2057107.4`→ln=**−1.978569274**, `limehh`/`freqbin`=0.05) sources; oracles constructed panel iHH_A=10/iHH_D=40→ln(0.25)=**−1.386294361** (long derived haplotype→negative iHS), EHH unit values 0.5/0.3333/1.0/0.0, balanced decay→iHS≈0; INV EHH∈[0,1], single-element bin→std iHS 0, window value = count(|iHS|>2)/size; throws on monomorphic core / null / empty / inconsistent-length / invalid core allele / OOR coreIndex; assumptions (N−1 SD, 20 default bins) affect magnitude only; scope = single-core iHS/EHH scan (no XP-EHH, no Fst-outlier/Tajima's-D scan, no genetic-map interpolation); no deviations/contradictions. Own concept [[selection-scan-ihs-ehh]].
- [[primer-tm-001-dimer-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PRIMER-TM-001 (self-/hetero-dimer melting temperature; **first PCR-primer-design PRIMER-\* / MolTools unit**): SantaLucia & Hicks 2004 (unified DNA nearest-neighbour ΔH°/ΔS°, bimolecular Tm Eq. 3 with symmetry factor x=1 palindrome / x=4 otherwise, [Na⁺] entropy salt correction Eq. 5) + Untergasser 2012 Primer3 `ntthal` thermodynamic-alignment engine + `thal.c` reference constants + primer3-py 2.3.0 numeric oracle; the dimer DP now models the full possibly-non-contiguous optimum (internal mismatch/loop, bulge, `tstack2` terminal overhang), reproducing `calc_homodimer`/`calc_heterodimer` to machine precision (GCGCGCGC self x=1 Tm 40.0906 °C, TGCATGCATG/CATGCATGCA x=4 Tm 25.6596 °C, GCGCATGCGC 2×2 loop Tm 43.1572 °C); no stable dimer (poly-A) / invalid input → null/NaN; deviations none remaining. Own concept [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]].
- [[primer-tm-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for the **base** test unit PRIMER-TM-001 (**Primer3 weighted per-primer penalty / objective function** — a *selection/scoring* algorithm, not a Tm calc, sibling of the dimer-Tm unit): Primer3 `libprimer3.cc` `p_obj_fn` (weighted sum of sign-gated one-sided deviations — Tm `temp_gt·(Tm−opt)`/`temp_lt·(opt−Tm)`, GC% `gc_content_gt/lt`, size `length_gt/lt`, plus `compl_any·self_any + compl_end·self_end + num_ns·#N`; **lower is better**, primers sorted ascending) + `libprimer3.h` (`DEFAULT_OPT_GC_PERCENT` undefined) + manual §19 + Untergasser 2012; defaults `opt_tm=60`/`opt_size=20`, weights `temp_*=length_*=1`, `gc/self/num_ns=0` ⇒ **default objective `|Tm−60|+|len−20|`**; oracles (60,20)→0.0, (63,20)→3.0, (57,18)→5.0, combined→8.0; sign-gated (at optimum term=0), weight-zero short-circuit, penalty≥0 (=0 iff all-optimal); `self_any`/`self_end` are caller-supplied `dpal` local-alignment scores (arithmetic exact, input external); no contradictions. Own concept [[primer3-weighted-penalty-objective]].
- [[primer-tm-001-hairpin-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PRIMER-TM-001 (**intramolecular hairpin self-folding MFE + unimolecular hairpin Tm** — the hairpin/secondary-structure extension of the primer-Tm unit; same ntthal/`thal.c` engine as the dimer): SantaLucia & Hicks 2004 (Table 1 unified DNA NN ΔH°/ΔS° reused verbatim as `NnUnifiedParams` stem stacks + **Table 4 hairpin-loop ΔG°37 increments** 3→3.5…30→6.3, loop ΔH°=0 / loop ΔS°=−ΔG°37·1000/310.15, **unimolecular hairpin Tm Eq. 11 `Tm=ΔH°·1000/ΔS°−273.15` with NO `R·ln(C_T/x)` concentration term**, Jacobson-Stockmayer large-loop Eq. 7 coeff 2.44, steric floor loops <3 nt, supplementary triloop/tetraloop + closing-A·T +0.5 as opt-in caller increment) + SantaLucia 1998 NN cross-check + Vallone & Benight 1999 (hairpin Tm concentration-independent 0.5–260 µM); hand-derived oracles `GGGCTTTTGCCC` (4-bp GGGC stem, TTTT loop) → ΔH°=−25.8, ΔS°=−75.48486216346927, ΔG°37=−2.3883700000000054, **Tm=68.6404 °C**, `GGGCAAAAAGCCC` (5-nt loop, 3.3) → Tm≈71.585 °C, poly-A → no hairpin (null)/NaN; assumptions bimolecular init & terminal-A·T penalty excluded (unimolecular core, UNAFold-consistent); no contradictions. Enriches concept [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]].
- [[primer-tm-001-nn-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PRIMER-TM-001 (**per-oligo nearest-neighbour salt-corrected design Tm**, opt-in — the core ΔH°/ΔS°→Tm path + salt corrections, same SantaLucia model as the dimer/hairpin siblings): SantaLucia & Hicks 2004 (Table 1 unified NN ΔH°/ΔS°, Tm Eq. 3 with x=1/4 symmetry factor, p.419 worked example **Tm 35.8 °C**, Na⁺ entropy Eq. 5 `0.368·(N/2)·ln[Na⁺]` valid 0.05–1.1 M / ≤16 bp, Tables 2 & 3 mismatch/dangling cross-check) + **Owczarzy 2004** monovalent quadratic 1/Tm correction `(4.29·f(GC)−3.95)·1e−5·ln[Na]+9.40e−6·(ln[Na])²` (non-linear over 69 mM–1.02 M) + **Owczarzy 2008** divalent Mg²⁺/dNTP 1/Tm correction (dNTP chelation Ka=3×10⁴, mixed-regime reparam, falls back to monovalent) + Biopython `DNA_NN4`/`DNA_IMM`/`DNA_DE`/`Tm_NN`/`salt_correction` methods 5–7 (verbatim transcription of Allawi/SantaLucia/Peyret + Bommarito 2000 primaries → `NnInternalMismatch`/`NnDanglingEnd`; complement-not-revcomp key convention mirrored in `CalculateNearestNeighborThermodynamicsMismatch`); oracles GCGCGC self x=1 Tm 35.0473, ATGCATGC x=4 Tm 30.4338, CGCGAATTCGCG 61.1452 (@1 M/0.5 µM), Owczarzy vs Eq.5 @50 mM Na, CGTGAC/GCGCTG T·G mismatch Tm −6.4061; assumptions default C_T=0.5 µM + N=2·(len−1); non-ACGT → null/NaN; no contradictions. Enriches concept [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]].
- [[primer-tm-001-special-loop-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PRIMER-TM-001 (**bundled special tri/tetraloop hairpin bonus tables** — the sequence-specific loop stability bonuses ntthal adds to a length-3/4 hairpin loop, now applied inside `calc_hairpin`, completing the opt-in increment the hairpin sibling flagged): libprimer3 `triloop.dh/.ds` (**16** entries, 5-char key incl. closing pair, ΔH −1500/−2000 by closing-pair family, **all ΔS=0**) + `tetraloop.dh/.ds` (**76** entries, 6-char key → `NtthalHairpin.TetraloopTable`, e.g. CGAAAG ΔH=−1100 ΔS=0) + `thal.c` `calc_hairpin` (bonus **added** for loopSize==3/==4 via bsearch, key = full loop string incl. closing pair, ΔH cal/mol / ΔS cal/K/mol; loops.* size ΔS°, unimolecular `Tm=mh/(ms+(N/2−1)·saltCorr)−273.15`) + SantaLucia & Hicks 2004 Eqs. 8–9 (model source) + primer3-py 2.3.0 oracles (tetraloop CGAAAG `GGGGCGAAAGCCCC` Tm 85.0335 °C, triloop CGAAG `GGGCGAAGCCC` Tm 84.7061 °C, non-special TTTT `GGGCTTTTGCCC` Tm 69.3995 °C unchanged, homopolymer/short → structure_found=False); only 3/4-nt loops get a bonus, closing pair is part of the key, legacy `FindMostStableHairpin`+`loopBonusDeltaG37` path unchanged; assumptions none correctness-affecting (verbatim, machine-precision verified); no contradictions. Enriches concept [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]].
- [[probe-design-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PROBE-DESIGN-001 (**TaqMan 5'-nuclease hydrolysis-probe design rules**, opt-in extension over the unchanged generic hybridization-probe designer; **first PROBE-\* unit**): Applied Biosystems / Thermo Fisher (rank 2, chemistry manufacturer) + PREMIER Biosoft (rank 3) + ScienceDirect "TaqMan" (5'-G quenching rationale) + IDT (corroborating) sources; the TaqMan-specific hard rules — **no G at the 5' end** (a 5'-G quenches the reporter *even after cleavage* → hard rule, not a soft penalty; `SelectTaqManStrand` moves to the antisense strand when unavoidable), **more Cs than Gs**, **no run of ≥4 consecutive Gs** (separate from the generic homopolymer cap), **GC 30–80%**, **length 18–22 nt** (default, `minLength`/`maxLength` parameterised), **probe Tm ≥ primer Tm + 10 °C** (caller-supplied primer Tm; probe Tm via the PRIMER-TM-001-validated salt-adjusted `81.5+16.6·log₁₀[Na⁺]+41·GC−600/N` formula, not a TaqMan-specific NN calc); oracles CCATCACCCTACATCACC passes-all (primerTm ≤ 39.35), GCATCACCCTACATCACC fails 5'-G, ACCCCGGGGACCCTACAT fails GGGG-run, C=1/G=9 fails more-G-than-C, 16-nt fails len<18, GC 100% fails, sense GTTAGGGTTAGGGTTAGG → RC CCTAACCCTAACCCTAAC strand-selection; two parameterisation assumptions (18–22 default window, repository salt-adjusted Tm engine), no source contradictions. Own concept [[taqman-probe-design-rules]].
- [[probe-design-001-lna-evidence]] — evidence artifact for the **LNA (locked nucleic acid) Tm-adjustment** variant of PROBE-DESIGN-001: an **LNA-adjusted nearest-neighbour Tm** that raises a probe's Tm/specificity (enabling shorter MGB-style 13–20 nt probes) by locking internal bases. Sources: **McTigue, Peterson & Kahn 2004** (*Biochemistry*, rank 1 — ΔΔH°/ΔΔS° increments for all **32** LNA+DNA:DNA nearest neighbours; internal LNA **raises Tm**), **MELTING 5** reference impl (`McTigue2004lockedmn.xml` verbatim table in **cal/mol** + `McTigue04LockedAcid.java` — **additive-increment** application and **terminal-LNA rejection**), rmelting worked example. Model: compute plain DNA NN ΔH°/ΔS° then **add** the McTigue increment per LNA-containing step, onto the library's SantaLucia-1998-unified DNA NN engine (same as PRIMER-TM-001 [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]); terminal/non-ACGT/out-of-range → not-computable. Oracle CCATTGCTACC (LNA@4) → ΔH° −80.014 / ΔS° −216.6 → LNA Tm **63.528 °C** vs all-DNA 59.692 (**ΔTm +3.84 °C**), agreeing with MELTING `mct04` 63.614 to 0.086 °C (documented base-NN-set residual; increments applied exactly). Enriches [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] (LNA section).
- [[probe-valid-001-evidence]] — evidence artifact for test unit PROBE-VALID-001 (**hybridization-probe validation / off-target specificity scan** — a **gapped Smith–Waterman local alignment** of the candidate probe against a pooled reference, replacing an earlier ungapped Hamming scan; the **specificity-checking sibling** of PROBE-DESIGN-001, a genuinely distinct algorithm): Smith & Waterman 1981 (local-alignment recurrence with the **zero floor** → local, indel-aware; traceback stops at 0 so a mismatched tail is trimmed), Altschul et al. 1990/1997 BLAST (the **gapped-vs-ungapped** improvement — a single gapped alignment finds indel off-targets the ungapped HSPs miss; the unit realizes the *gapped local alignment* property, an **exact** full SW scan, not seed-and-extend or a genome-scale index), Karlin & Altschul 1990 / Altschul 1990 statistics (opt-in `ComputeLambdaNucleotide`/`ComputeKarlinAltschul`: `E=K·m·n·e^(−λS)`, λ = root of `Σ p_i p_j e^(λ s_ij)=1`, bit score `S'=(λS−ln K)/ln 2`, `E=m·n·2^(−S')`; preconditions expected-score<0 **and** a positive score; K caller-supplied), Kane et al. 2000 (empirical **>75% identity** cross-hybridization threshold, `minIdentity` default 0.75, caller-configurable; <14–15 contiguous-complement caveat); oracles — probe `ACGTACGTACGT` vs an indel copy `ACGTACTGTACGT` aligns `ACGTAC-GTACGT` 12/12 identity 1.0 `HasGaps=true` (**found by gapped, missed by ungapped Hamming maxMismatches=3**); indel+mismatch `ACGTACTGTACTT` → SW trims `TT` tail → 10/12 = 0.8333 (admitted @0.75, rejected @0.90); λ for +1/−3 uniform-0.25 = **1.3740631** (≈ blastn 1.37, expected score −2.0<0), K=0.711/S=30/m=20/n=1000 → bit **59.9627**, **E=1.7802e−14**, E↓ in S and linear in m·n; BLAST DNA scoring +2/−3 gap −2. ASSUMPTION: on-target = first perfect ungapped full-coverage exact match (API/labelling, not a sourced constant); no source contradictions. Own concept [[probe-offtarget-specificity-scan]].

## Concepts

- [[three-front-doors]] — one algorithm engine exposed through skills, the C# API, and MCP, with identical results.
- [[skill-layer]] — the Agent-Skill routing + discipline layer that keeps 427 tool schemas out of the model's context.
- [[layered-architecture]] — the strict up-only dependency layering (Levels 0–4) enforced by architecture tests.
- [[scientific-rigor]] — runtime honesty: `LimitationPolicy`, tool-only computation, provenance on every result.
- [[validation-and-testing]] — 22k+ tests across ten methodologies plus the per-unit validation campaign.
- [[property-based-testing]] — P0 methodology (FsCheck): hundreds of generated inputs checked against expressible invariants (R/S/I/M/P/RT/D); 258/258.
- [[metamorphic-testing]] — P0 methodology: metamorphic relations across runs (SUB/MON/INV/SYM/COMP/SHIFT) that solve the oracle problem; 258/258, ~200+ relations.
- [[fuzzing]] — P2 methodology: random/malformed/boundary input for clean-failure; parsers the hot target; zero→258/258.
- [[snapshot-testing]] — P1 methodology (Verify): golden-master `.verified.txt` regression capture; the least-complete methodology at 37/255.
- [[algebraic-testing]] — P1 methodology: explicit algebraic laws (identity/associativity/involution/round-trip…); 89 applicable + 169 not-applicable.
- [[architecture-testing]] — P2 methodology (ArchUnitNET): 22 IL-level module rules enforcing the [[layered-architecture]] Dependency Rule; scales by module not algorithm.
- [[differential-testing]] — P2 methodology: two independent implementations cross-checked (ALT/BRUTE/REF/DUAL); 107/255.
- [[combinatorial-testing]] — P3 methodology: minimal pairwise parameter-interaction coverage; 193/255 + 65 not-applicable.
- [[characterization-testing]] — P3 methodology: golden-master pinning of behaviour before refactors (invariance, not correctness); on-demand.
- [[build-quality-gate]] — the build-time static-analysis gate: SonarAnalyzer ratcheted to blocking under `TreatWarningsAsErrors`, fix-or-silence, review-not-blind-fix.
- [[test-unit-registry]] — the area-prefixed Test Unit ID scheme and per-unit record behind the validation effort.
- [[definition-of-done]] — the six-criterion acceptance bar (TestSpec, tests, ≥80% coverage, edge cases, CI, evidence) each unit must clear.
- [[algorithm-validation-evidence]] — the templated per-unit `docs/Evidence/` artifact pattern (sources, worked-example dataset, deviations) behind the "Evidence documented" DoD criterion.
- [[global-alignment-needleman-wunsch]] — the canonical DP global-alignment algorithm (`GlobalAlign`): linear-gap recurrence, O(nm), traceback, affine-as-extension.
- [[multiple-sequence-alignment]] — aligning 3+ sequences (NP-complete): Seqeron's star (`MultipleAlign`), iterative-refinement (MUSCLE), and consistency (T-Coffee) aligners; sum-of-pairs + consensus.
- [[semi-global-alignment-fitting]] — ends-free "glocal" alignment: fitting/query-in-reference variant (Rosalind SIMS); NW recurrence with free reference end gaps, traceback from max of last row.
- [[alignment-statistics]] — post-alignment metrics: percent identity/similarity/gaps (EMBOSS/BLAST convention, denominator includes gaps, positive-score ⇒ similar) and srspair three-line markup.
- [[coding-potential-hexamer-score]] — CPAT hexamer usage-bias coding-potential score: mean of ln(coding/noncoding) over in-frame hexamers (wordSize 6/step 3), sign convention, ±1 pseudo-scores; Fickett TESTCODE as not-implemented alternative.
- [[relative-synonymous-codon-usage]] — RSCU (Sharp & Li 1986) codon-usage-bias measure: n_i·x/Σx normalization, 1.0=no bias, bounded [0,n_i], Σ-over-family=n_i invariant; pooled counts, sense codons only; base anchor of the codon-usage family (vs CAI's max-normalization).
- [[codon-adaptation-index]] — CAI (Sharp & Li 1987) whole-gene codon-bias / expression-proxy score in [0,1]: geometric mean of relative adaptiveness w=f/max_synonym_f, low-value-sensitive, stop excluded; dual include/exclude-Met/Trp mode (exclude can give L=0→0); E. coli oracles; Seqeron deviation = 1e-6 zero-freq clamp (vs Sharp & Li's 0.5 reference-table pseudocount); one level above RSCU.
- [[rare-codon-analysis]] — codon-usage family's *localization/diagnostic* unit (`FindRareCodons` + cluster addendum): a codon is rare when its per-family frequency < threshold (default 0.15), reports position/AA/frequency (E. coli AGA 0.04/AGG 0.02/CGA 0.06/CUA 0.04); addendum adds two published cluster methods — Clarke & Clark 2008 %MinMax (18-codon window, signed %Min/%Max ∈[−100,+100], rare clusters = negative peaks) and Chartier 2012 Sherlocc (7-codon window, ≥4 of 7 freq≤threshold "slow" positions = a rare-codon cluster); single-codon-AA contributes 0 to %MinMax (no NaN), overlapping windows merged; feeds [[codon-optimization]]'s AvoidRareCodons; oracles −86.36/+100/+36.47% and 7×AGA→1 cluster; deviations None.
- [[codon-usage-comparison]] — codon-usage family's *raw* end (`CalculateCodonUsage` + `CompareCodonUsage`): unnormalized codon-count table (non-overlapping triplets, T→U, drop partial codon, Dictionary<codon,int>, Σcounts=total invariant) + Total Variation Distance similarity `1−Σ|f₁−f₂|/2 ∈ [0,1]` between two codon-frequency distributions; proven identity 1.0 / symmetry / range [0,1] / disjoint→0 / partial-overlap-exact properties; empty→0, TVD-not-cosine deliberate metric choice; Kazusa-verified organism tables; shares RSCU's counting primitive, the distribution-comparison op none of the bias measures provide.
- [[codon-optimization]] — codon-usage family's CDS-*rewriting* operation (`OptimizeSequence`): synonymous substitution to improve host expression; five strategies (MaximizeCAI / BalancedOptimization 40-60% GC / HarmonizeExpression=Mignon 2018 / AvoidRareCodons / MinimizeSecondary→ReduceSecondaryStructure); invariants protein-preservation + Met/AUG & Trp/UGG fixed + stop preserved + CAI∈(0,1]; RNA notation, T→U, trim-to-codon, 1e-6 CAI clamp; E. coli/yeast/human preferred-codon fixtures; actuator to RSCU/CAI/ENC's measurement.
- [[effective-number-of-codons]] — ENC/Nc (Wright 1990) reference-free whole-gene codon-bias measure in [20,61]: reciprocal of codon homozygosity F̂=(n·Σp²−1)/(n−1) aggregated by degeneracy class (Nc=2+9/F̂₂+1/F̂₃+5/F̂₄+3/F̂₆); 20=max bias / 61=uniform, unbiased→61, no-bias-sim→40.5; Ile absent→(F̂₂+F̂₄)/2 fallback, overshoot re-adjusts to 61; reference-free counterpart of CAI; one assumption = non-source-prescribed lower clamp at 20.
- [[repetitive-element-detection]] — repeats/tandem family anchor: tandem (head-to-tail, ≥2 copies, primitive unit), inverted (W·G·W̄ᴿ / zero-gap palindrome, IUPACpal), and RepeatMasker-class assignment; ClassifyRepeat = exact-substring containment, not Smith-Waterman homology.
- [[consensus-sequence]] — assembly CONSENSUS family anchor: column-wise majority/threshold consensus (Biopython dumb_consensus rule) — gaps skipped, emit iff unique max and freq ≥ threshold else ambiguous, tie→ambiguous, all-gap→N no div-by-zero; N/0.5 parameterized defaults; shared with MSA consensus step.
- [[consensus-from-alignment]] — Motif-Analysis consensus-from-a-multiple-alignment (MOTIF-CONS-001, `MotifFinder.CreateConsensusFromAlignment`): pure most-frequent (plurality) column consensus over equal-length aligned strings, deterministic alphabetical tie-break (A<C<G<T), no threshold (always emits); Rosalind CONS `ATGCAACT` oracle; `alternative_to` the threshold/tie→ambiguous assembly [[consensus-sequence]], motif-family sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]].
- [[iupac-degenerate-consensus]] — MotifFinder degenerate-consensus unit (MOTIF-GENERATE-001, `MotifFinder.GenerateConsensus`): collapses equal-length aligned columns into an IUPAC-ambiguity-coded string — per column keep every base with `count > 0.25·n` (strict `>`), emit the NC-IUB 1984 symbol for that base set (R/Y/S/W/K/M, B/D/H/V, N), no-pass fallback → most-frequent (alphabetical tie); DECIPHER threshold-consensus family + NC-IUB/UCSC/Wikipedia bijective set→symbol table; `A,A,G,G,C`→R / strict-`>` boundary / four-way→A-fallback oracles; `alternative_to` the plurality [[consensus-from-alignment]], degenerate sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]] and de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]].
- [[regulatory-element-detection]] — Motif-Discovery regulatory-element unit (MOTIF-REGULATORY-001, `KnownMotifs` catalog scan): matches a **fixed, cited catalog of 12 canonical regulatory consensus elements** (TATA/−10/−35/CAAT/GC promoter boxes, Kozak + Shine-Dalgarno translation signals, poly(A), and E-box/AP-1/NF-κB/CREB TF sites) against a DNA sequence, reporting each occurrence's Name/Pattern/Sequence at its 0-based start; mixes exact and one IUPAC-degenerate (E-box `CANNTG`) match; anchors the AP-1 corrected-consensus regression (`TGAGTCA`→`TGACTCA`, `AATGAGTCAGG`→0 hits); two source-backed representative-site assumptions (NF-κB `GGGACTTTCC`, Kozak `GCCGCCACCATGG`); the curated-biological-catalog specialization of the generic exact [[known-motif-search]], distinct from the generation-direction [[iupac-degenerate-consensus]] and de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]].
- [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]] — Motif-Discovery de-novo unit (MOTIF-DISCOVER-001, `MotifFinder.DiscoverMotifs`): finds **unknown** over-represented motifs by enumerating every length-`k` k-mer, counting overlapping occurrences, and ranking by observed/expected enrichment `Count/((N−k+1)/4^k)` under a zero-order i.i.d. uniform background (Compeau & Pevzner); deterministic exact single-pass, 0-based positions; `ATGC` in `ATGCATGCATGC` k=4 → 768/9≈85.333, `AAA` in `AAAAAAAAAA` k=3 → 64.0 oracles; `k>N`→empty, minCount presentation-only, zero-order-only + no-p-value simplifications; the de-novo inverse of the exact [[known-motif-search]] and distinct from the [[consensus-from-alignment]] plurality consensus.
- [[shared-motifs]] — Motif-Discovery cross-sequence unit (MOTIF-SHARED-001, `FindSharedMotifs`): the van Helden / RSAT oligo-analysis **"matching sequences"** quorum — enumerate every fixed-`k` exact word across a *set* of sequences and report each word present in ≥ `minSequences` of them (each carrying its `SequenceIndices` set + `Prevalence`=matching/total); a within-sequence repeat counts **1** (presence/absence, not multiplicity); exact-word only (no degenerate/substitution); the cross-sequence sibling of the single-sequence O/E [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]] and `alternative_to` the fixed-k-quorum-vs-single-longest LCSM framing of [[longest-common-substring]] (returns all qualifying words, not one longest present in all).
- [[approximate-pattern-matching-mismatches]] — pattern-matching PAT-APPROX family anchor (PAT-APPROX-003): Hamming-distance **approximate matching** — a `k`-mer appears with ≤`d` mismatches when `HammingDistance(P,P')≤d` (BA1H); `Count_d`/`FindApproximateOccurrences` scan windows, `FindFrequentKmersWithMismatches` (BA1I) ranks `k`-mers by their **d-neighborhood** (Hamming-ball) tally so the winner need not occur exactly, `Neighbors` (BA1N) enumerates the ball (includes identity), `FindBestMatch` returns the leftmost min-Hamming window; oracles {GATG,ATGC,ATGT} count 5, {6,7,26,27,78}, Count_1=4, ACG/1→10; d=0 degenerates to exact so it is the mismatch-tolerant `alternative_to` [[k-mer-positions]] and the fuzzy sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]] / de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]]; substitution-only (no indels — that is the alignment family), deviations none.
- [[coverage-depth-calculation]] — assembly COVER family anchor: per-base sequencing depth over a reference (count of placed reads spanning each position, exact); average depth = Σdepth/G = Lander-Waterman C=LN/G, breadth = covered/G = 1−e^−c; boundary-clip + empty-input rules; ACGTTGCAAT→1.5/1.0 oracle; Poisson (e^−c gap) as a property check only; read placement (minOverlap best-match) out of scope.
- [[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]] — assembly DBG family anchor: k-mer graph (distinct (k-1)-mers = nodes, each k-mer = one prefix→suffix edge, directed multigraph) + Eulerian-walk reconstruction (balanced/semi-balanced, Euler theorems 8.1/8.2, O(|E|) Hierholzer); spelling = path[0]+last char of each node; unique-walk oracles only (AAABBBA, a_long…, to_every… k=4, ATGGCGTGCA); repeat/gap/error → non-Eulerian; walk-selection unspecified so exact asserts on unique-walk inputs; OLC is the alternative formulation.
- [[overlap-layout-consensus-assembly]] — assembly OLC family anchor: the three-stage Overlap-Layout-Consensus paradigm (`FindAllOverlaps` + `AssembleOLC`) — overlap graph (read=node, edge on longest suffix-of-A/prefix-of-B ≥ threshold), Layout = Hamiltonian path (NP-complete) + transitive reduction + non-branching contigs, Consensus = majority vote; GTACGTACGAT 12-edge / 5-overlap-tiling oracles; suffix-tree O(N+a) vs all-pairs O(N²); NP-complete/repeat-split/greedy-suboptimal failure modes; identity-1.0 + empty-input assumptions; Hamiltonian/overlap-graph alternative to DBG's Eulerian/k-mer formulation.
- [[contig-merge-overlap-collapse]] — assembly MERGE family anchor: suffix–prefix overlap collapse primitive (`MergeContigs`) behind greedy SCS and OLC layout; overlap = length-l suffix of X = prefix of Y, longest match reported, collapse keeps one copy so |merge|=|c1|+|c2|−l; overlap 0 / out-of-range → plain concatenation; BAA+AAB→BAAB, chain→AAABBBA oracles; caller-trusts-length + out-of-range→concat API-contract assumptions; overlap-based sibling of DBG's k-mer/Eulerian formulation.
- [[scaffolding]] — assembly SCAFFOLD family anchor: joining ordered contigs into a scaffold, adjacent contigs separated by `N`-runs of length = the (upstream) inter-contig distance estimate (ABySS 2.0 rule); positive gap `g` → `g`×`N`, scaffold length = Σ|contig|+Σgap; non-positive (zero/negative) estimate → AGP unknown-size default 100 N (negative = overlap, unresolved here); each contig in ≤1 scaffold, unlinked → singleton; parameterized fill char; ACGTNNNTTGGNNCCAA / AAAA+100N+TTTT oracles; downstream of DBG/OLC/merge, hands off to contig-merge on the negative-gap overlap case; 100-constant source-backed (INSDC), only the fall-back-not-resolve decision is assumed.
- [[assembly-statistics]] — assembly STATS family anchor: contiguity/QC summary metrics over contig lengths (read-only, downstream of DBG/OLC/merge/scaffold) — Nx = shortest length covering ≥x% (largest-first, inclusive ≥; N50/N90), Lx = the matching contig count, N90 ≤ N50 / L90 ≥ L50, auN = ΣLᵢ²/ΣLⱼ (area under Nx curve, more stable than N50); + totals/largest/smallest/GC and 0-based inclusive N-run gaps; Miller 2010 + Wikipedia + QUAST + Heng Li 2020; Assembly A N50 70/L50 2, auN 73.333 oracles; empty→zeros (not None) + upper-median-not-source-derived assumptions.
- [[quality-trimming-running-sum]] — assembly TRIM family anchor: BWA/cutadapt running-sum quality trimming — subtract cutoff from each Phred quality, take partial sums to the 3' end, cut at the minimum (= BWA argmax of accumulated threshold−q, with `s<0` early break + `BWA_MIN_RDLEN=35` floor); Phred+33 decode (Cock 2010); `KI;<)(,%#$`@thr 10→first 4 bases oracle; threshold<1 disables / all-high unchanged / all-low dropped / good-base-among-bad refinement; both-end pass + downstream minLength filter as assumptions; read-QC preprocessing upstream of correction/DBG/OLC.
- [[kmer-spectrum-error-correction]] — assembly CORRECT family anchor: two-sided k-mer-spectrum read error correction (Musket/Quake) — trusted (multiplicity > cut-off) vs untrusted k-mers, base trusted if covered by any trusted k-mer, unique alternative making all covering k-mers trusted, ambiguity/no-set→unchanged; substitution-only (count+length preserved); kmerSize=15/minKmerFrequency=2 non-behavioral defaults.
- [[centromere-analysis]] — chromosome centromere/alpha-satellite family anchor (second Chromosome-analysis unit): `AnalyzeCentromere` + 4 additive detectors — Levan 1964 q/p arm-ratio classes (Metacentric ≤1.7 / Submetacentric ≤3.0 / Subtelocentric <7.0 / Acrocentric ≥7.0 / Telocentric p=0); alpha-satellite-specific `DetectAlphaSatellite`/`FindCenpBBoxes` (171-bp tandem period ±5, AT>0.5, 17-bp CENP-B box `YTTCGTTGGAARCGGGA`, no embedded monomer); `DetectHigherOrderRepeat` (HOR period = smallest k with monomers k apart ≥95% identical across ≥90%, intra-HOR 50–70% vs inter-HOR 97–100%); `AssignSuprachromosomalFamily` (bundled CC0 Dfam ALR/ALRa=A/ALRb=B, SF3 pentameric/SF4 monomeric/{SF1,SF2} dimeric/SF5 irregular); base AlphaSatelliteContent is density-heuristic-not-specific + SF1/SF2-unresolved (non-redistributable consensus library) limitations.
- [[karyotype-analysis]] — chromosome karyotyping/ploidy-detection family anchor (third Chromosome-analysis unit): `AnalyzeKaryotype` builds a karyotype from chromosome descriptors (split sex/autosome, group by base name, count copies, compare to expected ploidy, label nullisomy..pentasomy by absolute count; TotalChromosomes/TotalGenomeSize/MeanChromosomeLength invariants) and `DetectPloidy` estimates whole-genome ploidy from read depth (true-median ratio → round(ratio×2) clamped [1,8], confidence 1−|ratio×2−ploidy|×2, empty→(2,0)); Down/Turner + diploid/tetraploid/haploid oracles; DD4 nullisomy-unreachable-via-GroupBy, DD5 disomy-only-aneuploid-in-polyploid; deviations None. Descriptor-count sibling of depth-log-ratio [[aneuploidy-detection]].
- [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] — shared synteny anchor (fourth Chromosome-analysis unit; comparative-genomics COMPGEN-SYNTENY will reuse it): `FindSyntenyBlocks` builds syntenic blocks from ortholog pairs (group by chr pair, sort by ref position, collinear runs merged under maxGap, emit ≥minGenes; block carries strand '+'/'-', GeneCount, SequenceIdentity=NaN for coordinate-only input per MCScanX; I1–I5) + `DetectRearrangements` classifies adjacent-block signals (diff target chr→Translocation, same chr diff strand→Inversion, gap asymmetry→Deletion, overlapping source diff targets→Duplication); forward/inverted-block + translocation(50000)/inversion(size 10000) oracles; empty/below-minGenes/maxGap-split/multi-pair edge cases; MCScanX/SyRI/MUMmer + Wikipedia; deviations None.
- [[telomere-analysis]] — chromosome telomere family anchor (fifth Chromosome-analysis unit): telomere repeat detection + length estimation — 3′ end forward TTAGGG / 5′ end reverse-complement CCCTAA (6-bp vertebrate unit, Meyne 1989), configurable 70%-per-window purity so imperfect repeats accepted (5/6 for 6-bp, 5/7 for Arabidopsis TTTAGGG; divergent TTAGGA→0.833), purity∈[0,1] tracked with length; length direct from run or qPCR T/S ratio (Cawthon 2002) EstimatedLength=referenceLength×(tsRatio/referenceRatio); IsCriticallyShort=(hasTelomere&&length<criticalLength)OR empty; criticalLength 3000 / minTelomereLength 500 / searchLength(truncates) / referenceLength 7000 configurable defaults not biological constants; Wikipedia/Meyne/Cawthon/Blackburn-Gall sources; deviations None. Sibling of [[aneuploidy-detection]].
- [[conserved-gene-clusters-common-intervals]] — comparative-genomics common-interval / conserved-cluster unit: a conserved gene cluster = a gene-label SET contiguous in EVERY genome (order- and strand-free inside the window), the common-interval model (Uno & Yagiura 2000, Heber & Stoye 2001 k-permutation O(kn+z), Bui-Xuan/Habib/Paul 2013 unifying view, Didier et al. 2013 sequences-with-duplicates/paralogs); interval size ≥2 (singletons excluded), whole set (1..n) trivially common, meaningful only for K≥2; Seqeron does the strict O(n²·K) check with minClusterSize filter; strict gap-free model — maxGap retained for API/MCP back-compat only and does NOT relax it, gene-teams gapped extension (Bergeron 2002) not implemented; golden vector Id₇ vs (7 2 1 3 6 4 5) → {1,2}/{1,2,3}/{3,4,5,6}/{4,5}/{4,5,6}/{1..6} + trivial {1..7}, split-negative {2,3}, duplicates T/S → {1,2,3,4}; order-free sibling of [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] and [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; deviations None.
- [[average-nucleotide-identity]] — comparative-genomics ANI family anchor (first COMPGEN unit): the ANIb genome-similarity metric (Goris 2007) that operationalizes the prokaryotic species boundary (ANI≈95%↔70% DDH) — fragment query into 1020 nt pieces, best-match place each against the reference (`CalculateAni`), keep fragments >30% identity over ≥70% alignable (both recalculated over the query-fragment length), average the qualifying per-fragment identities; gapped Smith-Waterman placement recovers indels (`gapped:true`), reciprocal/symmetric ANI = mean of both directions (`CalculateReciprocalAni`, order-independent); null/empty→0, non-positive fragmentLength throws; engine decision = SequenceAligner.LocalAlign (full DP, BLAST DNA scoring) not NCBI-BLASTN, indel handling correct; sibling of [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] in the COMPGEN family; deviations None.
- [[dot-plot-word-match]] — comparative-genomics visual pairwise-comparison unit (`COMPGEN-DOTPLOT-001`): the word-match / k-tuple dot matrix (Gibbs & McIntyre 1970 → EMBOSS `dottup`) — dot at (x,y) iff the length-`wordSize` word at x in seq1 exactly matches the word at y in seq2 (case-insensitive, x=seq1/y=seq2, all overlapping occurrences via suffix tree), diagonals = similarity / main diagonal = self-comparison / repeats = extra diagonals / indels break the diagonal; `wordSize` (EMBOSS default 10) noise-vs-sensitivity trade-off (longer=less noise/less sensitive), `stepSize` x-subsampling; exact-match `dottup` not scored `dotmatcher`; AGCGT/AT k=1→{(0,0),(4,1)}, ACGTACGT self wordSize4→{(0,0),(0,4),(1,1),(2,2),(3,3),(4,0),(4,4)}, ACGT self main-diagonal oracles; word>seq/null/empty/disjoint→no dots, non-positive wordSize/stepSize throws; sibling of ANI/synteny/conserved-clusters; orientation + case-insensitivity assumptions, deviations None.
- [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] — comparative-genomics ortholog & in-paralog detection unit (`COMPGEN-ORTHO-001`): orthologs by Reciprocal Best Hits (RBH — each gene the other's best hit across two genomes, Moreno-Hagelsieb 2008 / Tatusov 1997 / Fitch 1970 speciation-vs-duplication), recent (in-)paralogs by within-genome mutual best hits (Remm 2001); best hit=max-similarity with deterministic tie-break, reciprocity mandatory (one-directional best hit is NOT an ortholog = the guarded defect), ≥50% coverage + min-similarity gates, partial-matching output, empty→no orthologs / single-gene→no paralogs; reciprocity/non-reciprocity(RBH count 1)/in-paralog oracles; one assumption = alignment-free 5-mer Jaccard replaces BLAST bit-score ranking (reciprocity/coverage/threshold source-backed); shared anchor for COMPGEN-RBH-001, the core/shared-gene sub-unit of [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]]; sibling of ANI/synteny/conserved-clusters/dot-plot; deviations None.
