- [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]] — comparative-genomics signed-permutation / breakpoint rearrangement-detection unit (`COMPGEN-REARR-001` + `COMPGEN-REVERSAL-001`): the Hannenhalli–Pevzner/Bafna–Pevzner theory — signed permutation (strand=sign), extended `(0,…,n+1)` (endpoints=telomeres), breakpoint = consecutive pair where neither `(x,y)` nor `(−y,−x)` survives in β, `b(α)` count = `d_BP=n−sim(common adjacencies)`, reversal-distance lower bound `d≥b/2`; `ClassifyRearrangement` → Inversion (reversal = sign-flip + local reverse) vs Transposition (block move preserving orientation), Translocation/Deletion/Insertion/Duplication "Not implemented" (single permutation can't express them); Hunter `(−2,−3,+1,+6,−5,−4)`→b=6/d≥3, identity→0, single-inversion `(+1,−4,−3,−2,+5)`→b=2 oracles; `b∈[0,n+1]` invariant; the signed-permutation `alternative_to` the block-signal [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]], sibling of ANI/ortholog/clusters/dot-plot; deviations None.
- [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]] — comparative-genomics end-to-end pipeline (`CompareGenomes`): partitions each genome's genes into core (conserved = RBH ortholog pairs, Tettelin 2005 pan-genome) vs dispensable (genome-specific = the rest), reports Conserved/Specific1/Specific2 + OverallSynteny=(genes in MCScanX syntenic blocks)/min(|g1|,|g2|) clamped ≤1; symmetric partition, empty→all-0; orchestrates RBH ortholog detection (COMPGEN-RBH-001) + synteny (COMPGEN-SYNTENY-001); sibling of [[average-nucleotide-identity]] & [[conserved-gene-clusters-common-intervals]]; two source-backed assumptions (alignment-free RBH gate, MCScanX ≥5-anchor block threshold → OverallSynteny can be 0 with conserved orthologs); deviations None.
- [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]] — protein-disorder family MoRF unit (DISORDER-MORF-001, second DISORDER-* unit): Molecular Recognition Feature prediction by the "dip within disorder" heuristic (Oldfield 2005 / Cheng-Oldfield PMC2570644 / Mohan 2006) — a short ordered run (per-residue TOP-IDP disorder score <0.5) of total length 10–70 flanked on both sides by disorder (score ≥0.5) = one MoRF; 0.5 order/disorder threshold, α/β/ι bound-state sub-types (Mohan 2006), MoRF score∈[0,1] rising with dip depth; terminal dip / fully-ordered / fully-disordered / out-of-band → none; TOP-IDP normalized `(raw+0.884)/1.871` per-residue score from `PredictDisorder`; one assumption = exact flank-length params paywalled → qualitative criterion (threshold/band/shape source-traceable); distinct sibling of [[protein-low-complexity-seg]]; deviations None.
- [[protein-low-complexity-seg]] — protein disorder / features family anchor (first DISORDER-* unit, DISORDER-LC-001): the SEG algorithm (Wootton & Federhen 1993/1996) partitioning a protein into low-/high-complexity segments; complexity = Shannon entropy `H=−Σpᵢlog₂pᵢ` bits/residue (max log₂20≈4.322), two-stage scan with W=12 trigger window / K1=2.2 trigger cutoff / K2=2.5 extension cutoff (NCBI `blast_seg.c` defaults); homopolymer H=0 triggers, 12-distinct H≈3.585>K2 no segment; X-rich/X-Y-rich label + greedy single-residue extension are flagged repository extensions not moving boundaries; distinct from [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp|intrinsic-disorder prediction]] (TOP-IDP) and the genomic-DNA [[repetitive-element-detection]] low-complexity counterpart.
- [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]] — protein-disorder family shared anchor (DISORDER-PRED-001 + DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001 + DISORDER-REGION-001): the TOP-IDP `PredictDisorder` sliding-window intrinsic-disorder predictor (Campen 2008) that [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]] + disordered-region detection sit on; also hosts the region-detection layer (contiguous runs ≥ minRegionLength, default RegionType classification proline-rich/acidic/basic/Ser-Thr-rich > 0.25 + Long/Standard IDR, opt-in MobiDB-lite flavor scheme); per-residue Sᵢ=mean over window of min-max-normalized TOP-IDP `(p−(−0.884))/1.871 ∈ [0,1]`, disordered when Sᵢ≥0.542 (max-likelihood cutoff), default window 21 (edge-clipped) / minRegionLength 5; Dunker 2001 disorder{A,R,G,Q,S,P,E,K}/order{W,C,F,I,Y,V,L,N}/ambiguous{D,H,M,T} sets + Kyte-Doolittle `CalculateHydropathy`; W30→0.0/P30→1.0/E30→0.866 oracles, null/empty→empty, non-canonical skipped (all-unknown window→0.0), case-insensitive, O(n·w); also anchors the raw per-residue propensity primitives (DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001: `GetDisorderPropensity` returns the RAW un-normalized Table-2 value, unknown→0.0, + the two public Dunker sets); assumptions None (params source-traced), impl = simplified single-feature heuristic not competitive with IUPred2A/MobiDB-lite; distinct sibling of [[protein-low-complexity-seg]].
- [[coiled-coil-prediction]] — ProteinMotif family anchor (first ingested unit, PROTMOTIF-CC-001): the heptad a/d hydrophobic-core occupancy coiled-coil predictor `ProteinMotifFinder.PredictCoiledCoils` — for each window `score = (#a/d positions with residue ∈ {I,L,V})/(#a/d positions)` maximised over the 7 heptad registers (`p(k,r)=(k−r) mod 7`, core a=0/d=3), contiguous windows with score ≥ threshold mapped to residue regions ≥21 residues (3 heptads) with peak `Score∈[0,1]`; defaults window 28 (4 heptads, Lupas 1991) / threshold 0.5 / min-region 21 (Mason & Arndt ≥3-heptad); INV-01..05 (score∈[0,1]; region≥21; len<window→empty; off-frame found via 7-register max); (LAALAAA)×5→(0,34,1.0) / no-{I,L,V}→none / (LAAAAAA)→0.5 boundary oracles; COILS 21×20 PSSM deliberately omitted (weights not retrievable, use COILS/Paircoil2 for P-scores) + {I,L,V}-only core-set assumption (source-verbatim); sequence-only heuristic, distinct from the ProteinPred disorder/features family ([[protein-low-complexity-seg]], [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]], [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]]).
- [[common-protein-motifs]] — ProteinMotif family second unit (PROTMOTIF-COMMON-001, `ProteinMotifFinder.FindCommonMotifs`): scans an amino-acid sequence against a fixed built-in `CommonMotifs` dictionary of canonical PROSITE patterns and aggregates every hit carrying its accession/name — PS00001 `ASN_GLYCOSYLATION` `N-{P}-[ST]-{P}`, PS00005 `PKC_PHOSPHO_SITE` `[ST]-x-[RK]`, PS00006 `CK2_PHOSPHO_SITE` `[ST]-x(2)-[DE]`, PS00016 `RGD` `R-G-D`, PS00017 `ATP_GTP_A` `[AG]-x(4)-G-K-[ST]`; PROSITE syntax (`x` wildcard, `[ ]` allowed set, `{ }` excluded set, `x(n)`/`x(m,n)` repetition); 0-based-inclusive `MotifMatch.Start`/`End` (PROSITE reports 1-based) + substring invariant + overlaps-all-reported (ScanProsite "overlaps, no includes"); `NFTA`/Pro-exclusion-no-match/`SAR`/`SAAE`+`SDED`/`GXXXXGKS`/`RGD`+`RGD`-overlap oracles; one API-shape assumption (0- vs 1-based origin, no correctness effect); the **protein** fixed-catalog analogue of the DNA [[regulatory-element-detection]], sibling of the windowed [[coiled-coil-prediction]], distinct from the caller-supplied-set DNA exact [[known-motif-search]].
- [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] — ProteinMotif family third unit (PROTMOTIF-DOMAIN-001): protein **domain** prediction + **signal-peptide** prediction. `ProteinMotifFinder.FindDomains` scans PROSITE **domain patterns** (PS00028 C2H2 zinc finger/PF00096, PS00017 P-loop/PF00069, PS00678 WD40 15-residue/PF00400; ScanProsite→regex), 0-based inclusive hits, tandem repeats all detected — SH3/PDZ excluded (PROSITE **PROFILEs**, no deterministic pattern). Opt-in `FindDomainsByHmm`/`Plan7ProfileHmm` reproduces the **HMMER3** engine over 3 bundled CC0 Pfam HMMs (SH3/PDZ/WD40): Viterbi/Forward log-odds (exact 1e-9 hand-HMM), local-multihit `pre_score` vs Swiss-Prot `bg->f` (~1e-5-bit hmmsearch parity), null2 bias (omega 1/256), Gumbel/exponential E-values (`E=P·Z`), `p7_domaindef` multi-domain envelope decomposition (GBB1/PF00400→7 blades exact) + stochastic-traceback clustering for overlapping tandems (fixed-seed Easel LCG 42), verified vs pyhmmer 0.12.1. `PredictSignalPeptide` = von Heijne tripartite n(K/R+)/h(hydrophobic α-helix)/c(polar) + −1,−3 rule {A,G,S}, score (n+2h+c)/4 with evidence-based constraints (nScore>0, hScore≥0.5) and Probability=Score. Six resolved design decisions; MSV/bias prefilters + exact-RNG-bit parity + full-Pfam coverage out of scope (research-grade). Sibling of [[coiled-coil-prediction]] & [[common-protein-motifs]].
- [[protein-motif-pattern-search]] — ProteinMotif family general engine (PROTMOTIF-FIND-001, `ProteinMotifFinder.FindMotifByPattern`): the **general, arbitrary caller-supplied** PROSITE-pattern protein motif finder underneath the fixed-dictionary [[common-protein-motifs]]. Three primitives — `ConvertPrositeToRegex` (PROSITE→regex: `x`→`.`, `[ABC]`→`[ABC]`, `{ABC}`→`[^ABC]`, `x(n)`→`.{n}`, `x(n,m)`→`.{n,m}`, `<`→`^`, `>`→`$`); `FindMotifByPattern` (all matches incl. overlaps via zero-width lookahead `(?=(pattern))` per ScanProsite, 0-based `MotifMatch.Start`/`End`, case-insensitive, empty/null→empty, invalid regex handled gracefully); and information-content scoring `CalculateMotifScore` IC=Σlog₂(20/allowed_count) over constrained positions (`x`=0 bits, fixed≈4.32 bits) + `CalculateEValue` E=(N−L+1)·2^(−IC), Schneider & Stephens 1990 (NOT BLAST statistics — that citation was removed). Pins the PROSITE-pattern catalog (PS00001/00004–00009/00016–00018/00028 C2H2/00029 leucine-zipper) and fixed two impl bugs (PS00007 exact repeat counts; PS00018 EF-hand `{W}`+trailing `[LIVMFYW]`); five non-PROSITE linear motifs literature-verified (NLS1/NES1/SIM1/WW1/SH3_1); SKIP-FLAG=TRUE common sites noted. Sibling of the fixed-catalog [[common-protein-motifs]], windowed [[coiled-coil-prediction]], and longer-signature [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]]; all assumptions eliminated (0-vs-1-based coordinate convention only).
- [[aneuploidy-detection]] — chromosome copy-number/ploidy family anchor (first Chromosome-analysis unit): abnormal chromosome count from read depth — per-bin CN=round(2^log2(depth/median)×2) clamped [0,10], whole-chromosome call needs dominant CN across ≥80% of bins (mosaicism tolerance), confidence=1−min(1,|CN/2−2^logRatio|)=1.0 at integer-CN ratios; nullisomy..pentasomy terminology; Down/Edwards/Patau/Turner/Klinefelter oracles; sex-chromosomes-not-special-cased + partial-aneuploidy-needs-80%-bins limitations.
- [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] — epigenetics family bisulfite-sequencing unit (second EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-BISULF-001): base-level DNA-methylation calling from sodium-bisulfite reads — distinct from the age clock (it *produces* the β-values a clock consumes). Three deterministic ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: (1) `SimulateBisulfiteConversion` — single-strand per-base Frommer 1992 rule (unprotected C→T, protected 5mC stays C, non-C unchanged, case preserved, ACGTCGAA{1}→ACGTTGAA); (2) `CalculateMethylationFromBisulfite` — reuses `FindCpGSites`, Bismark C=methylated/T=unmethylated tally, level = meth/(meth+unmeth)∈[0,1], zero-coverage sites excluded (ACGTACGT reads→0.5&0.0); (3) `GenerateMethylationProfile` — Schultz 2012 per-context weighted level Σ(level·coverage)/Σcoverage (0.25≠unweighted 0.5), zero-total-coverage falls back to unweighted mean; CpG needs C+G, neither-C-nor-T call ignored, past-reference ignored; research-grade, no CHG/CHH calling / no complement merge / no non-conversion-rate correction; sibling of [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]; deviations None.
- [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]] — epigenetics family anchor (first EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-AGE-001): DNAm ("epigenetic") age from methylation β-values via the Horvath 2013 multi-tissue clock — two-stage model, linear predictor `Y = intercept + Σ coef_i·β_i` over 353 elastic-net-selected clock CpGs (transformed-age units), then the two-branch inverse calibration `anti.trafo` (adult.age=20): `21·exp(Y)−1` for Y<0 (exponential), `21·Y+20` for Y≥0 (linear), continuous at (0,20)=age 20; embedded intercept 0.695507258 + 353 `CoefficientTraining` weights cross-verified byte-identical; invariants Y=0→20 / CpGs-absent-ignored / empty-map→F⁻¹(intercept); null→ArgumentNullException, empty coefficients→ArgumentException; anti.trafo oracles (0→20, 1→41, −1→6.7254682646, −2.5→0.7237849711) + Y=0.684247258→34.369192418; scope = multi-tissue only (algorithm doc later extends to Horvath-2018 skin&blood 391-CpG + Levine-2018 PhenoAge 513-CpG no-transform); no BMIQ input normalisation (research-grade); sibling [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] (produces the β-values); third Epigenetics sibling [[chromatin-state-prediction]] (histone-mark axis).
- [[cpg-island-detection]] — epigenetics family CpG site & island unit (fourth EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-CPG-001): sequence-only CpG dinucleotide detection (no methylation state — distinct from all siblings). Three ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: `FindCpGSites` (linear scan, 0-based C position, `CGCG`→2 sites, reused by [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]); `CalculateCpGObservedExpected` (Gardiner-Garden O/E=CpG/((C·G)/L), div-by-zero guard→0, oracles CGCG× 2.0/ACGTCGACG 3.0/ACGT 4.0/AT-only 0); `FindCpGIslands` (sliding-window merge, default ≥200bp/GC≥0.5/O-E≥0.6 inclusive, 0-based inclusive-Start/exclusive-End tuple, 400bp CGCG→1 island, O(n·w)); GpC≠CpG, case-insensitive; Takai-Jones 2002 stricter (≥500/55%/0.65) + Saxonov 2006 alt-expected not preset (custom args); Gardiner-Garden & Frommer 1987 + Takai-Jones + Saxonov + Wikipedia; assumptions None. Siblings [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]/[[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]/[[chromatin-state-prediction]].
- [[chromatin-state-prediction]] — epigenetics family chromatin-state / histone-mark unit (third EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-CHROM-001): ChromHMM-style (Ernst & Kellis 2012) annotation of a locus from the *combination of present histone marks* — distinct from the methylation siblings (operates on histone ChIP-seq signals, not DNA methylation). Binary present/absent mark model (ChromHMM binarizes then learns; state = function of the SET of present marks, magnitude beyond the call irrelevant = binary invariance); `PredictChromatinState` takes the six Roadmap 18-state marks {H3K4me3, H3K4me1, H3K27ac, H3K36me3, H3K27me3, H3K9me3} as [0,1] signals, calls present > threshold (default 0.5), maps pattern → ActivePromoter(TssA, H3K4me3±H3K27ac)/ActiveEnhancer(H3K4me1+H3K27ac)/WeakEnhancer(H3K4me1 no H3K27ac)/Transcribed(Tx, H3K36me3)/Repressed(ReprPC, H3K27me3)/Heterochromatin(Het, H3K9me3)/BivalentPromoter(TssBiv, H3K4me3+H3K27me3)/BivalentEnhancer(EnhBiv, H3K4me1+H3K27me3)/LowSignal(Quies, none); two combinatorial rules — bivalency is a state not a contradiction, promoter(H3K4me3) dominates enhancer(H3K4me1); companions `AnnotateHistoneModifications` (per-mark region label) + `FindAccessibleRegions` (ATAC-like contiguous-merge + minWidth); research-grade — state-assignment logic source-backed, NOT a trained HMM (no LearnModel/Poisson binarization/spatial context); two assumptions (0.5 threshold, single-locus precedence); sibling of [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]] & [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]; no contradictions.
- [[differentially-methylated-regions]] — epigenetics family DMR-detection unit (fifth EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-DMR-001): methylKit (Akalin 2012) two-sample tiling-window + Fisher's-exact-test model — *compares* methylation between two samples (distinct from the single-sample siblings), consuming the per-CpG C/(C+T) β-values [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] produces over the CpGs [[cpg-island-detection]] locates. Fixed tiles (`win.size=1000/step.size=1000/cov.bases=0`, `tileMethylCounts`), meth.diff=group2%−group1% (percentage points), per-window pooled 2×2 methylated/unmethylated counts → Fisher's exact (one sample per group; replicates→logistic regression out of scope), hypergeometric single-table p `(a+b)!(c+d)!(a+c)!(b+d)!/(a!b!c!d!n!)` + two-sided ≤-observed sum; report q<0.01 AND |meth.diff|>25 strict (`getMethylDiff`): hyper meth.diff>+25 / hypo <−25; empty→no DMRs, zero-coverage group / zero marginal→p=1.0, |meth.diff|=25→excluded; oracles Fisher a=1/b=9/c=11/d=3→≈0.001346076, hyper window g1=0.0/g2=1.0→+100/p≈0; two evidence-backed assumptions (per-window pooling, numC/numT=round(level×coverage)); research-grade (no logistic path/SLIM/overlapping tiles); siblings [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]/[[chromatin-state-prediction]]; no contradictions.
- [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]] — Analysis alignment-free pairwise-similarity unit (`GENOMIC-SIMILARITY-001`, `GenomicAnalyzer.CalculateSimilarity`): Jaccard index of the two sequences' distinct k-mer sets (Jaccard 1901 `|A∩B|/|A∪B|` over HashSet k-mer sets, Ondov 2016 *Mash* fraction-of-shared-k-mers), exact (no MinHash sketch) J×100 in `[0,100]`, O(n+m); INV symmetry / identical→100 / disjoint→0 / distinct-set (repeats once); default k=5, empty-union→0 (ASM-1 convention), ×100 scaling; k=3 oracles 80/(100/3)/100/0; `alternative_to` positional [[alignment-statistics]], the 5-mer-Jaccard metric behind [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] and the exact-set basis Mash sketches for [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; limitations = exact-match/composition-only; deviations None.
- [[k-mer-euclidean-distance]] — K-mer family alignment-free word-frequency **distance** unit (`KMER-DIST-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.KmerDistance`): Euclidean (L2) distance between two sequences' normalized k-mer **frequency** vectors `f_s(w)=count/(L−k+1)` over the union of observed k-mers (absent word→0 component), exact/O(n+m); Zielezinski 2017 word-vector model + Lau 2022 frequency normalization + Vinga-Almeida 2003 4^k-vector + Boden 2014 relative-frequency Euclidean; INV d(x,x)=0 / symmetric / ≥0 / disjoint-single-kmer→√2; √0.11≈0.3316624790 (ATGTGTG/CATGTG k=3) + √0.125 (AAAA/AAAT k=1) oracles; case-insensitive (ASM-01) + empty/L<k→zero-vector (ASM-02); count-based/Manhattan/Canberra/Chebyshev/cosine/D2/spaced-word not implemented, deviations None; `alternative_to` the presence/absence [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]] (this captures abundance), shares the `CountKmers` primitive with [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-dist-001-evidence]].
- [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]] — K-mer family async count unit (`KMER-ASYNC-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.CountKmersAsync`): the cooperatively cancelable, progress-reporting thread-pool wrapper over synchronous `CountKmers` — numeric result identical to the sync reference (counts fixed by the k-mer formula `L − k + 1`, nᵏ possible), so the distinctive validated content is *execution* not arithmetic: the .NET cancellation contract (`ThrowIfCancellationRequested`→OperationCanceledException + Canceled state, pre-start `Task.Run(func,token)` cancellation, awaiting a canceled task throws) + `IProgress<double>` 0→1.0; INV Σcounts=L−k+1 / empty·k>L→empty dict / k≤0→ArgumentOutOfRangeException via awaited task; uppercased (case-insensitive) + alphabet-agnostic (IUPAC N counted literally); ATGG→{ATG:1,TGG:1} + GTAGAGCTGT oracles; one assumption = numeric contract identical to sync (non-correctness-affecting); single-thread offload (not parallelized), suffix-tree evaluated-not-used; wraps sync KMER-COUNT-001 (not yet ingested); record [[kmer-async-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-generation]] — K-mer family *space-enumeration* unit (`KMER-GENERATE-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.GenerateAllKmers`): exhaustive enumeration of ALL possible k-mers of length `k` over an alphabet — the complete k-mer universe `Σ^k` of size `n^k` (4^k for DNA), depends only on `k`+alphabet not on any sequence; DISTINCT from counting (produces the full n^k word set / address space, siblings extract observed substrings + counts); k-fold Cartesian product `itertools.product(Σ,repeat=k)`, lazy recursive prefix-extension, odometer emission → lexicographic for a sorted alphabet; INV n^k count / all-distinct-set / length-k / sorted→lexicographic; k=1→{A,C,G,T}, k=2→16 (AA..TT), k=3→64, protein 20^2=400, single-letter 1^4=1 oracles; k≤0→ArgumentOutOfRangeException, empty alphabet→ArgumentException, unsorted→positional order, verbatim/no-dedup; O(k·n^k) time/O(k) lazy space, suffix-tree N/A (generates not searches); shares the "ACGT"-default + k≤0-throws API contract with [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[k-mer-euclidean-distance]] but NOT the `CountKmers` primitive; supplies the index space for [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]]/[[k-mer-euclidean-distance]]/[[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]]; deviations None; record [[kmer-generate-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-positions]] — K-mer family *occurrence-index* unit (`KMER-POSITIONS-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.FindKmerPositions`): the ascending 0-based positions where a given k-mer occurs in a sequence — *where*, not *how many* (the inverse index to the counting units) — solving the exact Pattern Matching Problem `Occ(P,T)={i∈[0,L−k]:T[i..i+k)=P}` with all overlapping starts reported; INV-01..04 (match predicate / ascending / count=overlap-occurrences / range `[0,L−k]`, empty when k>L); case-insensitive upper-casing (sibling `CountKmers`), unrestricted-text alphabet, null/empty & k>L & absent → empty (no throw), whole-seq→`[0]`; `ATAT`/`GATATATGCATATACTT`→`[1,3,9]` + `AA`/`AAAA`→`[0,1,2]` oracles; O(L·k) naive span scan, suffix-tree evaluated-not-used (unordered leaves, single-query no amortization); three API-shape assumptions (0-based, case-fold, empty-not-throw), deviations None; the single-pattern K-mer sibling of multi-pattern [[known-motif-search]], distinct from the counting siblings [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-positions-001-evidence]].
- [[both-strand-kmer-counting]] — K-mer family strand-aware count unit (`KMER-BOTH-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.CountKmersBothStrands`): the ADDITIVE / kPAL-"balance" both-strand profile `count[w] = forward[w] + forward[RC(w)]` (count k-mers of S and of RC(S), sum per key), grounded in inversion symmetry (Shporer 2016) + kPAL balance (Anvar 2014); distinct from — and does NOT implement — the canonical-collapsing convention (lexicographically-smaller of {w,RC(w)} as one key, Jellyfish `-C` / Mash); INV Σcount=2·(L−k+1) / count[w]=count[RC(w)] strand-symmetric / palindrome RC(w)=w→count doubled on one key; two linear passes O(n·k), suffix-tree evaluated-not-used; case-insensitive/IUPAC-complemented, empty·k>L→empty dict, k≤0→ArgumentOutOfRangeException (inherited from `CountKmers`); ATGGC k=2→{AT:2,TG:1,GG:1,GC:2,CC:1,CA:1} + ACGT→{AC:2,CG:2,GT:2} + AAA→{AA:2,TT:2} oracles; built on the same sync `CountKmers` primitive as [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; two API-shape assumptions, deviations None; record [[kmer-both-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-statistics]] — K-mer family *summary-statistics* unit (`KMER-STATS-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.AnalyzeKmers`): a companion summary layer over the shared `CountKmers` multiset that reduces the count profile to `KmerStatistics` {TotalKmers=L−k+1=Σcounts, UniqueKmers=**distinct** count, MaxCount, MinCount, AverageCount=total/distinct (rounded 2dp), Entropy=Shannon **k-entropy** `−Σ p(α)log₂p(α)`, `p=mult/(L−k+1)`, bits}; the one distinct piece of content is the k-entropy (Manca 2021 + Entropy–Rank Ratio, corroborated by Wikipedia/BioInfoLogics count tables); GOTCHA `UniqueKmers` = distinct count NOT the count==1 singletons (that is KMER-UNIQUE-001); INV Total=Σcounts / Unique=distinct(CountKmers) / homopolymer→H0,max=min=total / all-distinct→H log₂D,max=min=1 / k>L·empty→all-zero; GTAGAGCTGT k=1 (10/4/4/1/2.5/1.8464) + k=3 (8/8/1/1/log₂8=3.0) + ATCGATCAC k=3 (7/6/2/1/2.5216) + AAAA k=2 (3/1/3/3/0) oracles; case-insensitive, k≤0→ArgumentOutOfRangeException; two presentation-only assumptions (AverageCount 2dp, Entropy unrounded); shares the `CountKmers` primitive with [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[both-strand-kmer-counting]], distinct from generation/positions/distance siblings; deviations None; record [[kmer-stats-001-evidence]].
- [[unique-and-mincount-kmers]] — K-mer family *frequency-filtering* unit (`KMER-UNIQUE-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.FindUniqueKmers` + `FindKmersWithMinCount`): selects k-mers by their per-k-mer **Count** (overlapping occurrences, Compeau & Pevzner `Count(Text,Pattern)`) at opposite ends of the frequency distribution — `FindUniqueKmers` = the `Count==1` **singletons**, `FindKmersWithMinCount` = the `Count≥minCount` **recurrent** k-mers ordered by count desc; total/distinct/unique terminology (BioInfoLogics: unique = "appear only once"; Wikipedia L−k+1 total); GOTCHA "unique"=singleton set here ≠ [[k-mer-statistics]]'s `UniqueKmers`=distinct count (ATCGATCAC k=3 → 5 unique vs 6 distinct, ATC=2 excluded); oracles ATCGATCAC k=3→{TCG,CGA,GAT,TCA,CAC}, AGAT k=2→{AG,GA,AT}, ACGTACGT k=4 FindKmersWithMinCount(…,2)→{(ACGT,2)}/(…,1)→all-4-count-desc/FindUniqueKmers→{CGTA,GTAC,TACG}, AAAAA k=3→∅; case-insensitive, k≤0→ArgumentOutOfRangeException, empty·k>L→empty; two assumptions (minCount≤1→all distinct count-desc; upper-casing), deviations None; filters the shared `CountKmers` multiset like [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[both-strand-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-unique-001-evidence]].
- [[longest-common-substring]] — Sequence-Comparison longest-common-substring / common-region-detection unit (`GENOMIC-COMMON-001`): the maximal *contiguous* substring shared by two strings (distinct from the gapped longest common *subsequence*) via a generalized suffix tree (LCS = deepest internal node whose subtree holds leaves from both strings, Θ(n+m) build + DFS, Gusfield 1997); `FindLongestCommonRegion` (0-based positions in both) + `FindCommonRegions(minLength)` (all distinct shared runs ≥ minLength), None=empty/len 0/pos −1, identical→whole seq at 0/0; documented deterministic first-found-in-`other` tie-break (CACAGAG/TACATAGAT ties ACA vs AGA → ACA); Wikipedia + GeeksforGeeks sources, shares the suffix-tree exact-match engine with [[dot-plot-word-match]]; deviations None.
- [[longest-repeated-substring]] — Repeat-Analysis LRS + repeat-enumeration unit (`GENOMIC-REPEAT-001`): the longest substring recurring within *one* DNA sequence (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindLongestRepeat`) + all distinct substrings occurring ≥2× with length ≥ minLength (`FindRepeats`), both via the *single-string* suffix tree's deepest internal node with ≥2 leaves (string depth = repeat length; CMU §2.1 / Wikipedia / GeeksforGeeks App-3 / Gusfield 5.4); overlaps counted, no-repeat/empty→`RepeatInfo.None`, `minLength≤0`→`max(1,minLength)`, ACGT-only, no reverse-complement/maximal-repeat classification; FindRepeats via sorted-suffix adjacent-LCP *every-prefix* enumeration (O(n²), FINDINGS_REGISTER short-prefix fix); ATCGATCGA→ATCGA{0,4}, AAAAAAAAAA→AAAAAAAAA{0,1}, ATATATA→ATATA{0,2}, ACGTACGTTTTTACGT@3→8-substring oracles; the *single-string* sibling of [[longest-common-substring]], distinct from the tandem/inverted [[repetitive-element-detection]] anchor; tie-break + ascending-positions assumptions, deviations None.
- [[open-reading-frame-detection]] — Analysis ORF-detection unit (`GENOMIC-ORF-001`): six-frame ATG→first-in-frame-stop enumeration (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindOpenReadingFrames`), standard code (start ATG / stops TAA-TAG-TGA), reported span **includes** the stop (Length%3==0) while the translated protein **excludes** it; THE correctness rule = every in-frame ATG reaching a stop reported, so **nested ORFs sharing a stop** both returned (Rosalind `MGMTPRLGLESLLE`/`MTPRLGLESLLE`), ATG-with-no-stop→none; `minLength` in **nucleotides** inclusive (default 100), 0-based Position, Frame 1–3 + IsReverseComplement, INV-01..05 (starts ATG / ends stop / len%3==0 / ≥minLength / six-frame), O(n²) worst / O(n) typical; Rosalind_99→4 distinct proteins + ATGAAAAAATAA→MKK oracles; Rosalind + Wikipedia + NCBI ORFfinder + transl_table=1 sources; deviations None (one fixed greedy bug); deliberately **not** contract-equivalent to annotation `GenomeAnnotator.FindOrfs` (ANNOT-ORF-001: ATG/GTG/TTG, aa-length, strand/start flags) or `Translator.FindOrfs` (genetic-code-parameterized); coding potential is a separate step ([[coding-potential-hexamer-score]]).
- [[known-motif-search]] — Motif-Analysis known-motif-search anchor (`GENOMIC-MOTIFS-001`): multi-pattern **exact** substring matching of a caller-supplied set of known query motifs (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindMotif`) — the "you know what you're looking for" exact-equality baseline, distinct from motif *discovery* and *degenerate* (IUPAC/PROSITE/PWM) matching; THE correctness rule = all **overlapping** occurrences reported (AAA in AAAAA→{0,1,2}, per Gusfield/Biopython `count_overlap` 3-not-2); 0-based sorted positions, per-motif position lists with absent motifs omitted, upper-cased result keys, empty/whitespace motif→no entry (`Array.Empty<int>()`); EcoRI GAATTC→{0,9} + `{ACGT,AA,TTT}` in ACGTACGTAA oracles; Tufts/Gusfield + Biopython `Seq.search` + Wikipedia "Restriction site" sources; shares exact-all-occurrences semantics with [[longest-common-substring]]/[[dot-plot-word-match]]; deviations None.
- [[alpha-diversity]] — Metagenomics diversity family anchor (first META-* unit, META-ALPHA-001): within-sample diversity indices from one taxon→abundance map (`MetagenomicsAnalyzer.CalculateAlphaDiversity` → `AlphaDiversity` record) — observed richness S_obs, Shannon H=−Σpᵢln(pᵢ) in nats, Simpson concentration λ=Σpᵢ², inverse Simpson 1/λ (Hill order-2 effective species), Pielou evenness J=H/ln(S) for S>1 else 0, Chao1 S_obs+f₁²/(2f₂) (f₂=0→bias-corrected S_obs+f₁(f₁−1)/2, non-integer/proportional→S_obs); Whittaker 1960 α/β/γ framework, Shannon 1948/Simpson 1949/Hill 1973/Chao 1984/Pielou 1966; counts-or-proportions internally normalized, non-positive filtered, O(n); empty/null→all-0, single species→H0/λ1/J0; one accepted deviation = Chao1 count-vs-proportion gate; between-sample [[beta-diversity]] its sibling; deviations else None.
- [[metagenomic-binning]] — Metagenomics family binning unit (third META-* unit, META-BIN-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.BinContigs`): groups mixed-community contigs back to their genome of origin (MAGs) by k-means over a composite distance `|ΔGC|+|Δcoverage|+TNF-Pearson-distance` (GC-sorted deterministic centroid init, ≤50 iters, minBinSize 500 kb filter) → `GenomeBin` records; completeness=`min(L/expectedGenomeSize×100,100)` (default 4 Mbp) + contamination=`min(gcStdDev/0.5×100,100)` are LENGTH-RATIO/GC-VARIANCE **proxies** (CheckM marker-gene QC now built as a SEPARATE opt-in path — CheckM Eqs. 1–2 over CC0 Pfam marker sets, `EstimateBinQualityFromMarkerCounts`/`DetectMarkers`, NOT wired into `BinContigs`; see [[meta-bin-001-markerqc-evidence]]); INV unique BinId / metrics [0,100] / GC [0,1] / TotalLength=Σ / disjoint partition / Coverage=mean; M5 50.0 / M6 0-100 / M7 1.0-0.0 / M12 25 oracles; opt-in TETRA z-score signature (`CalculateTetranucleotideZScores`/`TetranucleotideZScoreCorrelation`) — RC-extended strand, 256-word Markov expectation `E=N(n1n2n3)·N(n2n3n4)/N(n2n3)`, Schbath variance, Pearson correlation of z-vectors (scale-invariant), z(ACGT)=√5 for ACGTACGTGGCC, N(n2n3)=0/non-positive-var→z=0; Maguire 2020 limits (plasmids 1-29%/GIs 38-44% poorly recovered), similar-GC+coverage→co-bin; three prior assumptions resolved, deviations None; record [[meta-bin-001-evidence]]; Metagenomics-family sibling of [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]].
- [[taxonomic-classification]] — Metagenomics family taxonomic-classification unit (fourth META-* unit, META-CLASS-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.ClassifyReads` + `BuildKmerDatabase` + `TaxonomyTree.Lca`): faithful Kraken (Wood & Salzberg 2014) per-read/contig assignment — canonical-k-mer (`min(kmer,revcomp)`, default k=31) database mapping each k-mer to the **LCA of all owning reference taxa**, per-read **classification tree** (hit taxa + ancestors weighted by k-mer count) scored over **root-to-leaf (RTL)** paths → assigned taxon = max-scoring path's leaf, equal-max → LCA of leaves, no k-mer hits → **Unclassified** (taxonomy root, C=0); Confidence = **C/Q** (Kraken 2: C = clade k-mers under assigned label, Q = non-ambiguous k-mers queried); ambiguous (non-ACGT) k-mers skipped/not in Q, upper-cased, semicolon/pipe taxonomy strings; invariants |out|=|in| / 0≤C/Q≤1 / C≤Q / Q=len−k+1 (all-ACGT) / canonical uniqueness / DB-build LCA / LCA siblings→parent, ancestor/descendant→ancestor, self→self, disjoint→root; empty/short-<k/no-match → Unclassified, empty DB → all Unclassified; scoped to **per-read classification** (abundance *profiling* Taxonomic_Profile is a separate later unit); research-grade, no deviations / no open questions; siblings [[metagenomic-binning]] (per-contig MAGs) & [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]] (consume the abundance profile); record [[meta-class-001-evidence]].
- [[beta-diversity]] — Metagenomics diversity family between-sample unit (second META-* unit, META-BETA-001): between-sample dissimilarity from two taxon→abundance maps (`MetagenomicsAnalyzer.CalculateBetaDiversity` → `BetaDiversity` record) — Bray-Curtis BC=1−2·Σmin(N_ij,N_ik)/Σ(N_ij+N_ik) (abundance-sensitive, range [0,1], NOT a true metric) + Jaccard distance J=1−|A∩B|/|A∪B| (presence/absence via abundance>0, true distance metric); Whittaker 1960 α/β/γ (beta=turnover), Bray & Curtis 1957, Jaccard 1901; single union-pass O(u), no BC normalization (caller-scaled), +SharedSpecies/UniqueToSample1/2 counts; identical→0/0, disjoint→1/1, both-empty→0/0 & one-empty→1 guards; fish-tank BC 13/33 & J 1/3, symmetry BC 3/5 & J 2/3 oracles; one accepted deviation = UniFracDistance placeholder 0 (no phylo tree); within-sample sibling [[alpha-diversity]]; ecological-Jaccard shares the index math but not domain with sequence [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]].
- [[functional-prediction]] — Metagenomics family functional-prediction unit (fifth META-* unit, META-FUNC-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.PredictFunctions` + `FindPathwayEnrichment`): predicts a community's *functional* capability (PICRUSt / KO-pathway style) in two exact-numeric pieces — (A) homology-based annotation transfer: exact-signature `string.Contains` hit scored by BLOSUM62 self-score S, bit `S'=(λS−lnK)/ln2` and E-value `E=K·m·n·e^(−λS)=m·n·2^(−S')` (ungapped BLOSUM62 λ=0.3176/K=0.134, Altschul/`blast_stat.c`), best hit = lowest E-value / highest bit (INV-01..03,06); (B) hypergeometric pathway ORA `P(X≥x)=1−Σ C(M,i)C(N−M,n−i)/C(N,n)` in log-Gamma space, background=union-of-pathways default + query unioned in, sorted ascending, p∈[0,1], x/M/n=0→p=1 (INV-04,05); oracles WWW→S'18.0202932787533/E 3.3852730346546e−5 + N8000/M400/n100/x20→7.88e−8; *Simplified* — exact substring not gapped alignment (ASM-01, divergent homologs missed), no gapped λ/K / composition stats / HMM / FDR; asks "what can they do" vs the "who is there" of [[taxonomic-classification]]/[[metagenomic-binning]] and the diversity of [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]]; BLAST significance distinct from percent-id [[alignment-statistics]]; ORA half owned by [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] (the dedicated META-PATHWAY-001 unit); record [[meta-func-001-evidence]].
- [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] — Metagenomics family pathway-enrichment unit (META-PATHWAY-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindPathwayEnrichment` / `HypergeometricUpperTail`): the GO::TermFinder / clusterProfiler over-representation statistic — score each pathway by the hypergeometric **right-tail** `P(X≥x)=1−Σ_{i=0}^{x−1}C(M,i)C(N−M,n−i)/C(N,n)` (N=background, M=pathway size, n=query, x=overlap; sampling without replacement, upper tail only), `phyper(x−1,M,N−M,n,lower.tail=FALSE)` reference (the q=x−1 shift gives P(X≥x)); log-Gamma summation to N=8000, p∈[0,1], pathways sorted ascending; p=1 when x/M/n=0, **M↔n symmetry**, without-replacement feasibility drops C(·,·)=0 terms; background = explicit `backgroundGenes` else union-of-pathway-members default (query always unioned in), members intersected with background; **no BH/Bonferroni FDR** correction; Boyle 2004 + PNNL ORA §8.2 sources, oracles 7.88e−8 + 1/252 + 5/6 + 251/252; one caller-overridable background-defaulting assumption; **owns** the ORA machinery that [[functional-prediction]] uses as component B; generic statistic (GO/proteomics), research-grade, no contradictions; record [[meta-pathway-001-evidence]].
- [[taxonomic-profile]] — Metagenomics family community-abundance profiling unit (sixth META-* unit, META-PROF-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.GenerateTaxonomicProfile`): the **aggregation/estimation** step downstream of per-read [[taxonomic-classification]] — takes an `IEnumerable<TaxonomicClassification>` and returns a `TaxonomicProfile` with **relative-abundance maps at four ranks** (kingdom/phylum/genus/species, abundance = count(taxon)/Σcount(classified)), **inline species-level diversity** (Shannon H=−Σpᵢln(pᵢ) in nats + Simpson concentration λ=Σpᵢ²), and **read counts** (TotalReads/ClassifiedReads); Unclassified excluded from denominators, empty rank strings filtered, per-rank Σ≈1.0; invariants ClassifiedReads≤TotalReads / ClassifiedReads=Σ(counts any rank) / Shannon≥0 / 0≤Simpson≤1; oracles Shannon=ln(3) (3 uniform), Simpson=0.375 ([2,1,1]); empty→0/0/empty & single taxon→1.0/H0/λ1 (vs empty→λ0); count-based tally (NOT MetaPhlAn marker-coverage, no genome-size correction), inherits upstream classifier accuracy; the profiling unit [[taxonomic-classification]] deliberately deferred, sibling of [[alpha-diversity]] (richer six-index within-sample summary) / [[beta-diversity]]; MetaPhlAn/Segata 2012, research-grade, no contradictions; record [[meta-prof-001-evidence]].
- [[antibiotic-resistance-gene-detection]] — Metagenomics family AMR gene-detection unit (seventh META-* unit, META-RESIST-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindAntibioticResistanceGenes`): ResFinder-style screen of assembled contigs against a **caller-supplied** resistance-gene reference DB, reporting the single **best-matching gene per contig** — `BestUngappedMatch` slides each reference across the contig (offsets −(m−1)..n−1, overhanging both ends), keeps the max-match window (tie→shorter/higher-identity), then identity=matches/w (BLAST gapless, Heng Li 2018) & coverage=w/m (fraction of **reference** length, so contig-edge/split genes still scored), reported iff identity≥idThreshold AND coverage≥covThreshold; best match = max identity, tie→max coverage (Zankari 2012 "best-matching gene", CARD RGI best-hit); INV-01..05, defaults 0.90 ID / 0.60 cov (named constants), Perfect=1.0/1.0 (CARD); oracles CGTACGT@AAACGTACGT→1.0/1.0, CGTTCGT vs CGTACGT→6/7≈0.857/1.0, edge CGTA→1.0 / 4⁄7≈0.571; *Simplified* — gapless ungapped (ASM-01, indel matches under-scored vs gapped BLAST; substitution + edge-truncation exact), no SNP/protein-homology (CARD variant/homolog models out of scope), nucleotide-only case-sensitive, legacy `FindResistanceGenes` motif stub separate; asks "**which known resistance genes are present**" vs the who/what/how-diverse of [[taxonomic-classification]]/[[functional-prediction]]/[[alpha-diversity]]; BLAST-style homology screen sharing machinery with [[functional-prediction]] but scoring nucleotide identity/coverage not BLOSUM62 bit-score (identity denominator = [[alignment-statistics]] rule); provenance note flagged (evidence 0.80/0.98 vs impl 0.90 default); record [[meta-resist-001-evidence]].
- [[significant-taxa-detection]] — Metagenomics family differential-abundance unit (eighth META-* unit, META-TAXA-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.MannWhitneyU` / `FindSignificantTaxa`): per-taxon **two-group Mann–Whitney U (Wilcoxon rank-sum)** test asking "which taxa differ in abundance between two groups?" — non-parametric, rank-based, suits compositional/zero-inflated data (Xia & Sun 2017). Pool→midranks (tied values averaged, accumulate Σ(t³−t))→`U1=R1−n1(n1+1)/2`, `U2=n1·n2−U1`; `m_U=n1·n2/2`, tie-corrected `σ_U=sqrt(n1·n2·(n1+n2+1)/12 − n1·n2·Σ(t³−t)/(12n(n−1)))`; `z=(|U−m_U|−cc)/σ_U` on `max(U1,U2)`, cc∈{0,0.5} (0.5 on by default = SciPy `use_continuity`); two-tailed `p=2·(1−Φ(z))` clamped [0,1], Φ via `StatisticsHelper.NormalCDF` (A&S 7.1.26, ≈1e−6 accuracy). `FindSignificantTaxa` runs it per taxon over label-defined ({1,2}) groups → `SignificantTaxon` ascending by p. INV-01..06 (U1+U2=n1·n2, 0≤U≤n1·n2, p∈[0,1], Significant⇔p<threshold, all-tied→σ0→z0→p1, group-swap symmetric); oracles SciPy x[19,22,16,29,24]/y[20,11,17,12]→U1=17/U2=3/σ=4.0825/z_cc=1.5922→p≈0.11135 (z_nocc=1.7146→p≈0.08641) + tortoise/hare U_T=11/U_H=25/sum=36; empty group→ArgumentException, absent taxon→abundance 0 (ASM-03); asymptotic-not-exact, no FDR (caller applies BH), ignores compositionality; **consumes** [[taxonomic-profile]] abundance vectors; distinct-by-**test** from the hypergeometric [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] and Fisher's-exact [[differentially-methylated-regions]]; siblings [[alpha-diversity]] / [[beta-diversity]]; record [[meta-taxa-001-evidence]].
- [[methylation-context-classification]] — epigenetics family CpG/CHG/CHH context-classification unit (sixth/final EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-METHYL-001): sequence-only trinucleotide classifier partitioning cytosines into CpG/CHG/CHH from the downstream base(s) — distinct because it handles the *non-CpG* CHG/CHH contexts [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] does not call from reads. Rule (Cornish-Bowden 1985 IUPAC H={A,C,T}="not G"): CpG⟺b₁=G, CHG⟺b₁∈H & b₂=G, CHH⟺b₁∈H & b₂∈H; CpG/CHG symmetric, CHH asymmetric (Krueger-Andrews 2011). Three ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: `GetMethylationContext` (O(1), null when not a classifiable C), `FindMethylationSites` (O(n) scan → one site/classifiable C, 0-based, sequence-only level=0/coverage=0 placeholder), `GenerateMethylationProfile` (shared with [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]], Schultz 2012 weighted Σ(level·cov)/Σcov, zero-coverage→unweighted-mean fallback); CGACAGCAA→CpG@0/CHG@3/CHH@6 + weighted (8+2)/(10+10)=0.5 oracles; G-never-H (CGG→CpG), terminal-CG-still-CpG, incomplete-trailing / non-ACGT unclassified; Lister 2009 realism (IMR90 99.98% CG vs H1 ES ~25% non-CG); single-strand only, no symmetric-strand pairing; two assumptions (level=0 placeholder, 0.5 MethylatedCpG count cutoff); no contradictions.
- [[rna-base-pairing]] — MiRNA family anchor + shared RNA base-pairing primitive (first MiRNA unit, MIRNA-PAIR-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): deciding **whether two RNA bases can pair** and building the antiparallel miRNA-mRNA duplex from that rule. `CanPair`⟺{A-U,U-A,G-C,C-G,G-U,U-G} = Watson-Crick {A-U,G-C} (Agarwal 2015) + the single standard **G-U wobble** (Crick 1966); `IsWobblePair`⟺{G-U,U-G}, wobble⊆pairable, wobble counted **separately** from matches (PMC4870184). `GetReverseComplement` = antiparallel RNA reverse complement for seed→target motif (Lewis 2005; let-7a `GAGGUAG`→`CUACCUC`). `AlignMiRnaToTarget` pairs miRNA[i]↔target[len−1−i] over the shorter overlap, ungapped, emitting `|`(WC)/`:`(wobble)/space(mismatch); counts sum to min(len), Gaps=0; ΔG = **simplified** Turner-2004 stacking sum over consecutive paired runs (sign reliable — fully-WC ≤0, all-mismatch ≥0 — magnitude not). Oracles AAAA/UUUU→4 matches, GGGG/UUUU→4 wobbles, AAAA/AAAA→4 mismatches; DNA T→U normalised, unknown base→N never pairs, empty→empty duplex. The **shared** pairing rule RNA secondary-structure classification also uses; **not** target-site efficacy prediction (that is `FindTargetSites`/MIRNA-TARGET-001), and the A-opposite-position-1 preference is Argonaute recognition, not base pairing; record [[mirna-pair-001-evidence]].
- [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] — MiRNA family precursor-hairpin unit (second MiRNA unit, MIRNA-PRECURSOR-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): finding stem-loop pre-miRNA precursors (~60-120 nt) from which Dicer excises the ~22 nt mature duplex. **Default heuristic** `FindPreMiRnaHairpins` counts uninterrupted complementary pairs ({A-U,G-C}+G-U wobble, [[rna-base-pairing]] primitive) from both ends inward → accept iff stem ≥18 bp (Krol 2004) + loop 3-25 nt (Bartel 2004); extracts mature(5' arm)/star(3' arm), balanced dot-bracket, Turner-2004 ΔG; **documented limitation** — consecutive-pairing is stricter than real structure, rejects natural miRBase precursors (hsa-mir-21 16 end-pairs, let-7a-1 5, tests M18/M19). **Opt-in** `AssessHairpinByMfe`/`FindPreMiRnaHairpinsByMfe` fold with the RNA-STRUCT-001 Zuker–Stiegler engine and read the hairpin from the real MFE structure (single dominant hairpin/no multibranch + stem ≥16 (Ambros 2003) + loop 3-25 + MFEI ≥0.85 (Zhang 2006, AMFE=100·|ΔG°|/n, MFEI=AMFE/GC%)) → detects hsa-mir-21 (ΔG° −35.13/MFEI 1.0037) & let-7a-1; rejects a stronger-ΔG° multibranch 5S-rRNA-like on **structure**. **Opt-in** `PredictDroshaDicerCleavage` = published ruler (Drosha +11 bp basal junction/Han 2006, Dicer 22-nt 5'-count/Park 2011, RNase III 2-nt overhang/Lee 2003, CNNC 16-18 nt confidence flag/Auyeung 2013; hsa-miR-21-5p cross-check). **Opt-in** `ClassifyPreMiRna` = logistic regression over [ΔG,AMFE,MFEI,GC,%paired], 13 public-domain miRBase positives vs Altschul-Erickson di-shuffle negatives (Bonnet 2004 convention), held-out AUC 1.0, no GPL miRDeep2 code; read-stacking miRDeep2 signal out of scope (needs reads); record [[mirna-precursor-001-evidence]].
- [[seed-sequence-analysis]] — MiRNA family seed-extraction unit (third MiRNA unit, MIRNA-SEED-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): **string-level** extraction and comparison of the mature-miRNA 5' seed — the primary determinant of animal target recognition — not binding prediction. `GetSeedSequence` returns positions **2-8** (7 nt, extended seed) via `Substring(1,7)` uppercase (casing only, **no** T→U); `<8 nt`/null/empty → `""`. `CreateMiRna(name, sequence)` normalises `ToUpperInvariant()`+`T→U`, extracts the seed from the normalised sequence, stores `SeedSequence` + fixed **zero-based** `SeedStart=1`/`SeedEnd=7`. `CompareSeedRegions` = Hamming over the 7-nt seed (`Matches`+`Mismatches`=7, mismatches also count any length diff), `IsSameFamily` ⟺ **exact seed-string equality**; empty seed → zeroed result. **miRNA family = identical 2-8 seed** (let-7a/-7b/-7c-5p all `GAGGUAG` → same family; miR-21-5p `AGCUUAU` differs); self→0 mismatches. Domain context: TargetScan site ladder 8mer/7mer-m8/7mer-A1/6mer over the 2-7-vs-2-8 distinction, but matching-to-target + site-class assignment is deferred to target-site prediction (MIRNA-TARGET-001, future); seed→target motif reverse complement is owned by [[rna-base-pairing]] (`GetReverseComplement`). **Intentionally simplified** — exact-7-mer family equality (no isomiR/offset/noncanonical seeds, not a curated taxonomy); 2-7-vs-2-8 terminology collapse flagged, no source contradictions; record [[mirna-seed-001-evidence]].
- [[mirna-target-site-prediction]] — MiRNA family target-site-prediction unit (fourth & **final** MiRNA unit, MIRNA-TARGET-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`, **completes** the family): finding mRNA target sites for a miRNA and classifying the **Bartel/TargetScan hierarchy**. `FindTargetSites(mRna, miRna, minScore=0.5)` = two-pass, `T→U`, 0-based-inclusive antiparallel scan for the seed reverse complement (`seedRC=revcomp(m₂…m₈)`, 6mer core `seedRC[2..7]`): pass-1 upgrades 6mer-core hits to **8mer** (pos 2-8 + A opposite pos 1) / **7mer-m8** (2-8) / **7mer-A1** (2-7 + A1) / **6mer** (2-7); pass-2 finds **offset-6mer** (3-8) only where not overlapping a retained higher-priority site (INV-04). Heuristic `Score∈[0,1]` (base 1.0/0.52/0.32/0.15/0.10, +0.05 >10 matches, −0.01/mismatch) + heuristic `FreeEnergy` (sign-reliable) — ranking aid, **not** calibrated repression. **Depends on** [[seed-sequence-analysis]] (the 2-8 seed determines targeting) + [[rna-base-pairing]] (`GetReverseComplement` motif + `AlignMiRnaToTarget` `|`/`:`/space duplex). **Opt-in `ScoreTargetSiteContextPlusPlus`** = source-fitted TargetScan **context++** (Agarwal 2015): per-site-type MLR, sum of `coeff×scaledScore`, continuous features min-max scaled + indicators raw; realises Intercept/Local_AU/sRNA1/sRNA8/Site8/3P_score/Min_dist/Len_3UTR/Off6m, **computes** TA_3UTR=log10 N (`ComputeTa3Utr`, Garcia 2011) + SA (Turner-2004 McCaskill partition unpaired-prob) + PCT (Friedman Bls→published sigmoid); SPS/Len_ORF/ORF8m/PCT-`b0..b3` caller-supplied (compiled TargetScan tables, not bundled) → honest **partial** `ContextScorePartial` + `OmittedFeatures` (8mer let-7a all-G-flank partial CS = −0.7561913315126536). `Centered`/`Supplementary` enum members not emitted (accepted); bulged/centered/supplementary/noncanonical + isoforms out of scope; no contradictions; record [[mirna-target-001-evidence]].
- [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]] — Oncology family anchor (first ONCO-* unit, ONCO-ACTION-001): **clinical actionability assessment** by the OncoKB Therapeutic Levels of Evidence (Chakravarty 2017). A **pure ranking** — given a variant's caller-supplied leveled drug associations, return the **maximum** level under the fixed combined order `R1 > 1 > 2 > 3A > 3B > 4 > R2` (sensitivity axis `1 > 2 > 3A > 3B > 4`, resistance axis `R1 > R2`), the two axes reported separately (a variant may carry both); no leveled association → **NotActionable**. Seven tiers: 1 (FDA in-indication) / 2 (NCCN in-indication) / 3A (clinical evidence in-indication) / 3B (another indication) / 4 (biological evidence) / R1 (standard resistance) / R2 (investigational resistance); 1/2/R1 = standard vs 3A/3B/4/R2 = investigational (SOP v3, consistent with AMP/ASCO/CAP Li 2017). **Knowledgebase is a caller input** — the library ranks, it does not embed/annotate the OncoKB DB; NotActionable-name is the library's; not for clinical use; record [[onco-action-001-evidence]].
- [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] — Oncology family, second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ANNOT-001): **cancer variant tier classification** by the **AMP/ASCO/CAP 2017 four-tier** consensus (Li MM et al. 2017). A **pure decision rule** over caller-supplied evidence level (A–D) + population MAF + cancer-association flag → **Tier I** (strong, Level A/B) / **II** (potential, Level C/D) / **III** (unknown, no level + rare + cancer assoc) / **IV** (benign, no level + MAF ≥ 1% **or** no assoc). Population frequency is the **III↔IV discriminator**; **evidence level dominates frequency** (a significant biomarker stays Tier I at high MAF). 1% (0.01) is the guideline **primary benign cutoff**, inclusive (MAF 0.01 → Tier IV). `AnnotateCancerVariants` = one annotation per variant in input order; `GetCOSMICAnnotation` = null-on-miss lookup against a **caller-supplied** COSMIC catalog (external DB, not embedded). Distinct from but **consistent with** the sibling OncoKB level-ranking [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; not for clinical use; record [[onco-annot-001-evidence]].
- [[sequencing-artifact-detection]] — Oncology family, third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ARTIFACT-001): **sequencing artifact detection** (`FilterArtifacts`) — the **QC** sibling that removes false-positive somatic calls from DNA damage / mapping bias **before** clinical interpretation (distinct from the two clinical-significance ONCO units). Three disjoint signals: **substitution class** (OxoG oxidation G>T/C>A per Chen 2017 vs FFPE cytosine-deamination C>T/G>A per Do & Dobrovic 2015; else not-an-artifact), the **GIV** read-pair imbalance ratio (`GIV_G_T = count(G>T in R1)/count(G>T in R2)`, neutral 1 / damaged > 1.5, Chen 2017 + Damage-estimator), and **FisherStrand** FS = −10·log10(two-sided Fisher-exact p) on the `[ref_fwd,ref_rev,alt_fwd,alt_rev]` 2×2 table (GATK, FS ≈ 0 no bias / high = artifact). Result ⊆ input; **no BAM parser** (per-strand/read-mate evidence supplied on the variant record); GIV thresholds from the Nature Methods summary; not for clinical use; record [[onco-artifact-001-evidence]].
- [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] — Oncology family, fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ASCAT-001): the **upstream tumor copy-number layer** — allele-specific integer copy number (nA/nB) from per-locus **logR/BAF** by a joint **purity ρ / ploidy ψ** grid fit (**ASCAT**, Van Loo 2010: `nA/nB` inversion, minimise length-weighted squared minor-allele distance to non-negative integers, BAF=0.5 down-weighted ×0.05, GoF = (1−d/maxdist)·100, **γ=1 for sequencing**). Four disjoint stages: (1) ASCAT core (ρ,ψ) fit; (2) **ASPCF** penalised-least-squares joint segmentation `L=Σ(y−ȳ)²+γ|S|` via O(n²) DP (Nilsen 2012) with common change points + BAF mirroring (Ross 2021); (3) **subclonal** two-state mixture `n_obs=f·n₁+(1−f)·n₂` over bracketing integers (Battenberg / Nik-Zainal 2012); (4) **multiplicity/CCF** VAF inversion `VAF=(m·CCF·p)/(c·p+2(1−p))`, clamp m to [1,major-CN] (McGranahan 2016 / PICTograph / DeCiFering). Planted-truth tests invert the forward model (ρ₀=0.80, ψ₀∈{2,3}). The allele-specific/clonal counterpart to the total-CN [[aneuploidy-detection]]; substrate beneath the clinical-interpretation ONCO siblings; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ascat-001-evidence]].
- [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] — Oncology family, fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CCF-001): the **downstream clonal-structure layer** — estimate each mutation's **cancer cell fraction** `CCF = f·(ρ·N_T+2(1−ρ))/(ρ·m)` (`EstimateCCF`; McGranahan 2016 / PICTograph / Tarabichi 2021, corroborated three ways; m ∈ [1,tumor CN], ρ ∈ (0,1]) with a reported-value **[0,1] cap** that exposes the uncapped raw (the raw formula can exceed 1 — CNAqc 1.06 noise case), then **`ClusterCCFValues`** deconvolutes the CCF vector into clones/subclones by a **deterministic 1D Lloyd k-means** (Lloyd 1982, quantile seeding, no RNG) with **highest-centroid = clonal** (Tarabichi 2021). Consumes the purity ρ / copy number N_T / multiplicity m from the upstream [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (whose §4 carries the same CCF closed form); two source-consistent assumptions ([0,1] cap; Lloyd k-means as the concrete 1D method); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ccf-001-evidence]].
- [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] — Oncology family, sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CHIP-001): the **pre-interpretation biological-origin filter** for liquid biopsy — removes **clonal-hematopoiesis (CHIP)** false positives, the dominant cfDNA confounder (Razavi 2019: 81.6% controls / 53.2% cancer). `IdentifyCHIPVariants` flags a driver-gene variant ({DNMT3A,TET2,ASXL1,TP53,JAK2,SF3B1,SRSF2,PPM1D}, top-3 DNMT3A/TET2/ASXL1) at **VAF ≥ 0.02** (Steensma 2015 / Genovese 2014); `FilterCHIP` removes CH calls by **matched-WBC subtraction** (present in matched WBC ⇒ blood-derived, the definitive origin test, Razavi 2019) plus a **conservative labelled gene+VAF heuristic fallback** (over-removes; strict mode = empty gene panel); `CallVariantOrigin` = the strict **Bolton 2020** rule (WBC VAF ≥ 2% AND ≥ 10 reads AND ≥ φ× tumour VAF, φ=2.0 / 1.5 lymph node). The **biological-origin sibling** of the technical-artifact QC filter [[sequencing-artifact-detection]], upstream of the clinical-interpretation and clonal-structure ONCO units; two source-consistent assumptions (canonical default gene set, ≥1-alt-read WBC presence test); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-chip-001-evidence]].
- [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]] — Oncology family, seventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CLONAL-001): the **probabilistic clonal-structure classifier** — per-mutation **Bayesian CCF posterior** `P(c) ∝ Binom(a|N,f(c))` (uniform prior, 100-point grid `c∈[0.01,1]`) with expected allele fraction `f(c) = αMc/(2(1−α)+αq)` (Landau 2013 ABSOLUTE-style; multiplicity M generalisation, Satas 2021 DeCiFering Eq. 1), classified **clonal iff `P(CCF>0.95) > 0.5`** (two distinct thresholds: 0.95 CCF cut, 0.5 posterior-mass cut) via `ClassifyClonality(variants, purity)`, plus the point-estimate `IdentifyClonalMutations` (strict CCF > 0.95, boundary excluded → indices {0,2,4}). The **`alternative_to`** the point-estimate + Lloyd-k-means [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] — same clonal/subclonal question, but classifies each mutation on its own read-count uncertainty without clustering; consumes purity α / local copy number q / multiplicity M from the upstream [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]]; one API-shape assumption (per-variant local copy number q over a genome-wide ploidy scalar); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-clonal-001-evidence]].
- [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] — Oncology family, eighth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-001): the **total-copy-number classification layer** — a single **log2 copy ratio** → absolute integer CN `n = 2·2^log2` (CNVkit `_log2_ratio_to_absolute_pure`, diploid ref_copies=2) → discrete **CNA state** via CNVkit's `absolute_threshold` hard-threshold caller (default `−1.1/−0.25/0.2/0.7` → DeepDeletion/Loss/Neutral/Gain/Amplification; CN = index of the **first** threshold with `log2 <= thresh`, **boundary-inclusive → lower bin**; above the last → `ceil(2·2^log2)` open-ended Amplification; NaN → neutral CN 2), corroborated by **GISTIC2** (Mermel 2011: ±0.1 noise band subsumed by the neutral bin + +0.848/−0.737 high-amplitude cutoffs). The **total-CN** counterpart to the allele-specific [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] and the per-segment oncology-state sibling of the whole-chromosome [[aneuploidy-detection]] (both share the `n = 2·2^log2` conversion); distinct from SV-CNV-001's `round`-based integer CN (no state classification). One diploid-ploidy=2 assumption; threshold-variant note (docs germline `−0.4/0.3` vs code tumor `−0.25/0.2`); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-001-evidence]].
- [[focal-amplification-detection]] — Oncology family, ninth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-002): the **focal-amplification layer** — a two-part predicate `DetectFocalAmplifications` keeps segments both **amplified** (log2 gain > GISTIC2 `t_amp` 0.1) **and** **focal** (SegLen / ArmLength < `broad_len_cutoff` 0.98 — Mermel 2011's length-based, not amplitude-based, focal-vs-arm-level split; strict `< 0.98`, exactly 0.98 → arm-level), then `IdentifyAmplifiedOncogenes` maps each focal amplification's arm prefix to a built-in oncogene panel (17q→ERBB2 · 8q→MYC · 7p→EGFR · 11q→CCND1 · 12q→MDM2 **and** CDK4, NCBI Gene cytobands). Orthogonal to the log2→5-state [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) — a **length** question, not an amplitude bin — sharing only the GISTIC2 `t_amp`=0.1 amplitude gate. Sources GISTIC2 Mermel 2011 + GISTIC2 docs (`broad_len_cutoff`/`t_amp`) + CNVkit (single-copy gain log2 0.585 > 0.1) + NCBI Gene. Worked oracles A 17q 0.50→ERBB2 / B 8q 0.99 arm-level / C 7p log2 0.05 not-amplified / D 11q 0.98 boundary. Two assumptions (amplitude+length fusion; caller-supplied arm label + length, no cytoband table); deletions out of scope (ONCO-CNA-003); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-002-evidence]].
- [[homozygous-deletion-detection]] — Oncology family, tenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-003): the **deep-deletion layer**, the **deletion mirror of ONCO-CNA-002** — filter segments whose classified integer copy number is **exactly 0** (a homozygous / deep deletion: cBioPortal `−2` "Deep Deletion", Cheng et al. 2017 "zero copies of both alleles" / two hits; **reuses** [[copy-number-alteration-classification]]'s CN-0 = `DeepDeletion` call, **no new threshold**), then `IdentifyDeletedTumorSuppressors` maps each arm prefix to a built-in tumour-suppressor panel (17p→TP53 · 13q→RB1 **and** BRCA2 · 9p→CDKN2A · 10q→PTEN · 17q→BRCA1, NCBI Gene cytobands). A single-copy loss (`−1`, heterozygous, CN ≥ 1) is NOT a homozygous deletion. The loss-side counterpart of the amplification unit [[focal-amplification-detection]] (`IdentifyDeletedTumorSuppressors` mirrors `IdentifyAmplifiedOncogenes`) and a consumer of [[copy-number-alteration-classification]]'s CN-0 state. Two assumptions (CN-0 reuse, caller-fixed panel); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-003-evidence]].
- [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] — Oncology family, eleventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CTDNA-001): the liquid-biopsy **quantification / limit-of-detection** layer for **circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA)** — the Poisson detection probability `DetectionProbability` **p = 1 − e^(−n·d·k)** (n genome equivalents, d mutant allele fraction, k reporters; Patent US 11,085,084 restating Avanzini 2020, corroborated by Pessoa 2023's λ = n·d = 15) with a detectability test (caller threshold default 0.95 **and** λ = n·d·k ≥ 1; only p is non-assumption), **`CalculateTumorFraction` = 2 × mean clonal-heterozygous VAF** (copy-neutral diploid, CNAqc/Antonello 2024 v = π/2), `CalculateMeanVaf` = mean altReads/totalReads across reporters (Newman 2014 CAPP-Seq across-reporter fraction, detection 0.025%–10%), and a genome-equivalents helper (3.3 pg/haploid, Devonshire 2014 ⇒ ≈303 GE/ng, Alcaide 2020). The **quantification counterpart** on the same cfDNA input as the biological-origin filter [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] (measures signal vs filters it), sharing the diploid-heterozygous VAF inversion with [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] / [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]]; underpins MRD monitoring; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ctdna-001-evidence]].
- [[driver-gene-classification-20-20-rule]] — Oncology family, twelfth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-DRIVER-001): the **gene-level** driver classifier — the Vogelstein 2013 **20/20 rule** classifying a cancer gene **Oncogene** (> 20% missense at **recurrent** positions, ≥ 2× = activating), **TumorSuppressor** (> 20% **truncating / inactivating** — nonsense / frameshift / splice donor-acceptor / stop gain-loss = loss of function), or **Ambiguous** (neither criterion, or exact dual-pass tie), via `IdentifyDriverMutations` (driver ⊆ somatic) + `MatchCancerHotspots` (caller-supplied (gene, position) hotspot set) + `ScoreDriverPotential` (= max of the two criterion fractions in [0,1]; CADD/SIFT/PolyPhen are caller-supplied, not implemented). Oracles: IDH1 10 missense@codon 132 → recurrent-missense 1.00 → Oncogene; dispersed 8/10 truncating → 0.80 → TumorSuppressor; truncating exactly 0.20 → NOT TSG (strict `>`). A **heuristic, not a statistical test** (passenger truncations / low-recurrence drivers mislead it; 20/20+ / MutSigCV successors out of scope), **orthogonal** to the variant-level clinical classifiers [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] and [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]. Three assumptions (strict `> 0.20`, dual-pass tie-break by larger fraction with Ambiguous on tie, ScoreDriverPotential proxy); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-driver-001-evidence]].
- [[expression-outlier-zscore-signature-score]] — Oncology family, thirteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-EXPR-001), and the wiki's **first expression/transcriptome method**: the per-gene **outlier z-score** `z = (r − μ)/σ` against a caller-supplied **reference (base) population** (cBioPortal's diploid or all-samples convention) with **σ = sample SD, divisor (n − 1)** (settled by `NormalizeExpressionLevels.java`), classified over/under-expressed under the **strict ±2** default threshold (exactly ±2 is NOT an outlier), plus the **combined-z signature/pathway activity** `a = (Σᵢ zᵢ)/√k` (Lee et al. 2008, the GSVA `zscore` method). Zero-SD reference **throws** (reference-code `fatalError`, a behavioural deviation from the prose "z ← NA" spec — the two cBioPortal sources disagree); reference `{2,2,4,6,6}` → σ=2 so x=10→3.0 over / x=8→2.0 boundary-not-outlier / x=4→0.0 / x=−1→−2.5 under, signature `{3,1,−1,1}`→2.0 & single-gene `{2.5}`→2.5 oracles. **Orthogonal** to the copy-number / clonal-structure ONCO units ([[copy-number-alteration-classification]], [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]]) — the diploid reference option touches copy number only as an input filter. Two scope assumptions (caller-supplied cohort + signature; inputs pre-normalized) + one behavioural deviation (throw not NA); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-expr-001-evidence]].
- [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] — Oncology family, fourteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-001), and the wiki's **first gene-fusion / read-evidence structural-rearrangement method**: the STAR-Fusion / Arriba **split-read + discordant-pair + minimum-support** candidate-fusion caller (BCR-ABL1 / EML4-ALK / TMPRSS2-ERG). **DETECTED** iff (junction ≥ `MIN_JUNCTION_READS`=1 AND total ≥ `MIN_SUM_FRAGS`=2) OR (zero junction AND discordant ≥ `MIN_SPANNING_FRAGS_ONLY`=5), where **total support = split_reads1 + split_reads2 + discordant_mates** (Arriba) and the **gene5p ≠ gene3p** distinct-gene invariant rejects self-fusions; results ordered by descending support (STAR-Fusion scores by "abundance of fusion-supporting reads"). Plus a standalone **exon-phase in-frame** check `(5' coding bases − 3' start phase) mod 3 == 0` (Genomics England / Wikipedia Reading-frame). Oracles: EML4-ALK(3,2,4)/TMPRSS2-ERG(1,0,1)/CD74-ROS1(0,0,5) DETECTED, NCOA4-RET(0,0,4) span<5 / KIF5B-RET(1,0,0) sum<2 / ALK-ALK same-gene REJECTED, frame 300/0→in 301/0→out 301/1→in. Consumes **already-grouped candidate breakpoint counts** (Arriba schema, not raw BAM — chimeric-read extraction is a separate `FindChimericReads`) and does **not** scan for a premature stop before the junction (Arriba `stop-codon` value, ONCO-FUSION-003 scope). **Orthogonal** to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units, distinct from the gene-order [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]. Two scope assumptions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-001-evidence]].
- [[gene-fusion-nomenclature-known-fusion-lookup]] — Oncology family, fifteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-002), the wiki's fusion **annotation/naming** method: the **HGNC gene-fusion designation** `GetFusionAnnotation(5p,3p) = "5p::3p"` (Bruford et al. 2021 — `::` double-colon separator, **5′-partner-first** directional order irrespective of chromosomal location, HGNC approved symbols, read-throughs keep the hyphen `INS-IGF2`) plus the **directional known-fusion match** `MatchKnownFusions` against a **caller-supplied** set keyed by `5′::3′`, case-insensitive. A **Framework** algorithm — format/keying source-backed (Bruford 2021 + consortium extension letter), set contents caller-supplied (no bundled Mitelman/COSMIC/ChimerDB). `BCR::ABL1` worked example; `A::B ≠ B::A` reciprocal-direction and hyphen ≠ `::` corner cases; null/empty rejected. The **naming layer downstream** of the read-evidence caller [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] (annotation round-trips through a `DetectFusions` `FusionCall`), distinct from the ONCO-FUSION-003 premature-stop scope; orthogonal to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units. Two assumptions (caller-supplied set, case-insensitivity); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-002-evidence]].
- [[fusion-breakpoint-frame-and-protein-prediction]] — Oncology family, sixteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-003), the **protein-consequence** third member of the fusion trio: given a fusion breakpoint it computes the **four-state** `BreakpointFrameStatus` (`InFrame`/`OutOfFrame`/`StopCodon`/`NotPredicted`) and reconstructs the **fusion protein**. Follows **Arriba's two-way** native-frame model (Uhrig 2021 `reading_frame`/`site` columns) — the in/out call is whether the 3′ gene is read in its NATIVE frame via the exon-phase rule `(5' coding bases − 3' start phase) mod 3 == 0` (reused from [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] ONCO-FUSION-001) — deliberately **not** AGFusion's three-way class (`in-frame (with mutation)`, contiguous ORF multiple-of-3 but 3′ frameshifted, maps to **`OutOfFrame`**). Gated by breakpoint-site classification: a breakpoint in UTR/intron/non-coding-exon/intergenic → `NotPredicted`. `PredictFusionProtein` follows AGFusion `model.py` exactly: 5′ CDS prefix + 3′ CDS suffix → concatenate → translate (transl_table=1) → **truncate at first stop** (out-of-frame trims to whole codons first). Oracles `ATGAAA|GATGGT`→`MKDG`, `ATGAAA|GATTAAGGT`→`MKD` (in-frame premature stop), `ATGA|AAGGT` phase-0→`OutOfFrame` yet clean `MKG` (the Arriba-vs-AGFusion divergence point) / phase-1→in-frame, `ATGAA|GATGGT`→trim-to-9 `MKM`. Downstream of ONCO-FUSION-001 (elaborates its binary in-frame check into a full consequence + transcript/peptide reconstruction, the premature-stop scope both siblings deferred here), orthogonal to the naming unit [[gene-fusion-nomenclature-known-fusion-lookup]] and to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units. One API-shape assumption (caller supplies CDS strings + junction offsets, no bundled GTF); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-003-evidence]].
- [[intratumor-heterogeneity-metrics]] — Oncology family, seventeenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HETERO-001): the **scalar-summary ITH-metric layer** that reduces the reconstructed clonal structure to comparable numbers — the **MATH score** `100·1.4826·median(|VAF−median VAF|)/median(VAF)` (Mroz & Rocco 2013 / Mroz 2015 / maftools `mathScore.R`, three-way identical; the ratio of the width to the centre of the mutant-allele-fraction distribution, no clustering needed), the **Shannon clonal diversity** `H = −Σ pᵢ ln pᵢ` (natural log, Liu 2017 / Shannon 1948), the **subclone count** (Liu richness = number of occupied CCF clusters), and the **subclonal fraction** `#(CCF<0.95)/n` (Landau 2013 threshold). MATH oracles 49.42 (odd) / 59.304 (even); Shannon 0 / ln2 / ln4; zero-median-VAF→throw, MAD=0→MATH=0. **Depends on** [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] (subclone count + Shannon pᵢ consume its CCF clusters) and reuses the 0.95 clonal threshold of [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]]; a summary layer, NOT per-mutation reconstruction; shares the Shannon-index math but not the domain with [[alpha-diversity]]. Two source-consistent assumptions (Shannon pᵢ = per-cluster mutation proportions; R even-count median); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hetero-001-evidence]].
- [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] — Oncology family, eighteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HLA-001), the wiki's **first HLA / immuno-oncology antigen-presentation method**: two disjoint pieces sharing the HLA locus — (1) **HLA allele nomenclature parsing/validation** of the WHO IPD-IMGT/HLA name `HLA-[Gene]*[F1]:[F2][:F3][:F4][suffix]` (Marsh 2010 colon-delimited convention; Field1 type/allele-group / Field2 specific protein / Field3 synonymous / Field4 non-coding; **two-field "four-digit" minimum**, four-field maximum, `HLA-` prefix required, numeric fields, `N/L/S/C/A/Q` expression-suffix set — `HLA-A*24:02:01:02L` valid, `HLA-A*02`/`A*02:01`/five-fields/`…X` rejected), and (2) **allele-specific HLA LOH** by the **LOHHLA** rule (McGranahan 2017 *Cell* / `mskcc/lohhla`): per-allele copy number from tumor-vs-germline logR + BAF, call HLA LOH iff min copy number **< 0.5** AND allelic-imbalance paired Student's t-test **p < 0.01** — both strict `<`, the p-test the explicit "avoid over-calling LOH" guard; oracles (1.8, 0.30, 0.001)→LOH allele 2 / (1.60, 0.40, 0.05)→no (p≥0.01) / (1.50, 0.50, 0.001)→no (0.5 not <0.5) / (1.70, 0.40, 0.01)→no (0.01 not <0.01); the **HLA-locus specialization** of the genome-wide allele-specific copy-number / LOH derivation [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (same logR + BAF allelic-contrast idea restricted to the HLA genes), a mechanism of immune escape via lost neoantigen presentation; one assumption (both alleles <0.5 → distinct `HomozygousLoss` label, thresholds unchanged); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hla-001-evidence]].
- [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] — Oncology family, nineteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HRD-001): the **HRD composite genomic-scar score** `HRD = LOH + TAI + LST`, an **unweighted sum** of three large-scale copy-number scar counts with the **HRD-high cutoff ≥ 42** inclusive (Telli 2016 + Stewart 2022, independently corroborated). All three components **derived per segment** from the [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] major/minor CN substrate in `DetectHRD(segments)`: **HRD-LOH** = LOH regions > 15 Mb & < whole chromosome, excluding whole-chr-LOH chromosomes (Abkevich 2012 / oncoscanR / scarHRD `calc.hrd.R`, no centromere table needed); **TAI** = imbalanced (major ≠ minor CN) segments reaching a sub-telomere but not crossing the centromere (Birkbak 2012 / scarHRD `calc.ai_new.R`, sub-1 Mb dropped, single-segment whole-chr imbalance excluded); **LST** = adjacent ≥ 10 Mb same-arm regions separated by < 3 Mb after iterative 3 Mb smoothing (Popova 2012 / scarHRD `calc.lst.R`, autosomes only). TAI + LST need the per-chromosome centromere `[start,end]` **acen** table embedded for GRCh38/GRCh37 (UCSC cytoBand cross-verified vs NCBI GRC — resolving the prior "centromere table unretrievable" blocker). Oracles (14,14,14)→42 HRD-high / (14,13,14)→41 negative / (0,0,0)→0. The genomic-scar aggregation layer above [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]], distinct from the total-CN [[aneuploidy-detection]]; one even-ploidy AI-path assumption; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hrd-001-evidence]].
- [[immune-infiltration-deconvolution]] — Oncology family, twentieth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-IMMUNE-001), the wiki's **second expression/transcriptome method**: **immune infiltration estimation** — quantifies the tumor immune microenvironment two ways. (1) **Cell-type deconvolution** of the linear mixture `m = S·f` (Σf=1, f≥0): CIBERSORT **ν-SVR** `DeconvoluteImmuneCellsNuSvr` (Newman 2015 / Schölkopf 2000 linear-kernel ν-SVR — z-standardize m + signature columns, sweep ν∈{0.25,0.5,0.75} by **lowest RMSE**, zero-clip negatives + normalize to Σ=1; cross-validated by planted-truth `m=S·f` recovery + scikit-learn `NuSVR`/libsvm match) with the NNLS/LLSR baseline `DeconvoluteImmuneCells` (Abbas 2009) retained. (2) **ESTIMATE** ssGSEA immune/stromal enrichment `EstimateInfiltration` (**simplified** = rank-weighted mean of signature genes, not full KS running-sum) + opt-in **tumor purity** `EstimateTumorPurity` = `cos(0.6049872018 + 0.0001467884·ESTIMATE)` (verbatim, confirmed 3 sources + tidyestimate R; **Affymetrix-only** calibration, negative cosine → **NaN**, monotone-decreasing). MCP-counter geometric-mean marker abundance noted. Signature matrices: **LM22** (547 genes × 22 cell types) **caller-supplied** — Stanford licence forbids redistribution/modification/commercial use, no exact-CIBERSORT parity claim, `LoadSignatureMatrix` LM22-format loader only; **ABIS-Seq** (Monaco 2019, CC BY 4.0, 1296 genes × 17 types) **bundled** as embedded resource via `LoadBundledAbisSignatureMatrix` so deconvolution works out-of-the-box (not an LM22 substitute); synthetic 5-marker `DefaultSignatureMatrix` for tests. Oracles: planted {CD8 0.60,B_naive 0.30,Mono 0.10}→{0.5971,0.2989,0.1040} corr 0.99997; sklearn cross-check ν=0.75 {A 0.5085,B 0.1795,C 0.3120}; ABIS {NK 0.60,MonoC 0.40}→{≈0.650,≈0.350} corr 0.996 (tol 0.06) & pure MonoC 1.0 exactly; ABIS ref `CD8A`/T CD8 Mem=1060.1507652944399. Corner cases: collinear cell types (resting/activated NK) recover support but looser proportions; missing/non-overlapping genes → unreliable/zero; non-hematopoietic content in residual; ESTIMATE solid-tumors-only. Antigen-agnostic quantitative sibling of the immuno-oncology [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]], shares the ssGSEA signature-scoring layer with [[expression-outlier-zscore-signature-score]]; two scope assumptions (LM22 caller-supplied, simplified ssGSEA) + Affymetrix purity domain, no contradictions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-immune-001-evidence]].
- [[loss-of-heterozygosity-detection]] — Oncology family, twenty-first ONCO-* unit (ONCO-LOH-001): the standalone genome-wide **LOH caller** — `DetectLOH` counts **HRD-LOH** regions (minor CN 0 **and** major CN ≠ 0 = allelic loss not homozygous deletion; length **strictly > 15 Mb**, length = end − start; excluding any **whole-chromosome** global-LOH chromosome via `chrDel`) and `CalculateLOHFraction` returns the length-weighted per-chromosome LOH fraction ∈ [0,1]. Abkevich 2012 (intermediate-size LOH ↔ BRCA1/2 deficiency) + scarHRD `calc.hrd.R`/`scar_score.R` (exact R criterion + 15 Mb cut-off + `chrDel`; major CN capped to 1 so LOH state, not absolute CN, drives merging) + oncoscanR `score_loh` (independent corroboration; adjacent/overlapping LOH merged ≤ 1 bp first). Synthetic 7-segment dataset → score **1** (only the 20 Mb chr1 segment; exactly-15 Mb / het-retained / homozygous-deletion / whole-chr-LOH all excluded); LOH-fraction 0.333/0.0/1.0. This **is** the LOH term the composite [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] sums with TAI + LST (centromere-free, unlike its siblings), reads its segments off [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]], and is the genome-wide counterpart of the HLA-locus [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (LOHHLA). Two assumptions (segment input shape; length-weighted LOH-fraction is a definitional/API choice); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-loh-001-evidence]].
- [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] — Oncology family, twenty-second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MHC-001): the wiki's first **MHC / peptide-presentation prediction** method — the affinity gate of neoantigen candidate scoring, three layers over one `Strong`/`Weak`/`NonBinder` output. (1) **Classification**: IC50 tiers `< 50` Strong / `< 500` Weak / `≥ 500` NonBinder (Sette 1994 ≈ 500 nM CTL threshold + IEDB) and NetMHCpan-4.1 %Rank tiers (class I SB `< 0.5` / WB `< 2`, class II `< 2` / `< 10`, all strict `<`; Reynisson 2020), + peptide-length validity (class I **8–14**, class II 13–25). (2) **Matrix prediction**: BIMAS **product rule** (T½ = const · ∏ coeffs, 180 coeffs + const, unlisted = 1.0; Parker 1994) and SMM **additive** rule `IC50 = 50000^(1−score)` (Peters & Sette 2005 / IEDB log50k; 0→50000, 0.5→223.6068, 1→1 nM). (3) Ported **MHCflurry 2.0** pan-allele class-I NN (BLOSUM62 `left_pad_centered_right_pad` 45×21 peptide + 37-residue allele pseudosequence 37×21, `tanh` Dense `feedforward`/`with-skip-connections`, `to_ic50 = 50000^(1−x)`, geometric-mean ensemble; matches `mhcflurry` 2.1.5 to < 0.03 %). **Framework/packaging** — trained matrices caller-supplied (BIMAS CGI defunct / Parker paywalled / IEDB non-commercial) and 80 MB ensemble not embedded (one member for CI + `LoadWeightPack`), explicitly analogized in-file to CIBERSORT LM22 of [[immune-infiltration-deconvolution]]. Downstream of neoantigen generation [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]] (ONCO-NEO-001), presentation-machinery sibling of [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (HLA LOH removes the platform); class I 8–14 resolved vs NetMHCpan-4.1; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-mhc-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-informed-mrd-detection]] — Oncology family, twenty-third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MRD-001): the liquid-biopsy **MRD calling / statistical-detection** layer that `depends_on` and reuses the Poisson quantification primitive [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] (ONCO-CTDNA-001). Two engines. (1) **Signatera positivity** (`DetectMRD`): tumor-informed workflow — up to 16 WES-selected clonal somatic SNVs tracked in plasma cfDNA — **MRD-positive iff ≥ 2 of the 16 tracked variants are detected** (Reinert 2019 / PMC9265001 Table 1; 0/1→negative, 2/3→positive), panel Poisson `p = 1 − e^(−nfm)`, sensitivity scales with panel size (>8 markers at ≤0.1% VAF, LoD 0.01% / specificity >99.5%; post-op ctDNA+ → HR 7.2 relapse), longitudinal `TrackVariantsOverTime` (per-timepoint + first-positive). (2) **INVAR GLRT** (Wan 2020 + INVAR2 verbatim): per-locus mixture `q = p·g + e(1−p)`, EM ctDNA-fraction, `LR = logL(p̂) − logL(0)` (pure background → p̂≈0/LR≈0; AF/SNR-weighted, monotone), `IntegratedMutantAlleleFractionV2` background-subtracted depth-weighted, fragment-size-weighted GLRT (`EstimateInvarSignalWithSize`/`FragmentSizeProfile`/`InvarMolecule`; discrete `COUNT/TOTAL` default + opt-in Gaussian-KDE `FromKernelDensity`; flat P1==P0 → reduces to no-size), outlier suppression `SuppressOutlierLoci` (repolish binomial + Bonferroni), control-derived background `EstimateLocusBackground`/`PassesBothStrandsFilter`.
