Distinct from ONCO-CTDNA-001 (multi-variant verdict vs single-reporter probability); one flagged per-variant "detected"=≥1 alt read assumption (tunable); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-mrd-001-evidence]].
- [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] — Oncology family, twenty-fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MSI-001): the **microsatellite-instability biomarker** — MSI from unstable-loci fraction + status classification. Two inputs, two classifiers. (1) **Continuous MSI score** = `unstable loci / valid loci` (as %) with **MSI-High cutoff ≥ 20%** inclusive (MSIsensor2 niu-lab README verbatim; per-site **chi-square** tumor-vs-normal repeat-length test at **FDR 0.05**, score = "% sites with a somatic indel", Niu 2014; tumor-only mode unchanged; the original cohort's **3.5%** separation is dataset-specific, not the production cutoff) → classified **binary** MSI-H (≥20%) vs not-High only. (2) **Categorical Bethesda** marker-count over the validated 5-marker panel (BAT-25/BAT-26/D2S123/D5S346/D17S250): **0/5→MSS · 1/5→MSI-L · ≥2/5→MSI-H** (Boland 1998, cross-checked vs the 2004 revised-Bethesda ≥40% / ≥20%&<40% fraction form BJC 2014). Key modelling choice: **no MSI-L band is fabricated for the continuous score** — the three-way MSS/MSI-L/MSI-H scheme applies only to the discrete marker count. Oracles 5/25→20%→MSI-H(boundary) · 4/25→16%→not-High · 0/25→0%→MSS-range; corner cases zero-valid-loci→undefined(throws) · unstable>valid/negative→throws · MSS-vs-MSI-L 1-marker low-confidence. An independent immunotherapy/mismatch-repair biomarker orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]], consumed by [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-msi-001-evidence]].
- [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]] — Oncology family, twenty-fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-NEO-001): the **upstream partner** of the affinity gate [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] — **neoantigen candidate peptide window generation** (`GenerateNeoantigenPeptides`). Given a somatic **missense SNV** at 1-based position `p` in a protein of length `L`, enumerate **every length-`k` window of the mutant protein that spans the mutated residue** (valid 0-based start `s ∈ [max(0, p−1−k+1), min(p−1, L−k)]`, count `= last − first + 1`; an interior mutation gives exactly `k` windows per length), each paired with its matched **wild-type (germline)** peptide at the same coordinates + the mutation offset — the mutant/WT **agretope** on which the differential agretopic index (DAI, Wells 2020 TESLA) is computed. Class I search lengths **8–11** (pVACtools Hundal 2020; a 21-mer with the substitution centred = ProGeo-neo Li 2020's ±10-flank construction contains exactly every overlapping 8–11-mer; NetMHCpan 8–14 / 9-mer-dominant Jurtz 2017 motivates enumerating 8–11 not 9 alone). Oracles: interior **Y5C** on `MKTAYIAKQRSTVWLNDEFGH` → 5 windows per k = 8/9/10/11 → **20** candidates (each WT = mutant with `C`→`Y` at the offset); **terminal M1V** k = 9 → exactly 1 truncated window `VKTAYIAKQ`/`MKTAYIAKQ` offset 0; corner cases non-coding/synonymous → no peptide, length outside 8–11 not enumerated, short-protein skips that `k`. **Missense-only** (frameshift/indel/fusion neopeptides out of scope, separate translation) and **binding affinity out of scope** (IC50/%Rank scoring caller-supplied via the downstream [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] ONCO-MHC-001 gate, whose resolved class I 8–14 window propagates to this generator's default); presentation-platform sibling [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (HLA LOH removes the restricted allele). Two source-backed scoping assumptions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-neo-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] — Oncology family, twenty-sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PHYLO-001): the **clonal-tree reconstruction** layer — assemble per-cluster **cancer cell fractions (CCF)** into a rooted **clonal-evolution tree**, deciding parent→child descent via two per-sample CCF-ordering constraints from **LICHeE** (Popic 2015) and **PICTograph** (Zheng 2022): **lineage precedence** (ancestor CCF ≥ descendant CCF − ε per sample, + presence pattern `u.CCF=0 ⇒ v.CCF=0`; LICHeE Eq. 2) and the **sum rule** (children CCF sum ≤ parent CCF + ε per node — the cell-fraction **pigeonhole generalization**; LICHeE Eq. 5 / PICTograph sum condition — what forces **branching vs nesting**), plus **trunk** (CCF-≈1 root-path clusters = clonal) vs **branch** (subclones) identification. A **constraint-satisfaction / perfect-phylogeny** builder, **not** distance-based Neighbor-Joining / UPGMA. Oracles: linear Normal→A→B→C (1.0/1.0/0.6/0.3, Trunk {A}); two-sample branching A→{B,C} (B 0.6/0.0, C 0.0/0.7 — each private, absent in the other's sample, so mutually non-ancestral; sum under A per sample 0.6 & 0.7 ≤ 1.0); equal 0.6/0.6 siblings forced into a chain Normal→A→B→C by the sum rule (0.6+0.6=1.2 > 1.0). Two reconstructed-tree **invariants** as oracles (ancestor CCF ≥ descendant per edge; per-node sum rule); empty→root-only, single cluster→trunk. **Downstream of** the CCF clustering [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] (ONCO-CCF-001, which produces the clusters it orders), the structural counterpart of the per-mutation trunk↔clonal / branch↔subclonal [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]], and the structure the heterogeneity metrics [[intratumor-heterogeneity-metrics]] summarize. Two source-consistent assumptions (deepest-valid-ancestor deterministic tie-break; default ε=0 strict inequalities); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-phylo-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-ploidy-estimation-and-whole-genome-doubling]] — Oncology family, twenty-seventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PLOIDY-001): two **post-hoc genome-state summaries** over already-called allele-specific segments (shared `AlleleSpecificSegment` = Major+Minor CN, not raw logR/BAF): (1) **average ploidy** `EstimatePloidy` = length-weighted mean total CN **ψ = Σ(CN_i·L_i)/Σ(L_i)** (Patchwork PMC4053982; n-scale Van Loo 2010, pure diploid → 2.0, >2.7n aneuploidy; CN 2/4/3 at 100/100/50 Mb → 3.0, genuinely length-weighted not plain segment mean); (2) **whole-genome doubling** `DetectWholeGenomeDoubling` = facets-suite `is_genome_doubled` / Bielski 2018 rule — WGD iff **autosome-restricted fraction at major CN ≥ 2 strictly > 0.5** (`mcn = tcn − lcn`; major not total CN, so all-1:1 → not doubled), denominator = **reference chromosome-size table** (`ReferenceGenome {GRCh38,GRCh37}`, UCSC hg38/hg19 Ensembl-verified, Σchr1–22 = 2,875,001,522 / 2,881,033,286 bp) NOT supplied segments, autosomes only (sex chromosomes excluded); half+1→true / exactly-half→false (strict) / 100 Mb amp→0.035 false / chrX-only→false oracles, legacy `DetectWholeGenomeDoublingFromSuppliedLength` keeps the supplied-length denominator (60%→true/50%→false). **Distinct from** the joint grid fit [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (ONCO-ASCAT-001 *fits* ρ/ψ from raw logR/BAF; this *summarizes* ψ post-segmentation), reads the same segment substrate as [[loss-of-heterozygosity-detection]] / [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]]. Two assumptions (input shape; resolved reference-genome WGD denominator); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ploidy-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-purity-from-mutation-vaf]] — Oncology family, twenty-eighth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PURITY-001): a **standalone closed-form tumor-purity estimator** that inverts the **CNAqc expected-VAF generative model** `v = m·π·c/[2(1−π)+π(n_A+n_B)]` (Antonello 2024) to recover purity π from a somatic-SNV VAF + local allele-specific copy number: `EstimatePurityFromVAF` = the copy-neutral diploid heterozygous special case **π = 2·VAF** (clonal c=1, het m=1, n_tot=2; VAF 0.30→0.60, band 0.55–0.65↔VAF 0.275–0.325, invariant 0≤π≤1) and `EstimatePurity` = the general inversion `π = 2v/(m·c + 2v − v·n_tot)` recovering π=1 on a 2:1 (n_tot=3) segment for both m=1 (v=1/3) and m=2 (v=2/3). The `2(1−π)+π·n_tot` denominator (normal diploid weighted 1−π + tumour) is confirmed by **FACETS** (Shen & Seshan 2016) and inverted the other way by **ABSOLUTE** (Carter 2012). Corner cases: multiplicity ambiguity on amplified segments (two VAF peaks 1/3, 2/3 — need CN state + m), subclonal c<1 depresses VAF (use **clonal** mutations or underestimate purity), purity <0.1 below detection, no informative variants → undefined. **`alternative_to`** the joint logR/BAF grid fit [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (ONCO-ASCAT-001 — same purity scalar, different substrate + method), mutation-VAF counterpart to the ploidy-side [[tumor-ploidy-estimation-and-whole-genome-doubling]], shares the diploid `π=2·VAF` inversion with [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]]. Two modelling-scope assumptions (copy-neutral-diploid default, median cross-variant aggregation); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-purity-001-evidence]].
- [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] — Oncology family, twenty-ninth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-001): the wiki's first **mutational-signature** method — the **SBS-96 trinucleotide context catalog**, the classification step that builds the 96-channel single-base-substitution spectrum downstream signature fitting decomposes. A **channel** = a substitution + its centred trinucleotide context: **6** subtypes named by the **pyrimidine** of the mutated Watson–Crick pair (`C>A/C>G/C>T/T>A/T>C/T>G`) **× 4** 5′ bases **× 4** 3′ bases = **96**, labelled `5'[REF>ALT]3'` (COSMIC SBS96 + SigProfilerMatrixGenerator Bergstrom 2019 + Alexandrov 2013, identical 6×4×4 definition). The defining rule is **pyrimidine-strand folding**: a **purine (A/G) reference** base is reverse-complemented (context via A↔T/C↔G then reverse, plus the substitution) onto the pyrimidine strand before counting; a C/T reference classifies to itself, centre unchanged. Worked fold TGA/G→T → revcomp TCA + G>T→C>A → `T[C>A]A`; oracles A,C,A,A→A[C>A]A · G,T,C,A→G[T>C]A · A,A,T,A→T[T>A]T. Catalog **partition** invariants: exactly 96 canonical keys, Σ per-channel counts = number of classifiable SBS variants. Corner cases: purine-ref must fold (never counted directly), non-SBS variants (indels/DBS) excluded, non-ACGT context unclassifiable, ref==alt out of scope. **Catalog/classification only** — the NMF/NNLS signature-exposure fitting against COSMIC reference signatures is a separate downstream concern. A somatic-mutation-spectrum biomarker orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] and the mismatch-repair [[microsatellite-instability-detection]]; one cosmetic label-rendering assumption; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-001-evidence]].
- [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] — Oncology family, thirtieth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-002): the **downstream signature-deconvolution** partner of the catalog [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] (which it `depends_on`) — decompose the 96-channel SBS spectrum into **signatures × exposures** two ways. **Supervised refit** by **non-negative least squares** `min_x ‖S·x−d‖₂², x≥0` (MutationalPatterns/deconstructSigs; Lawson-Hanson active-set — clamp any would-be-negative coefficient to 0 and refit, S=[[1,1],[0,1]], d=[0,1]→x=[0,0.5]; reconstruction `S·x`, **cosine ≥ 0.95** quality gate, raw counts + proportion `x/Σx` exposures). **Unsupervised de-novo extraction** by **NMF** `V ≈ WH` (Lee & Seung multiplicative updates, **Frobenius** default + **KL/Poisson** enhancement, both **monotonically non-increasing**; Alexandrov blind-source-separation W=signatures/H=exposures; COSMIC **L1-normalize** each W column to 1). Shared **cosine similarity** `A·B/(‖A‖‖B‖)∈[0,1]` (identical→1, orthogonal→0, [1,1]/[1,0]→1/√2, scale-invariant, **zero-norm→0.0** by convention). **Rank selection** = Brunet-2004 **cophenetic correlation** (consensus of argmax-over-H connectivity matrices; rank-1 trivially 1.0) + SigProfiler **silhouette stability**; **reference matching** = greedy best-cosine to COSMIC. Sharp edges: NMF **non-convex → local minimum** (planted-truth + fixed-seed recovery only), **permutation/scale ambiguity**, ε-guarded denominators. The NNLS refit and NMF extraction are `alternative_to` each other over the same `V ≈ WH` model; the fitted exposure profile feeds the clinical-interpretation ONCO units, orthogonal to [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] / [[microsatellite-instability-detection]]; five modelling assumptions (Frobenius, seeded init, proportions, zero-cosine, consensus/silhouette/greedy matching); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-002-evidence]].
- [[signature-exposure-bootstrap-confidence-intervals]] — Oncology family, thirty-first ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-003): the **signature-exposure uncertainty** layer over the NNLS refit [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] (which it `depends_on`) — a **resample → refit → percentile** loop that turns the point-estimate exposure vector into a **per-signature confidence interval**. Resample the 96-channel catalog `R` times (default 1000; sigminer ≥100), re-run the ONCO-SIG-002 **NNLS** `FitSignatures` per replicate, and report the **[2.5%, 97.5%] percentiles** (Efron 1979 percentile CI) read off the finite bootstrap sample by the **type-7** quantile (Hyndman & Fan 1996, `h=p·(n−1)`, R/NumPy default). **Two resampling schemes** differing only by whether total burden N is fixed: **multinomial** (sigminer `sample(...,prob=catalog/Σ)` = fixed-N multinomial(N,p), the byte-for-byte **default**) vs **Poisson** (Senkin 2021 MSA variant, each channel `Poisson(observedₖ)`, N unfixed, justified by the Poisson↔multinomial conditional equivalence). The **discriminating** corner case is a single non-zero channel: multinomial **collapses deterministically** (width 0, point=mean=lower=upper) while **Poisson(λ>0) fluctuates** (variance=mean → positive width — the reason the Poisson variant was added); plus N=0→[0,0] and R=1→lower=upper=mean. Invariants Lower≤Mean≤Upper, exposures ≥0 (NNLS), fixed-seed determinism; type-7 oracles [0,1,2,3,4]→0.1/2.0/3.9 and [2,4,6,8]→2.15/5.0/7.85. The uncertainty layer two steps above the [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] spectrum; two source-aligned assumptions (type-7 interpolation, fixed seed 42); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-003-evidence]].
- [[mutational-process-classification]] — Oncology family, thirty-second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-004): the **aetiology-annotation** layer over the fit [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] (which it `depends_on`) — turn per-signature **exposures** into a set of **active mutational processes** via **normalize → cutoff → map → aggregate**. Normalize to relative contributions `Wᵢ = exposureᵢ/Σexposure` (deconstructSigs "weights between 0 and 1"); drop any `Wᵢ < 0.06` (the deconstructSigs `signature.cutoff = 0.06` / `weights[weights < signature.cutoff] <- 0`, **strict `<`** so exactly 0.06 is retained, empirically 1.4% false-negative rate); map each surviving COSMIC label to its **proposed aetiology** (SBS1/5→**Aging** clock-like, SBS2/13→**APOBEC**, SBS4→**Tobacco**, SBS7a–d→**UV**, SBS6/15/20/26→**MMR deficiency**; COSMIC + Alexandrov 2020); **sum** member contributions per process → **active-process set** + `argmax` **dominant process**. Worked oracle SBS2/13/1/4 = 50/30/15/5 (Σ=100) → APOBEC 0.80 (dominant) / Aging 0.15 / Tobacco 0 (SBS4 0.05 below cutoff). Corner cases: surviving mass can sum < 1 (rest "unknown"), several processes reported simultaneously, an unmapped or "Unknown"-aetiology label contributes to no process (SBS5's aetiology is literally "Unknown (clock-like)" yet grouped as Aging), Σ=0 → no active/dominant process, custom `signature.cutoff` overridable. The interpretation layer answering "**which processes are active?**" one step above ONCO-SIG-002's "how much of each signature?" and ONCO-SIG-003's "how confident?"; orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] and mismatch-repair [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] (whose MMR signal SBS6/15/20/26 echo here as a signature-based read), feeds [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; two source-aligned assumptions (per-process summation, per-signature-cutoff-then-group); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-004-evidence]].
- [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] — Oncology family, thirty-third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SOMATIC-001): the **foundational somatic SNV caller** at the head of the pipeline — classify each candidate variant **Somatic / Germline / NotDetected** by comparing **tumor allele frequency `f_t`** against **matched-normal `f_n`** (`VAF = altReads/totalReads`). Strelka's somatic state `S = {(f_t,f_n): f_t≠f_n}` restricted to a **ref/ref normal genotype** (Saunders 2012; the raw somatic probability over-calls in LOH/CN regions) / Strelka2 continuous-VAF somatic-LOD+VAF comparison (Kim 2018). **Three configurable thresholds**: tumor **LoD f_t ≥ 0.05** (Yan 2021 WES 5% LoD, ≤5% frequently sequencing errors → NotDetected), normal **"absent" ceiling f_n ≤ 0.01** (`normalVafThreshold`), f_n above ceiling with substantial f_t → **Germline** (Mutect2 germline filter, Benjamin 2019). Bounded monotone **somatic score `max(0, f_t − f_n)` ∈ [0,1]** (a documented simplification, not a caller LOD). **Tumor-only mode**: no matched normal → Mutect2 `ℓ_n = 1`, tumor-only call; `FilterGermlineVariants` returns the somatic **subset** of input. Oracles A 0.25/0.00→Somatic(0.25) · B 0.48/0.50→Germline(0) · C 0.02→NotDetected · D CHIP-like 0.30/0.03→Germline · E tumor-only 0.20/(0/0)→Somatic · boundaries f_t=0.05 present / f_n=0.01 absent. The **upstream caller** whose raw call set the two pre-interpretation QC filters clean — technical-artifact [[sequencing-artifact-detection]] + biological-origin [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] — before the clinical-significance units; two flagged source-consistent assumptions (1% normal ceiling parameterized not invented; score a documented simplification); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-somatic-001-evidence]].
- [[chromothripsis-inference]] — Oncology family, thirty-fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SV-001), and the wiki's **first complex-rearrangement / chromothripsis** method: a **region-level pattern classifier** that consumes a per-segment integer copy-number profile (+ breakpoints / a clustered-SV count) and classifies **Chromothripsis** vs **NotComplex** by the **Korbel & Campbell 2013** six hallmark criteria, computing two directly — criterion B **oscillating copy-number states** (an oscillation = an adjacent-segment CN-state reversal; profile must alternate between ≤3, canonically **two**, states) gated by the Magrangeas-2011 **≥10 first-pass oscillation screen**, the Cortés-Ciriano-2020 confidence tiers (**≥7** adjacent oscillating segments high / **4–6** low / **<4** not-called), the **>60%** two-state fraction, and the **≥6 clustered intrachromosomal SV** burden floor; and criterion A **breakpoint clustering** via the exponential-null coefficient-of-variation flag (**CV>1**, exponential CV=1). Oracles `2,1,2,1,2,1,2,1,2,1,2`→10 two-state→Chromothripsis · `2,1,2,1,2,1`→5<10→NotComplex · `2,3,4,5,6,7` monotone→0 oscillations/>2 states→NotComplex (progressive amplification/BFB — the "clustering necessary but not sufficient" failure mode). **Consumes** the per-segment CN states of [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) — a pattern classifier over that profile, not a per-segment caller — orthogonal to the single-junction [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] and the length-based [[focal-amplification-detection]], distinct from the gene-order [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]. Two operationalisation assumptions (oscillation = CN-state-transition count; clustering = CV>1 vs exponential null); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sv-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-mutational-burden]] — Oncology family, thirty-fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-TMB-001): the **tumor-agnostic immunotherapy biomarker** — the continuous **TMB = (counted somatic mutations) / (sequenced coding region in Mb)** in mut/Mb (Chalmers 2017 Methods; the assay's **coding footprint** is the denominator — FoundationOne 315-gene = **1.1 Mb**, F1CDx 324-gene ≈ 0.8 Mb, WES ≈ 30–40 Mb, taken as a parameter) and the **TMB-High = TMB ≥ 10 mut/Mb** classification (FDA pembrolizumab tumor-agnostic approval June 16 2020, F1CDx companion diagnostic, Marcus 2021; boundary **inclusive** — 10.0 High, 9.9 not; mut/Mb reporting + cutoff cross-confirmed by the Friends of Cancer Research Harmonization Project, Merino 2020). Panel counting **includes synonymous** alterations to reduce sampling noise while WES counts nonsynonymous; germline/driver filtering happens **upstream** — this unit counts the caller-supplied somatic list of [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] (ONCO-SOMATIC-001). Oracles 11/1.1→10.0 High (315-gene) · 300/30→10.0 High (WES) · 150/10→15.0 High · 99/10→9.9 not-High · 0→not-High; corner cases `targetRegionMb=0`→division-by-zero throws, negative count/region rejected, **<0.5 Mb** panels compute but are known-unstable (documentation, not error), TMB monotone non-decreasing in count / non-increasing in region. An independent immunotherapy biomarker alongside [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] (MSI-H) and correlated with the neoantigen load of [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]], acted on by [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]. **One flagged conflict**: the unsupported registry three-tier "Low <6 / Intermediate 6–20 / High >20" scheme (no authoritative source for the 6/20 boundaries) resolved to the single source-backed two-tier ≥10 cutoff; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-tmb-001-evidence]].
- [[variant-allele-frequency-and-binomial-ci]] — Oncology family, thirty-sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-VAF-001): the **foundational VAF primitive** the VAF-based Oncology family sits on — three model-free quantities. (1) **Empirical VAF = altReads/totalReads** (= alt AD / sum AD, GATK Mutect2 FAQ; the model-free ratio, **not** Mutect2's model-estimate `AF` field). (2) The **Wilson score binomial confidence interval** on the proportion `center=(p̂+z²/2n)/(1+z²/n)`, `margin=(z/(1+z²/n))·√(p̂(1−p̂)/n+z²/4n²)`, **z=1.96** for 95% (Wilson 1927) — the genuinely distinct statistical content **not represented elsewhere**, chosen over **Wald** because it stays within [0,1] with non-zero width at the extremes (`p̂=0`→lower exactly 0 / `p̂=1`→upper exactly 1) where Wald overshoots/collapses. (3) The CNAqc purity/ploidy correction **`AdjustVAFForPurity`** = `m·CCF = VAF·(2(1−π)+π·n_tot)/π` (inverting CNAqc *Genome Biology* 2024 `v=mπ/(2(1−π)+π·n_tot)`, normal ploidy 2). Oracles 25/100→0.25 · 0/10→0.00 · 10/10→1.00, Wilson (25,100)→0.2592 [0.1755,0.3430] & no-overshoot (0,10)→[0,0.2775] / (10,10)→[0.7225,1], correction (0.40,0.80,2)→1.00 / (0.20,0.50,2)→0.80 / (0.30,0.50,4)→1.80; corner cases VAF>1 alignment-artifact/totalReads=0/π=0 all guarded. The empirical VAF is the same `altReads/totalReads` [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] compares and [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] averages; `AdjustVAFForPurity` shares the CNAqc/Tarabichi model [[tumor-purity-from-mutation-vaf]] inverts for π and [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] divides by m for CCF; two source-backed assumptions (z=1.96 verbatim, normal CN=2); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-vaf-001-evidence]].
- [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]] — comparative-genomics pan-genome family anchor (first PANGEN-* unit, PANGEN-CLUSTER-001): greedy incremental homolog/ortholog clustering (`ClusterGenes`) on the CD-HIT model (Li & Godzik 2006) — process genes long→short, assign each to the first existing cluster whose representative it matches at ≥ identity threshold else start a new cluster; global identity = identical aligned positions / alignment length (`-G 1`), Roary default 95% for orthologs (Page 2015); homolog groups only (no gene-neighbourhood/synteny paralog-split step), alignment-free identity may underestimate when internal indels are needed; sibling of [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]] / [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] / [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; upstream of [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]]; deviations None; record [[pangen-cluster-001-evidence]].
- [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]] — comparative-genomics pan-genome family, second PANGEN-* unit (PANGEN-CORE-001): the **pan-genome partition** `ConstructPanGenome` **downstream** of the clustering step — split gene clusters across N genomes into **core / accessory / unique** by cluster **occupancy** with the fractional Roary rule `occupancy/N ≥ coreFraction` ("at least 99% of samples", **not** `floor(coreFraction·N)`; hard core >99% / soft core 95–99% / shell 15–95% / cloud <15%, Page 2015), compute **genomic fluidity** `φ=[2/(N(N−1))]·Σ_{k<l}(U_k+U_l)/(M_k+M_l)` ∈[0,1] (Kislyuk 2011; 0 identical / 1 disjoint; 3-genome oracle 10/18=0.5̄), and classify **open ⟺ alpha<1 / closed ⟺ alpha>1** by the **Heaps'-law** decay exponent (Tettelin 2008, micropan); the N-genome occupancy counterpart of the pairwise-RBH [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]], both the Tettelin 2005 core/dispensable model; downstream of [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]]; two source-backed assumptions (clustering delegated to k-mer-Jaccard `ClusterGenes`, empty-pair fluidity term→0); no contradictions; record [[pangen-core-001-evidence]].
- [[pan-genome-heaps-law-fit]] — comparative-genomics pan-genome family, third PANGEN-* unit (PANGEN-HEAP-001): the **pan-genome growth model** / dedicated **Heaps'-law fitting engine** underneath the partition's open/closed facet — binarize the gene **presence/absence matrix** (count>0→1), extract the **new-gene curve** by the micropan first-appearance rule (a cluster is new at genome i≥2 when cumulative presence is 1 at row i and 0 at row i−1; genome index starts at 2), pool over random orderings (n.perm 100), fit the **power law** `y=K·x^(-alpha)` by bounded least squares `J=sqrt(Σ(y−K·x^(-alpha))²)/|x|` over K∈[0,10000]/alpha∈[0,2] from start `(mean(y at x==2),1)`, classify **open ⟺ alpha<1 / closed ⟺ alpha>1** (micropan verbatim, boundary not-open); exact oracles x=[2,3] y=[8,4]→alpha ln2/ln(3/2)≈1.7095 K≈26.164 closed, constant y=[1,1]→alpha 0 K 1 open, Tettelin 2005 qualitative anchor; the fitting engine whose alpha [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]] reports, consuming the families of [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]]; two assumptions (optimizer method non-correctness-affecting, fixed-seed RNG); no contradictions; record [[pangen-heap-001-evidence]].
- [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] — comparative-genomics pan-genome family, fourth PANGEN-* unit (PANGEN-MARKER-001): **phylogenetic marker selection** `SelectPhylogeneticMarkers` + the `CountParsimonyInformativeSites` primitive — from gene clusters across N genomes pick **single-copy core genes** (present **exactly once in every genome**, panX; **core** = "at least 99% of samples", Roary; paralog clusters filtered out) that carry **variable positions**, then **rank by descending parsimony-informative-site count** capped at `maxMarkers`; a **parsimony-informative site** (Zvelebil & Baum 2008) = a column with ≥2 states, each in ≥2 sequences → **monomorphic**/**singleton** columns score 0, a single-copy core cluster with **0 PIS** excluded; the input-selection step **upstream of** core-genome tree building (panX→FastTree), makes no tree-accuracy claim (recombination caveat); oracles `AAAAA`/`AAACA`/`AACCG`/`ACCTG`→PIS 2 (cols 3,5), 3-genome selection excludes paralog/not-core/conserved; selects the single-copy subset of [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]], consumes families of [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]], single-copy-ortholog constraint shared with [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]]; one assumption (no in-repo aligner → PIS over equal-length members, unequal→PIS 0); no contradictions; record [[pangen-marker-001-evidence]].
- [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] — the anchor for the **phylogenetics** `PHYLO-*` family (first PHYLO-* unit, PHYLO-BOOT-001): **Felsenstein's bootstrap** (Felsenstein 1985) — attach a **confidence to each clade** of an inferred tree by **resampling alignment columns (sites) with replacement** into same-length pseudo-alignments (taxa kept, characters resampled), rebuilding a tree per replicate (distance matrix → UPGMA/NJ), and scoring each **non-terminal clade of the reference tree** by the **fraction of replicate trees containing a clade with the identical terminal-leaf-name set** (Biopython `get_support`; Lemoine 2018 "proportion of pseudo-trees containing that branch"); binary per-replicate, only reference-tree clades scored, support = `count/replicates`, thresholds 70%/95% descriptive; oracles two-group `AAAAAAAAAA`/`GGGGGGGGGG` UPGMA+JukesCantor seed 42 → support{A,B}={C,D}=1.0, all-identical `ACGTACGT`→all clades 1.0; invariants support∈[0,1] / determinism / keys=non-trivial reference clades / null/<2-seq/replicates<1 throw; the **first general distance-based-phylogenetics concept** in the wiki (no NJ/UPGMA/distance-matrix page yet), **distinct from** the CCF-constraint oncology builder [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] (no distance matrix, no resampling) and a confidence layer over the tree the marker selector [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] feeds; two source-consistent assumptions (rooted-clade scoring vs unrooted bipartitions matching Biopython, proportion [0,1] vs percentage ×100); no contradictions; record [[phylo-boot-001-evidence]].
- [[tree-comparison-metrics]] — the second phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` unit (PHYLO-COMP-001): **tree comparison** — three operations on an already-built rooted binary `PhyloNode` tree. **Robinson–Foulds distance** (`RobinsonFouldsDistance` = symmetric difference `A+B` of the two trees' canonical split/bipartition sets, Robinson & Foulds 1981; raw count, proper metric, **even**, rooted-clade = Wikipedia dummy-leaf-at-root; **max RF = 2(n−2) rooted vs 2(n−3) unrooted**), **MRCA** (`FindMRCA`, deepest common ancestor, O(n) recursive leaf-name match, not-in-tree→null), **patristic distance** (`PatristicDistance` = `dist(x,MRCA)+dist(y,MRCA)` branch-length sum, not-in-tree→NaN, zero-branches→0); invariants RF identity/symmetric/≥0/even, MRCA symmetric/always-ancestor/unique, patristic PD(x,x)=0/symmetric/≥0; scope rooted-binary-only (two §7 decisions); the deterministic **compare** counterpart to the resampling-confidence [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] (agreement vs disagreement of the same split primitive, no resampling), distinct from [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]]; no deviations, no contradictions; record [[phylo-comp-001-evidence]].
- [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] — the third phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` unit (PHYLO-DIST-001): the **pairwise evolutionary-distance** primitive emitting the symmetric *n×n* matrix distance-based tree building (NJ/UPGMA) consumes — `CalculatePairwiseDistance`/`CalculateDistanceMatrix` over four methods **Hamming** (raw diff count) / **p-distance** (`differences/comparableSites`, uncorrected) / **Jukes–Cantor JC69** (`-3/4·ln(1−4p/3)`, equal-base/equal-rate) / **Kimura-2-parameter K2P** (`-1/2·ln((1−2S−V)·√(1−2V))`, S=transition/V=transversion); matrix symmetric / zero-diagonal / non-negative / *n×n*, correction ordering **JC69≥p & K2P≥p**, triangle inequality expected-not-guaranteed; **pairwise deletion** (gaps + ambiguous IUPAC N/R/Y skipped, only A,C,G,T compared), case-insensitive; **saturation** JC69→+∞ at p≥3/4 / K2P→+∞ at V≥1/2, all-gap/empty→0 (`0/n→0`), unequal-length→ArgumentException, null→ArgumentNullException; oracles `ACGTACGT`/`TCGTACGT`→Hamming 1/p 0.125/JC69≈0.137, pure-transition `GCGT` K2P≈0.34657 vs pure-transversion `CCGT`≈0.31713, mixed≈0.30679, gap→7 comparable sites; the **upstream substrate** the family sits on — [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] resamples + re-runs it per replicate, [[tree-comparison-metrics]] compares the trees it feeds; distinct from the column-selecting [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] and the distance-matrix-free [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]]; two API-contract assumptions (empty/all-gap→0, pairwise deletion); no contradictions; record [[phylo-dist-001-evidence]].
- [[tree-statistics]] — a phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` unit (PHYLO-STATS-001): **whole-tree descriptive statistics** read off a single rooted binary `PhyloNode` — `GetLeaves` (terminal nodes, no children; count via `.Count()` = Biopython `count_terminals`), `CalculateTreeLength` (**total tree length = Σ all branch lengths**; undefined/default 0 branch → 0; the minimum-evolution quantity, Rzhetsky & Nei 1992; Biopython `total_branch_length`/DendroPy `Tree.length()`), `GetTreeDepth` (**tree height = edges on the longest root-to-leaf path**, counts edges not nodes; single-node 0; empty tree −1); oracles balanced `((A:1,B:1):1,(C:1,D:1):1)`→4/6/2, caterpillar→4/5/3, single leaf→1/branch-len/0, null root→∅/0/−1; the **descriptive-summary** sibling of the **compare/query** [[tree-comparison-metrics]] (its Σ-all-branches length is the whole-tree analogue of patristic distance's per-path sum), over the same `PhyloNode` [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] resamples and [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] feeds via UPGMA/NJ; one assumption (null `PhyloNode`↔empty-tree convention); no deviations, no contradictions; record [[phylo-stats-001-evidence]].
- [[distance-based-tree-construction]] — the phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` **tree-building core** (PHYLO-TREE-001): the step that **consumes an [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] and emits a `PhyloNode` tree** via two agglomerative methods on `PhylogeneticAnalyzer` (`BuildTree` from sequences / `BuildTreeFromMatrix` from a pre-computed matrix; returns `PhylogeneticTree` Root/Taxa/DistanceMatrix/Method). **UPGMA** (Sokal & Michener 1958) — rooted **ultrametric**, molecular-clock, nearest-pair merge, arithmetic-mean distance update, **height = d/2**, incremental branch lengths, O(n³)/O(n²). **Neighbor-Joining** (Saitou & Nei 1987) — **unrooted** (midpoint-rooted final join preserving patristic distances), clock-free, join the **minimum-Q** pair `Q(i,j)=(n−2)·d(i,j)−Σd(i,k)−Σd(j,k)`, branch lengths `δ(f,u)=d(f,g)/2+(Σd(f,k)−Σd(g,k))/(2(n−2))`, **correct topology for additive matrices**, **negative branches preserved (no clamping)**, O(n³); invariants INV-01..05 (all taxa leaves, binary, n leaves / n−1 internal, UPGMA≥0) + UPGMA ultrametric/rooted/height=d/2 + NJ additive-correct/may-be-negative/no-clock; oracles UPGMA 5S-rRNA →(a,b)@17→((a,b),e)@22→(c,d)@28→final@33 (root 16.5, all tips 16.5), NJ 5-taxon →Q₁(a,b)=−50, δ(a,u)=2…δ(e,w)=1; the **hinge** of the family — downstream of [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]], wrapped per-replicate by [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]], its output compared/queried by [[tree-comparison-metrics]] and summarized by [[tree-statistics]], serialized by Newick ([[phylo-newick-001-evidence]]); distinct from [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] (no distance matrix) and [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] (selects columns, builds no tree); no deviations, no contradictions; record [[phylo-tree-001-evidence]].
- [[bed-format-parsing]] — FileIO file-parsing `PARSE-*` family anchor (first PARSE-* unit, PARSE-BED-001): UCSC **BED** interval parsing keyed on the **0-based half-open** coordinate model (`chromStart` 0-based / `chromEnd` 1-based-exclusive, length `chromEnd−chromStart`, `chromStart==chromEnd` = zero-length insertion; contrast 1-based GFF/GTF/VCF), the **BED3→BED12** column ladder (`chrom`/`chromStart`/`chromEnd` + optional `name`/`score`/`strand`/`thick*`/`itemRgb`/`block*`), and the UCSC validation rules (`chromStart ≤ chromEnd` else null, score clamp [0,1000], strand ∈ +/−/., first-line column-count lock, BED12 first-blockStart-0 / blockCount = array lengths / no-overlap / last-block-reaches-end); the malformed-input target of [[fuzzing]]; deviations None (rules verbatim from UCSC FAQ + Wikipedia); record [[parse-bed-001-evidence]].
- [[phred-quality-encoding]] — the FASTQ quality-score encoding concept (shared by FileIO parsing + Assembly trimming): Phred score `Q=−10·log₁₀(p)` / `p=10^(−Q/10)`, the +10-Q=10×-fewer-errors ladder (Q20/Q30 QC thresholds), the two live ASCII offsets **Phred+33** (Sanger/Illumina 1.8+, ASCII 33–126, Q0–93) vs **Phred+64** (Illumina 1.3–1.7, ASCII 64–126, Q0–62) with boundary chars (`!`=Q0/`I`=Q40/`~`=Q93 vs `@`=Q0/`h`=Q40/`~`=Q62), deterministic per-record offset auto-detection (`<'@'`→+33, high-band→+64, ambiguous `@`–`I`→default +33), and why a mis-detected offset silently corrupts all downstream Q-stats/trim/filter; traced by [[parse-fastq-001-evidence]], reused by [[quality-trimming-running-sum]].
- [[insdc-feature-location]] — the shared INSDC (DDBJ/ENA/GenBank) feature-table **location-descriptor** grammar underlying both GenBank and EMBL flat files (same location string, different line syntax): 1-based-inclusive coordinates (contrast BED 0-based), descriptors `n..m`/single `n`/between-bases `n^m`/`<`/`>` partials/`complement`/`join`/`order`/`complement(join(…))` with the no-nested-join/order rule, remote refs `accession.version:span`; operator assembly semantics (`join`/`order` concatenate in order, `complement` reverse-complements, `complement(join(a,b))==join(complement(b),complement(a))`), offline-first caller-supplied remote resolver, `<`/`>`-verbatim-slice assumption; oracles `join(1..3,7..9)`/`ACGTACGTAC`→`ACGGTA`, `complement(Y.1:1..4)`→`GTTT`; traced jointly by [[parse-genbank-001-evidence]] and [[parse-embl-001-evidence]].
- [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]] — anchor for the **population-genetics** `POP-*` family (**first POP-\* unit**, POP-ANCESTRY-001): estimate an individual's **ancestry proportions Q** (genome fraction from each of K reference populations) from unlinked SNP genotypes via **supervised/projection ADMIXTURE** — reference allele frequencies **F fixed/known**, only Q estimated by EM. Alexander, Novembre & Lange 2009 model: genotype g∈{0,1,2}=allele-1 copy count, **log-likelihood Eq. 2** `L=ΣᵢΣⱼ{g·ln(Σ_k q·f)+(2−g)·ln(Σ_k q·(1−f))}` under simplex `Σ_k q_ik=1`; **FRAPPE EM Eq. 4** `q^{n+1}=(1/2J)Σⱼ[g·a_ijk+(2−g)·b_ijk]` (a/b = posteriors an allele-1/allele-2 copy came from k), EM monotone ascent, convergence Eq. 5 ΔL<ε=10⁻⁴, O(IJK²); oracles symmetric K=2/J=2 f_A=[0.8,0.2]/f_B=[0.2,0.8] g=[2,0] → one EM iter **(0.8,0.2) exactly** → converges (1.0,0.0), single-SNP g=2→(0.9,0.1)/g=1→(0.5,0.5) uninformative-het/g=0→(0.1,0.9), identical panels uniform fixed point; INV simplex Σ_k q=1 & EM L non-decreasing, missing g∉{0,1,2} skipped, empty inputs→empty; **label non-identifiability** (K! maxima under population relabeling) **pinned by fixed labelled reference panels** (ADMIXTURE manual §2.10/§2.14) so Q interpretable relative to supplied labels; scope = estimate-Q-given-fixed-F only (does NOT jointly learn F, run unsupervised block-relaxation, choose K, or model linkage); **distinct from** the tree-building phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` family ([[distance-based-tree-construction]], [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]]) — a mixture-weight/EM decomposition of one admixed individual, not a tree; two research-grade assumptions (maxIterations budget + ε convergence; skip-missing); no contradictions; record [[pop-ancestry-001-evidence]].
- [[genetic-diversity-statistics]] — population-genetics `POP-*` family diversity-statistics unit (**second POP-\* unit**, POP-DIV-001, sibling of the anchor [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]]): four classical within-population variation scalars from an aligned sample (n seqs, length L, S segregating sites) — **nucleotide diversity π** = Σ_{i<j} d_ij/(C(n,2)·L) (Nei & Li 1979, mean per-site pairwise differences), **Watterson's θ_W** = S/a_n with harmonic a_n = Σ_{i=1}^{n−1} 1/i (per-site S/(a_n·L); Watterson 1975), **Tajima's D** = (k̂ − S/a_1)/√(e_1·S+e_2·S(S−1)) (Tajima 1989 — normalized π-vs-Watterson difference; **k̂ = pairwise-difference COUNT not per-site π**; D≈0 neutral, D<0 excess rare alleles→sweep/expansion, D>0 deficit→balancing/contraction), and **heterozygosity/gene diversity** H_exp = (1/L)Σ(1−Σp²) with unbiased haploid H_obs = n/(n−1)·H_exp ≡ π (Nei 1978); Wikipedia oracle n=5/L=20/S=4 → k̂=2.0/π=0.1/S/a_1≈1.92/θ_W≈0.096/**D≈0.273** (TD-C01/TD-C02); guards n<3→D undefined→0, S=0/monomorphic→all 0, Var≤0→D=0, `CalculateTajimasD(k̂,S,n)` expects k̂ not π; **distinct from** the anchor's ancestry-proportion EM (within-population *variation amount* vs *ancestry decomposition*), summary-only (no variant calling / phasing / recombination / Fu-Li / Fay-Wu); all formulae exact-match, no deviations; record [[pop-div-001-evidence]].
- [[allele-genotype-frequencies]] — **foundational** population-genetics `POP-*` primitive (POP-FREQ-001): turn per-locus **genotype counts** into **allele frequencies**, derive **minor allele frequency (MAF)**, and **filter variants by MAF** — the numeric substrate under the rest of the POP family (the fixed reference frequencies **F** of [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]] and the per-site `p_i` behind the heterozygosity term of [[genetic-diversity-statistics]] are exactly these quantities). Biallelic allele freq `p = f(AA)+½f(AB)` / `q = f(BB)+½f(AB)` via counts `total=2·(n_AA+n_AB+n_BB)`, `major=2·n_AA+n_AB`, `minor=2·n_BB+n_AB` (**INV `p+q=1`**, `major+minor=total`; oracle 49/42/9 → 0.70/0.30); VCF/PLINK dosage `alt_freq = Σg/(2n)`, `MAF = min(alt_freq, 1−alt_freq)` (**INV `0 ≤ MAF ≤ 0.5`**, symmetric — alt_freq 0.7 → MAF 0.3; monomorphic → 0; 50/50 → 0.5); MAF filter = inclusive `[minMAF,maxMAF]` band with conventional HapMap/common(>0.05)-vs-rare(<0.05) thresholds; edge cases zero samples→(0,0), empty vector→MAF 0, **negative count → `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`**; scope = biallelic counting/normalization only (no HWE test, no multiallelic, no phasing/imputation); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-freq-001-evidence]].
- [[population-differentiation-fst]] — population-genetics `POP-*` differentiation unit (POP-FST-001): measure **how differentiated populations are** — fraction of total variation due to between-population structure — from per-population allele frequencies (**consumes** [[allele-genotype-frequencies]]; distinct from within-sample [[genetic-diversity-statistics]] and from ancestry decomposition [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]]). **Wright 1965 variance Fst** `Fst = σ_S²/(pBar(1−pBar))`, two-pop size-weighted `pBar=(n1·p1+n2·p2)/(n1+n2)` / `σ_S²=(n1(p1−pBar)²+n2(p2−pBar)²)/(n1+n2)`, multi-locus **ratio-of-sums** `Σσ_S²/Σhet` — the **population parameter from known allele freqs**, explicitly **NOT** the Weir & Cockerham 1984 θ estimator (no bias correction); **F-statistics** heterozygosity partition `Fis=1−Hi/Hs`/`Fit=1−Hi/Ht`/`Fst=1−Hs/Ht` with **exact** `(1−Fit)=(1−Fis)(1−Fst)`; INV Fst∈[0,1] (0=panmixia/1=fixed differences), Fis∈[−1,1] (negative under excess heterozygotes), pairwise matrix symmetric + zero diagonal, **not a metric** (fails triangle inequality); oracles fixed p1=1/p2=0→**1.0 exactly**, pop1=(.9,.8)/pop2=(.1,.2)→1/2, Cavalli-Sforza/Elhaik ref values, Hartl-Clark bands (0.05/0.15/0.25); edge cases denominator 0 (empty/both-fixed-same/monomorphic)→**return 0**; scope = Wright Fst + heterozygosity F-statistics only (no significance test, no bootstrap CI); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-fst-001-evidence]].
- [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]] — population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-HW-001): the **Hardy-Weinberg equilibrium chi-square test** — does a biallelic locus's observed genotype counts match the `p²/2pq/q²` proportions expected under random mating? **Consumes** genotype counts from [[allele-genotype-frequencies]] (POP-FREQ-001, whose scope explicitly leaves the HWE test here) and turns them into a **hypothesis test**. Estimate `p = (2·n_AA + n_Aa)/(2n)` / `q = 1−p`, expected counts `E = {p²n, 2pqn, q²n}`, **Pearson χ² = Σ (O−E)²/E** over the 3 genotype classes, **df = 1** (`#genotypes − #alleles = 3 − 2`), p-value from chi-square CDF (lower-incomplete-gamma approx), default **α = 0.05** critical value **3.841**; returns `InEquilibrium`/`ChiSquare`/`PValue`. Oracles Ford moth (1469,138,5)→`p≈0.954`/`χ²≈0.83`→in-eq, perfect (25,50,25)→`χ²=0`, excess-het (10,80,10)→`χ²=36 ≫ 3.84`→out-of-eq; edge cases **zero samples→InEquilibrium true, PValue 1** (no evidence against H₀), monomorphic→`χ²=0`, **expected-0 term skipped** (div-by-zero guard); deviation causes non-random mating/selection/mutation/migration/drift/**genotyping error**; scope = biallelic chi-square only (no Wigginton 2005 **exact test**, no multiallelic); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-hw-001-evidence]].
- [[linkage-disequilibrium]] — population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-LD-001): **non-random association between alleles at two loci** — a **pairwise inter-locus** quantity distinct from per-locus counting ([[allele-genotype-frequencies]]), within-sample diversity ([[genetic-diversity-statistics]]), between-population differentiation ([[population-differentiation-fst]]), and the single-locus [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]]; **consumes** allele/haplotype frequencies from [[allele-genotype-frequencies]]. `D = p_AB − p_A·p_B` (Robbins 1918), normalized `D' = |D|/D_max` clamped [0,1] (Lewontin 1964, sign-branched `D_max`) and `r² = D²/(p_A·q_A·p_B·q_B)` (Hill & Robertson 1968); implemented **phase-free** via the diploid-frequency result `R_AB=r_AB` (Wright 1933) — `r²` = squared Pearson correlation of 0/1/2 genotype dosage vectors `Cov²/(Var·Var)`, `D` recovered from `Cov_diploid=2D ⇒ D=Cov/2`; `FindHaplotypeBlocks` = simplified adjacent-pair Gabriel 2002 (consecutive `r² ≥ threshold`, default **0.7**, ≥2 variants); INV `0≤r²≤1`/`0≤|D'|≤1`, empty→`r²=0,D'=0`, monomorphic/zero-variance→`r²=0` (guarded div), distance+IDs preserved, blocks Start≤End/≥2/non-overlapping/position-ordered; perfect correlation **and** perfect anti-correlation both →`r²=1`/`D'=1` (sign-blind); scope = two-biallelic-loci r²/D' + adjacent-pair blocks only (no full LD matrix, no phasing/EM, no LD-decay fit, no exact Gabriel CI); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-ld-001-evidence]].
- [[runs-of-homozygosity-inbreeding]] — population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-ROH-001): detect **long uninterrupted homozygous stretches** (**runs of homozygosity**, `FindROH`) in one individual and summarize their burden as the genomic inbreeding coefficient **F_ROH** — a **per-individual segment-detection** problem distinct from per-locus counting ([[allele-genotype-frequencies]]), within-sample diversity ([[genetic-diversity-statistics]]), between-population differentiation ([[population-differentiation-fst]]), two-locus [[linkage-disequilibrium]], and single-locus [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]]. **Window-free consecutive-runs** scan (Marras 2015 / detectRUNS): walk position-sorted 0/1/2 genotypes (1 = heterozygous = "opposite"), grow a run, **terminate** when opposite calls exceed `maxOppRun` (a few tolerated to absorb genotyping error) or an inter-SNP gap exceeds `maxGap` (breaks even an all-homozygous run); retain a stretch only if it passes **both** `minSNP` **and** `minLengthBps` (PLINK `--homozyg-snp 100` **and** `--homozyg-kb 1000`, one alone insufficient). **F_ROH = ΣL_roh / L_auto** (McQuillan 2008 verbatim; `L_auto` = SNP-covered autosome ≈2,674 Mb; r=0.86 vs pedigree; min-length lever ≥0.5/1.5/5 Mb, 1.5 Mb best); oracle ΣL_roh=20 Mb/L_auto=100 Mb → **0.20**, whole-genome → 1.0; INV each run once/Start≤End/SnpCount, one tolerated het keeps one run / het beyond splits, gap>maxGap breaks, below minSNP-or-minLength discarded, unsorted ordered internally, genotype 2 = homozygous, leading hets skipped, F_ROH∈[0,1]; two API-encoding assumptions (0/1/2 encoding; **missing-genotype handling out of scope** — no missing sentinel, non-`1` treated homozygous); scope = consecutive-runs scan + F_ROH only (no PLINK sliding-window scoring, no missing bounding, no LOD/model-based callers, no cohort ROH-island mapping); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-roh-001-evidence]].
- [[selection-scan-ihs-ehh]] — population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-SELECT-001): detect **recent positive selection** from **haplotype structure** — a selective sweep leaves an unusually long, low-diversity haplotype around the selected allele. A **haplotype-length/decay** statistic distinct from per-locus counting ([[allele-genotype-frequencies]]), within-sample diversity ([[genetic-diversity-statistics]]), between-population differentiation ([[population-differentiation-fst]]), single-locus [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]], pairwise [[linkage-disequilibrium]], and autozygosity [[runs-of-homozygosity-inbreeding]]; **consumes** derived/ancestral allele freqs from [[allele-genotype-frequencies]]. Pipeline **EHH→iHH→iHS→scan**: `EHH_c=ΣC(n_h,2)/C(n_c,2)` (Sabeti 2002 / selscan Eq.3, decays 1→0 with distance), `iHH` = trapezoidal area under EHH both directions truncated at **EHH<0.05**, **unstandardized iHS = ln(iHH_A/iHH_D)** (Voight 2006, ancestral numerator), standardized to std-normal in derived-allele-freq bins, `ScanForSelection` = proportion `|iHS|>2` in ~50-SNP windows; **sign convention critical** — Voight (A/D) is the opposite of selscan (D/A), large negative iHS ⇒ long *derived* haplotype, balanced decay ⇒ iHS≈0; oracles rehh F1205400→**−1.978569274**, constructed panel iHH_A=10/iHH_D=40→ln(0.25)=**−1.386294361**; INV EHH∈[0,1] (1 single chromosome / 0 all-distinct), single-element bin→std iHS 0, N−1 SD + 20 default 0.05 bins (overridable) affect magnitude only, throws on monomorphic core / null / empty / inconsistent length / invalid core allele / OOR coreIndex; scope = single-core iHS/EHH scan (no XP-EHH, no Fst-outlier or Tajima's-D scan, no genetic-map interpolation, no >200 kb gap masking); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-select-001-evidence]].
- [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] — PCR primer-design `PRIMER-*` / MolTools family anchor (PRIMER-TM-001): the **self-/hetero-dimer melting temperature (Tm)** of two primers via the Primer3 `ntthal` **thermodynamic alignment** over the SantaLucia & Hicks 2004 unified **DNA nearest-neighbour** model — the **DNA** counterpart of the **RNA** Turner-2004 folding [[rna-base-pairing]] / [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]], distinct by modelling an intermolecular duplex at finite strand concentration. Duplex ΔH°/ΔS° = Σ 10 Watson-Crick NN stacks + duplex-initiation + per-end terminal-A·T-penalty + self-complementary symmetry; **bimolecular Tm** `ΔH°·1000/(ΔS°+R·ln(C_T/x))−273.15` with **symmetry factor x=1 (reverse-complement palindrome) / x=4 (otherwise)**; **[Na⁺] entropy salt correction** `0.368·(N/2)·ln[Na⁺]` (Tm monotone in salt); the dimer DP finds the possibly-**non-contiguous** most-stable structure (internal mismatch/loop, single/multi-base bulge, `tstack2` terminal overhang), reproducing primer3-py 2.3.0 `calc_homodimer`/`calc_heterodimer` to machine precision (GCGCGCGC self x=1 Tm 40.0906 °C, TGCATGCATG/CATGCATGCA x=4 Tm 25.6596 °C, GCGCATGCGC 2×2 loop Tm 43.1572 °C); **no stable dimer** (poly-A) → `structure_found=False` → null/NaN, invalid input (null / <2 bases / non-ACGT) → null/NaN; deviations none remaining after the 2026-06-25 full-ntthal-DP port. Also covers the **intramolecular hairpin self-folding** extension (same engine): stem NN stacks (`NnUnifiedParams`) + **Table 4 hairpin-loop ΔG°37** (loop ΔH°=0, ΔS°=−ΔG°37·1000/310.15) + Jacobson-Stockmayer large-loop, **unimolecular hairpin Tm Eq. 11 with NO concentration term** (Vallone & Benight concentration-independent), bimolecular init & terminal-A·T penalty excluded, **bundled** special tri/tetraloop hairpin bonus tables (16 triloop / 76 tetraloop rows, applied in `calc_hairpin`, key incl. closing pair; oracle tetraloop GGGGCGAAAGCCCC Tm 85.0335 °C) plus the legacy opt-in caller increment (oracle GGGCTTTTGCCC Tm 68.6404 °C, poly-A → null/NaN); Also covers the **per-oligo (single-strand) design Tm** path (Eq. 3 applied to a primer vs its own complement; opt-in NN Tm, legacy Wallace/Marmur-Doty unchanged default) with the **Owczarzy 2004** monovalent-quadratic and **Owczarzy 2008** divalent-Mg²⁺/dNTP 1/Tm salt corrections (Biopython `salt_correction` methods 5–7) and the internal-mismatch/dangling-end tables (`NnInternalMismatch`/`NnDanglingEnd`); records [[primer-tm-001-dimer-evidence]], [[primer-tm-001-hairpin-evidence]], [[primer-tm-001-nn-evidence]], [[primer-tm-001-special-loop-evidence]].
- [[primer3-weighted-penalty-objective]] — PCR primer-design `PRIMER-*` / MolTools family (PRIMER-TM-001, **base** unit): the **Primer3 weighted per-primer penalty / objective function** `p_obj_fn` — the *only* score Primer3 sorts candidate primers by (**lower is better**), a **selection/scoring** algorithm distinct from the thermodynamic sibling [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] (Tm enters only as one input *term*). Weighted sum of **sign-gated one-sided deviations** from each parameter optimum: Tm `temp_gt·(Tm−opt_tm)`/`temp_lt·(opt_tm−Tm)`, GC% (percent 0–100) `gc_content_gt/lt`, size `length_gt/lt`, plus non-thermodynamic `compl_any·self_any + compl_end·self_end + num_ns·#N`; left/right primers identical (`p_args`). Defaults `opt_tm=60`/`opt_size=20`, weights `temp_*=length_*=1` and `gc/self/num_ns=0` (GC optimum undefined in header) ⇒ **default objective collapses to `|Tm−60|+|len−20|`**; sign-gated (term=0 exactly at optimum), weight-zero short-circuit, penalty ≥ 0 with **0 iff all-optimal**; `self_any`/`self_end` are caller-supplied Primer3 `dpal` local-alignment scores (arithmetic exact, value external, vanish under default 0 weights); oracles (60,20)→0.0/(63,20)→3.0/(57,18)→5.0/combined→8.0; record [[primer-tm-001-evidence]].
- [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] — **PROBE** family anchor (PROBE-DESIGN-001): the **TaqMan (5'-nuclease hydrolysis-probe) design rules** — an opt-in extension over the unchanged generic hybridization-probe designer, a distinct MolTools reagent-design algorithm alongside the primer units [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] / [[primer3-weighted-penalty-objective]]. The probe-specific hard constraints (no analogue in primer selection): **no G at the 5' end** (a 5'-G quenches the reporter dye *even after cleavage*, so it cannot be rescued — hard rule; `SelectTaqManStrand` moves the design to the complement/antisense strand when a compliant sense probe is impossible), **more Cs than Gs**, **no run of ≥4 consecutive Gs** (flagged separately from the generic homopolymer cap), **G+C 30–80%**, **length 18–22 nt** (default, `minLength`/`maxLength` parameterised — ABI/PREMIER 18–22 vs IDT/Thermo up to 30), and the **probe Tm ≥ primer Tm + 10 °C** gate (so the probe binds before Taq reaches it) with the primer Tm caller-supplied and the probe Tm via the PRIMER-TM-001-validated salt-adjusted `81.5+16.6·log₁₀[Na⁺]+41·GC−600/N` formula (not a TaqMan-specific nearest-neighbour calc); a `NoGuanineAt5Prime`/`PassesAll`-style checker; oracles CCATCACCCTACATCACC passes-all (primerTm ≤ 39.35), 5'-G/GGGG-run/more-G-than-C/len<18/GC-100% each fail, sense GTTAGGGTTAGGGTTAGG → RC CCTAACCCTAACCCTAAC strand selection; two parameterisation assumptions (18–22 default window, repository salt-adjusted Tm engine), no source contradictions; record [[probe-design-001-evidence]].
- [[probe-offtarget-specificity-scan]] — **PROBE** family (PROBE-VALID-001): the **hybridization-probe off-target specificity scan** — align a candidate probe against a pooled reference with a **gapped Smith–Waterman local alignment** and report every site whose identity clears a threshold. The **specificity-checking sibling** of [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] (composition rules), a genuinely distinct algorithm. Core improvement over the earlier **ungapped Hamming scan**: SW's gap-length maxima + **zero floor** (Smith & Waterman 1981) make it *local* and **indel-aware**, so an off-target reachable only through an insertion/deletion (which frame-shifts every downstream base and hides from a fixed window) is found — the **gapped-vs-ungapped BLAST** improvement (Altschul 1990→1997), realized as an *exact* full SW scan (not seed-and-extend). Zero-floor traceback **trims a mismatched tail** so identity is over the matched core. Off-target call at **≥0.75 identity** (Kane et al. 2000 microarray cross-hyb threshold; `minIdentity` caller-configurable). On/off labelling (assumption): the first perfect ungapped full-coverage exact match = intended on-target, all else off-target. Opt-in **Karlin–Altschul** significance (`ComputeLambdaNucleotide`/`ComputeKarlinAltschul`): `E=K·m·n·e^(−λS)`, λ = root of `Σ p_i p_j e^(λ s_ij)=1`, bit `S'=(λS−ln K)/ln 2`, `E=m·n·2^(−S')`, preconditions expected-score<0 + a positive score, K caller-supplied; +1/−3 uniform-0.25 → λ=1.3740631 (≈ blastn 1.37), example bit 59.9627 / E 1.7802e−14. Oracles: exact + indel `ACGTAC-GTACGT` 12/12=1.0 (gapped finds, ungapped misses), indel+mismatch trimmed to 10/12=0.8333 (in @0.75, out @0.90); BLAST DNA scoring +2/−3 gap −2. No source contradictions; record [[probe-valid-001-evidence]].

- [[research-grade-limitations]] — beta, not for clinical use; simplified-subset implementations; internal-only validation.
